### [1] [ESICA: A Scalable Framework for Text-Guided 3D Medical Image Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24876)
*Yu Xin,Gorkem Can Ates,Jun Ma,Sumin Kim,Ying Zhang,Kaleb E Smith,Kuang Gong,Wei Shao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ESICA是一种轻量级、可扩展的文本引导3D医学图像分割框架，通过相似性矩阵掩码预测、高效分解解码器和两遍优化策略，在CVPR BiomedSegFM基准上达到SOTA性能，且其精简版ESICA4 Lite以更少参数实现相近精度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有文本引导医学图像分割框架存在计算开销大、文本与体素特征对齐弱、难以捕捉精细解剖结构细节等缺陷，亟需一种高效、可扩展且适合临床部署的解决方案。

Method: (1) 基于相似性矩阵的掩码预测公式增强语义对齐；(2) 高效分解解码器搭配适配器模块实现精确体积解码；(3) 两遍优化策略锐化边界并解决不确定区域；(4) 两阶段训练方案：仅正样本预训练+平衡微调。

Result: 在覆盖CT、MRI、PET、超声和显微镜五种模态的CVPR BiomedSegFM基准上，ESICA取得了最优分割精度；紧凑版ESICA4 Lite以显著更少的参数达到相近性能，实现了优越的效率-精度权衡。

Conclusion: ESICA推动文本引导分割向高效、可扩展且临床可部署的系统迈进，代码已开源。

Original Abstract: Text guided 3D medical image segmentation offers a flexible alternative to class based and spatial prompt based models by allowing users to specify regions of interest directly in natural language. This paradigm avoids reliance on predefined label sets, reduces ambiguous outputs, and aligns more naturally with clinical workflows. However, existing text guided frameworks are often computationally expensive, exhibit weak text volume feature alignment, and fail to capture fine anatomical details. We propose ESICA, a lightweight and scalable framework that addresses these challenges through three innovations: (1) a similarity matrix based mask prediction formulation that enhances semantic alignment, (2) an efficient decomposed decoder with adapter modules for accurate volumetric decoding, and (3) a two pass refinement strategy that sharpens boundaries and resolves uncertain regions. To improve training stability and generalization, ESICA adopts a two stage scheme consisting of positive only pretraining followed by balanced fine tuning. On the CVPR BiomedSegFM benchmark spanning five imaging modalities (CT, MRI, PET, ultrasound, and microscopy), ESICA achieves state of the art segmentation accuracy, while the compact ESICA4 Lite variant attains similar segmentation performance with substantially fewer parameters, yielding a superior efficiency accuracy trade off. Our framework advances text guided segmentation toward efficient, scalable, and clinically deployable systems. Code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/mirthAI/ESICA.

中文摘要翻译: 文本引导的三维医学图像分割通过允许用户直接使用自然语言指定感兴趣区域，为基于类别和空间提示的模型提供了一种灵活的替代方案。该范式避免了对预定义标签集的依赖，减少了模糊输出，并更自然地契合临床工作流程。然而，现有文本引导框架通常计算开销大、文本与体素特征对齐弱，且难以捕捉精细的解剖结构细节。我们提出ESICA，一个轻量级且可扩展的框架，通过三项创新解决上述挑战：(1) 基于相似性矩阵的掩码预测公式，增强语义对齐；(2) 配备适配器模块的高效分解解码器，实现精确的体积解码；(3) 两遍优化策略，锐化边界并解决不确定区域。为提升训练稳定性和泛化能力，ESICA采用两阶段方案：仅正样本预训练，随后进行平衡微调。在覆盖五种成像模态（CT、MRI、PET、超声和显微镜）的CVPR BiomedSegFM基准上，ESICA取得了最先进的分割精度，同时紧凑版本ESICA4 Lite以显著更少的参数实现了相近的分割性能，展现出优越的效率-精度权衡。我们的框架推动文本引导分割向高效、可扩展且临床可部署的系统迈进。代码将公开发布于 https://github.com/mirthAI/ESICA。

</details>


### [2] [Learning Illumination Control in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24877)
*Nishit Anand,Manan Suri,Christopher Metzler,Dinesh Manocha,Ramani Duraiswami*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个完全开源可复现的扩散模型照明控制流水线，通过构建数据引擎生成训练三元组（欠照明图像、自然语言照明指令、良好照明图像），微调扩散模型，在感知相似性、结构相似性和身份保持上显著优于基线模型。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有闭源模型在照明控制上表现出色，但开源替代方案要么需要深度图等繁重的控制输入，要么不公开代码和数据，缺乏可复现的开源解决方案。

Method: 构建数据引擎将良好照明图像转换为监督训练三元组（欠照明输入图像、自然语言照明指令、良照明输出图像），并在此数据上微调扩散模型。

Result: 在感知相似性、结构相似性和身份保持方面显著优于SD 1.5、SDXL和FLUX.1-dev基线模型。

Conclusion: 提供了一套完全基于开源工具和公开数据构建的可复现解决方案，并公开了所有代码、数据和模型权重。

Original Abstract: Controlling illumination in images is essential for photography and visual content creation. While closed-source models have demonstrated impressive illumination control, open-source alternatives either require heavy control inputs like depth maps or do not release their data and code. We present a fully open-source and reproducible pipeline for learning illumination control in diffusion models. Our approach builds a data engine that transforms well-lit images into supervised training triplets consisting of a poorly-illuminated input image, a natural language lighting instruction, and a well-illuminated output image. We finetune a diffusion model on this data and demonstrate significant improvements over baseline SD 1.5, SDXL, and FLUX.1-dev models in perceptual similarity, structural similarity, and identity preservation. Our work provides a reproducible solution built entirely with open-source tools and publicly available data. We release all our code, data, and model weights publicly.

中文摘要翻译: 控制图像中的照明对于摄影和视觉内容创作至关重要。虽然闭源模型在照明控制上表现出令人印象深刻的能力，但开源替代方案要么需要深度图等繁重的控制输入，要么不公开其数据和代码。我们提出了一个完全开源且可复现的流水线，用于在扩散模型中学习照明控制。我们的方法构建了一个数据引擎，将良好照明的图像转换为监督训练三元组，包括欠照明的输入图像、自然语言照明指令和良好照明的输出图像。我们在此数据上微调扩散模型，并在感知相似性、结构相似性和身份保持方面显著优于基线SD 1.5、SDXL和FLUX.1-dev模型。我们的工作提供了一个完全基于开源工具和公开数据构建的可复现解决方案。我们公开了所有代码、数据和模型权重。

</details>


### [3] [VibeToken: Scaling 1D Image Tokenizers and Autoregressive Models for Dynamic Resolution Generations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24885)
*Maitreya Patel,Jingtao Li,Weiming Zhuang,Yezhou Yang,Lingjuan Lv*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VibeToken，一种分辨率无关的1D Transformer图像分词器，以及基于它的自回归生成模型VibeToken-Gen，能以极少token和恒定计算量生成任意分辨率的高质量图像，显著缩小与扩散模型的差距。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有自回归图像生成模型受限于固定分辨率，推理计算量随分辨率二次增长，且与扩散模型在生成质量上仍有差距。作者希望提出一种高效、分辨率无关的自回归方案，降低计算成本并支持任意分辨率，推动AR视觉生成模型在生产场景中的广泛采用。

Method: 提出VibeToken，一种分辨率无关的1D Transformer图像分词器，将图像编码为32-256个动态可控token序列。在此基础上构建VibeToken-Gen，一个类条件自回归生成器，原生支持任意分辨率生成，计算量恒定不随分辨率变化。

Result: VibeToken-Gen仅用64个token即可生成1024×1024图像，gFID为3.94；而扩散SOTA需要1024个token，gFID为5.87。推理FLOPs恒定为179G，与分辨率无关；相比之下，LlamaGen在1024×1024下需11T FLOPs，VibeToken-Gen效率提升63.4倍。

Conclusion: VibeToken实现了高效且分辨率无关的自回归图像生成，在计算效率上大幅超越现有AR模型，生成质量接近扩散模型，有望推动AR生成模型在工业界的实际部署。

Original Abstract: We introduce an efficient, resolution-agnostic autoregressive (AR) image synthesis approach that generalizes to arbitrary resolutions and aspect ratios, narrowing the gap to diffusion models at scale. At its core is VibeToken, a novel resolution-agnostic 1D Transformer-based image tokenizer that encodes images into a dynamic, user-controllable sequence of 32-256 tokens, achieving a state-of-the-art efficiency and performance trade-off. Building on VibeToken, we present VibeToken-Gen, a class-conditioned AR generator with out-of-the-box support for arbitrary resolutions while requiring significantly fewer compute resources. Notably, VibeToken-Gen synthesizes 1024x1024 images using only 64 tokens and achieves 3.94 gFID; by comparison, a diffusion-based state-of-the-art alternative requires 1,024 tokens and attains 5.87 gFID. In contrast to fixed-resolution AR models such as LlamaGen -- whose inference FLOPs grow quadratically with resolution (11T FLOPs at 1024x1024) -- VibeToken-Gen maintains a constant 179G FLOPs (63.4x efficient) independent of resolution. We hope VibeToken can help unlock the wide adoption of AR visual generative models in production use cases.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了一种高效、分辨率无关的自回归（AR）图像合成方法，该方法可泛化到任意分辨率和宽高比，在大规模下缩小了与扩散模型的差距。其核心是VibeToken，一种新颖的、基于1D Transformer的分辨率无关图像分词器，将图像编码为动态、用户可控的32-256个token序列，实现了最优的效率与性能权衡。基于VibeToken，我们提出了VibeToken-Gen，一个类条件自回归生成器，天然支持任意分辨率，同时所需计算资源显著更少。值得注意的是，VibeToken-Gen仅用64个token即可合成1024×1024图像，gFID为3.94；相比之下，基于扩散的最优替代方案需要1024个token，gFID为5.87。与LlamaGen等固定分辨率AR模型（其推理FLOPs随分辨率二次增长，1024×1024下为11T FLOPs）相比，VibeToken-Gen保持179G FLOPs恒定（效率提升63.4倍），与分辨率无关。我们希望VibeToken能帮助推动AR视觉生成模型在生产用例中的广泛采用。

</details>


### [4] [Interactive Episodic Memory with User Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24893)
*Nikesh Subedi,Loris Bazzani,Ziad Al-Halah*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出**情景记忆问答与反馈任务（EM-QnF）**，允许用户对模型初始预测提供反馈以交互式修正结果。同时提出轻量级训练方案和即插即用的**反馈对齐模块（FALM）**，使现有EM-NLQ模型能有效融合用户反馈，在三个基准上超越SOTA，且与商业大模型相比更具效率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有情景记忆自然语言查询（EM-NLQ）方法将查询视为一次性任务，忽略了用户查询可能存在歧义或不完整的问题，导致模型在真实场景中适用性受限。本文旨在填补这一空白，引入交互式反馈机制来提升预测准确性。

Method: 1）构建基于反馈交互的数据集；2）提出轻量级训练方案，避免昂贵的序列优化；3）设计即插即用的**反馈对齐模块（FALM）**，使现有EM-NLQ模型能够有效融入用户反馈信息。

Result: 在三个具有挑战性的基准上显著超越现有最优方法；与商业大语言-视觉模型相比性能更优或相当，同时保持计算效率；基于人类生成反馈的评估表明该方法能很好地泛化到真实场景。

Conclusion: 通过引入用户反馈交互机制，本文有效解决了EM-NLQ任务中查询歧义性问题，提出的FALM模块即插即用、轻量高效，显著提升了情景记忆检索的准确性和实际可用性。

Original Abstract: In episodic memory with natural language queries (EM-NLQ), a user may ask a question (e.g., "Where did I place the mug?") that requires searching a long egocentric video, captured from the user's perspective, to find the moment that answers it. However, queries can be ambiguous or incomplete, leading to incorrect responses. Current methods ignore this key aspect and address EM-NLQ in a one-shot setup, limiting their applicability in real-world scenarios. In this work, we address this gap and introduce the Episodic Memory with Questions and Feedback task (EM-QnF). Here, the user can provide feedback on the model's initial prediction or add more information (e.g., "Before this. I'm looking for the big blue mug not the white one"), helping the model refine its predictions interactively. To this end, we collect datasets for feedback-based interaction and propose a lightweight training scheme that avoids expensive sequential optimization. We also introduce a plug-and-play Feedback ALignment Module (FALM) that enables existing EM-NLQ models to incorporate user feedback effectively. Our approach significantly improves over the state of the art on three challenging benchmarks and is better than or competitive with commercial large vision-language models while remaining efficient. Evaluation with human-generated feedback shows that it generalizes well to real-world scenarios.

中文摘要翻译: 在基于自然语言查询的情景记忆（EM-NLQ）任务中，用户可能会提出一个问题（例如“我把杯子放在哪里了？”），需要从用户视角拍摄的长时间自我中心视频中搜索出回答该问题的时刻。然而，查询可能具有歧义或不完整，导致模型给出错误回答。现有方法忽略了这一关键问题，采用一次性设定来处理EM-NLQ，限制了其在真实场景中的适用性。本文填补了这一空白，提出了**情景记忆问答与反馈任务（EM-QnF）**。在该任务中，用户可以对模型的初始预测提供反馈，或补充更多信息（例如“在这之前。我找的是那个大的蓝色杯子，不是白色的。”），从而帮助模型交互式地优化其预测。为此，我们收集了基于反馈交互的数据集，并提出了一种轻量级训练方案，避免了昂贵的序列优化。我们还引入了一个即插即用的**反馈对齐模块（FALM）**，使现有的EM-NLQ模型能够有效地融合用户反馈。我们的方法在三个具有挑战性的基准上显著超越了现有最优方法，并且在与商业大语言-视觉模型对比中表现更优或相当，同时保持高效性。基于人类生成反馈的评估表明，该方法在真实场景中具有良好的泛化能力。

</details>


### [5] [Subjective Portrait Region Cropping in Landscape Videos with Temporal Annotation Smoothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24947)
*Cheng-Han Lee,Maniratnam Mandal,Neil Birkbeck,Yilin Wang,Balu Adsumilli,Alan C. Bovik*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了LIVE-YT VC和LIVE-YT VC++两个大规模视频裁剪主观标注数据集，并利用视频定位模型进行宽高比自适应变换，以解决移动端视频在不同分辨率和方向模式下的内容保留问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 移动端视频消费日益增长，但不同手持设备的显示分辨率和方向模式各异，导致视频宽高比变换时出现视觉质量下降（如静态裁剪、边框填充）或内容扭曲问题。现有方法缺乏大规模主观标注数据集来指导视频裁剪任务。

Method: 1) 构建LIVE-YT VC数据库：包含1800个视频，由90名受试者进行主观标注，是最大的公开视频人像区域裁剪数据集。2) 提出LIVE-YT VC++版本：引入新颖的帧内时序滤波器对主观标注进行平滑处理。3) 使用SmartVidCrop算法和先进的视频定位模型进行宽高比变换任务，并在数据集上微调这些模型。

Result: 建立了目前最大的公开视频人像区域裁剪主观数据集；验证了标签与视频显著性预测之间的相似性；重新利用视频定位模型进行宽高比变换并在数据集上微调取得了良好效果。

Conclusion: 该数据集和算法为视频宽高比自适应变换提供了基准资源，有助于在移动端视频重塑过程中保留视频质量和原始含义，研究代码将开源。

Original Abstract: With the rise of mobile video consumption on diverse handheld display resolutions and orientation modes, altering videos to aspect ratios poses challenges. Static cropping and border padding often compromises visual quality, while warping may distort a video's intended meaning. Here we advocate for a more effective approach: cropping significant regions within video frames in a temporal manner, while minimizing distortion and preserving essential content. One barrier to solving this problem is the lack of sufficiently large-scale database devoted to informing these tasks. Towards filling this gap, we introduce the LIVE-YouTube Video Cropping (LIVE-YT VC) database, featuring 1800 videos, annotated by 90 human subjects. Using videos sourced from the YouTube-UGC and LSVQ Databases, this new resource is the largest publicly-available subjective video portrait region cropping database. We also introduce a post-processed version of the database, called LIVE-YT VC++, whereby a novel intra-frame temporal filter was deployed to smooth subjective annotations within each video. We demonstrate the usefulness of this new data resource using the SmartVidCrop algorithm and state-of-the-art video grounding models, in hopes of establishing our subjective dataset as a benchmark for future research. Our contributions offer a resource for advancing video aspect ratio transformation models towards ensuring that reshaped mobile-friendly video content retains its quality and meaning. Since our labels bear resemblances to video saliency annotations, we also conducted an additional analysis to explore the similarity between our labels and video saliency predictions. Finally, we repurposed state-of-the-art video grounding models for aspect ratio change tasks, and fine-tuned them on our dataset. As a service to the research community, we plan to open source the project.

中文摘要翻译: 随着移动视频消费在各种手持设备的不同显示分辨率和方向模式上的兴起，将视频调整为其他宽高比面临着挑战。静态裁剪和边框填充通常会损害视觉质量，而图像扭曲则可能扭曲视频的预期含义。在此，我们倡导一种更有效的方法：以时序方式裁剪视频帧中的显著区域，同时最小化失真并保留关键内容。解决该问题的一个障碍是缺乏足够大规模的数据集来指导这些任务。为填补这一空白，我们引入了LIVE-YouTube视频裁剪（LIVE-YT VC）数据库，包含1800个视频，由90名受试者标注。该新资源使用来自YouTube-UGC和LSVQ数据库的视频，是最大的公开可用主观视频人像区域裁剪数据库。我们还引入了该数据库的后处理版本LIVE-YT VC++，其中部署了一种新颖的帧内时序滤波器来平滑每个视频中的主观标注。我们通过SmartVidCrop算法和先进的视频定位模型展示了该新数据资源的实用性，以期将我们的主观数据集建立为未来研究的基准。我们的贡献为推进视频宽高比变换模型提供了资源，确保重塑后的移动端友好视频内容保留其质量和含义。由于我们的标注与视频显著性标注具有相似性，我们还进行了额外分析，以探索我们标注与视频显著性预测之间的相似性。最后，我们将先进的视频定位模型重新用于宽高比变换任务，并在我们的数据集上对其进行了微调。作为对研究社区的服务，我们计划开源该项目。

</details>


### [6] [Learning from Noisy Preferences: A Semi-Supervised Learning Approach to Direct Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24952)
*Xinxin Liu,Ming Li,Zonglin Lyu,Yuzhang Shang,Chen Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Semi-DPO，一种半监督方法，通过将多维度人类偏好压缩为二值标签导致的梯度冲突问题视为噪声标签问题，利用一致性过滤的干净子集训练初始模型，再为冲突对生成伪标签进行迭代优化，从而在无需额外人工标注或奖励模型的情况下提升扩散模型与复杂人类偏好的对齐效果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有偏好数据集仅提供单一的、整体性的标注（获胜/失败），但人类视觉偏好本质上是多维的（美学、细节保真度、语义对齐等）。将多维偏好压缩为二值标签会产生严重的标签噪声，这些噪声在扩散直接偏好优化（DPO）中生成冲突的梯度信号，误导模型训练。

Method: 提出Semi-DPO半监督方法：1) 将偏好对分类为一致对（干净有标签数据）和冲突对（噪声无标签数据）；2) 在共识过滤后的干净子集上训练初始模型；3) 将该模型作为隐式分类器为噪声集生成伪标签；4) 迭代优化模型。

Result: 实验结果表明Semi-DPO达到了最先进的性能，显著提升了模型与复杂人类偏好的对齐效果，且无需额外人工标注或显式奖励模型。

Conclusion: 通过半监督方式处理偏好标注中的噪声，可以有效缓解多维偏好压缩为二值标签带来的梯度冲突问题，提升扩散模型的偏好对齐能力。

Original Abstract: Human visual preferences are inherently multi-dimensional, encompassing aesthetics, detail fidelity, and semantic alignment. However, existing datasets provide only single, holistic annotations, resulting in severe label noise: images that excel in some dimensions but are deficient in others are simply marked as winner or loser. We theoretically demonstrate that compressing multi-dimensional preferences into binary labels generates conflicting gradient signals that misguide Diffusion Direct Preference Optimization (DPO). To address this, we propose Semi-DPO, a semi-supervised approach that treats consistent pairs as clean labeled data and conflicting ones as noisy unlabeled data. Our method starts by training on a consensus-filtered clean subset, then uses this model as an implicit classifier to generate pseudo-labels for the noisy set for iterative refinement. Experimental results demonstrate that Semi-DPO achieves state-of-the-art performance and significantly improves alignment with complex human preferences, without requiring additional human annotation or explicit reward models during training. We will release our code and models at: https://github.com/L-CodingSpace/semi-dpo

中文摘要翻译: 人类视觉偏好本质上是多维的，涵盖美学、细节保真度和语义对齐等方面。然而，现有数据集仅提供单一的、整体性的标注，导致严重的标签噪声：在某些维度上表现出色但在其他维度上存在缺陷的图像被简单地标记为获胜者或失败者。我们从理论上证明，将多维偏好压缩为二值标签会产生冲突的梯度信号，误导扩散直接偏好优化（DPO）。为解决这一问题，我们提出Semi-DPO，一种半监督方法，将一致对视为干净的有标签数据，将冲突对视为带噪声的无标签数据。我们的方法首先在共识过滤后的干净子集上训练，然后将该模型作为隐式分类器，为噪声集生成伪标签以进行迭代优化。实验结果表明，Semi-DPO达到了最先进的性能，并且显著提升了与复杂人类偏好的对齐效果，而在训练过程中无需额外的人工标注或显式奖励模型。我们将在以下地址开源代码和模型：https://github.com/L-CodingSpace/semi-dpo

</details>


### [7] [Rapid tracking through strongly scattering media with physics-informed neuromorphic speckle analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25310)
*Yuqing Cao,Shuo Zhu,Rongzhou Chen,Jingyan Chen,Ni Chen,Edmund Y. Lam*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出计算神经形态跟踪（CNT）框架，结合异步事件传感与任务驱动散斑分析，实现低光强散射介质中快速运动物体的鲁棒跟踪，速度提升10倍、照度降低10倍。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于帧相机的固定曝光方法在信噪比和时间分辨率之间存在权衡，难以在低光照强散射条件下跟踪快速运动物体。

Method: 提出计算神经形态跟踪（CNT）框架，将神经形态散斑聚合建模为时空散斑表示，联合优化时间和空间参数以最大化极端条件下的跟踪稳定性。

Result: 实验表明，相比传统系统，该方法可跟踪快10倍的运动，并在暗10倍的照明条件下实现鲁棒运动跟踪。

Conclusion: 该方法显著拓宽了通过散射介质进行跟踪的工作范围，为快速运动和低光照条件下的苛刻场景提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Original Abstract: This work addresses the critical problem of tracking fast-moving objects through strongly scattering media in a low-light environment. Different from existing approaches that use frame-based cameras with fixed exposure times, which trade off signal-to-noise ratio for temporal resolution, we introduce computational neuromorphic tracking (CNT), a physics-informed framework that combines asynchronous event sensing with task-driven speckle analysis for robust motion estimation. We formulate the neuromorphic speckle aggregation as a spatiotemporal speckle representation, jointly optimizing the temporal and spatial parameters to maximize tracking stability under extreme conditions. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method enables robust motion tracking of 10x faster motion and under 10x dimmer illumination compared to conventional systems. These improvements significantly broaden the operational regime for tracking through scattering media, providing an efficient and scalable solution for demanding scenarios involving rapid motion and low-light conditions.

中文摘要翻译: 本工作解决了在低光照环境下通过强散射介质跟踪快速移动物体的关键问题。与现有使用固定曝光时间的帧相机方法（在信噪比和时间分辨率之间进行权衡）不同，我们引入了计算神经形态跟踪（CNT），这是一个物理信息驱动的框架，将异步事件传感与任务驱动的散斑分析相结合，以实现鲁棒的运动估计。我们将神经形态散斑聚合法建模为时空散斑表示，联合优化时间和空间参数以最大化极端条件下的跟踪稳定性。大量实验证明，与传统系统相比，我们的方法能够在暗10倍的照明条件下实现快10倍的运动鲁棒跟踪。这些改进显著拓宽了通过散射介质进行跟踪的工作范围，为涉及快速运动和低光照条件的苛刻场景提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

### [8] [ViPO: Visual Preference Optimization at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24953)
*Ming Li,Jie Wu,Justin Cui,Xiaojie Li,Rui Wang,Chen Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了Poly-DPO算法（通过多项式项增强DPO目标函数对噪声的鲁棒性）并构建了大规模高质量偏好数据集ViPO（含100万图像对和30万视频对），实验表明高质量数据下标准DPO已足够，而Poly-DPO在噪声数据上表现优异，证明算法适应性与数据质量对扩展视觉偏好优化同等重要。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前开源偏好数据集中存在冲突的偏好模式（同一对图像在不同维度上各有优劣），导致噪声数据阻碍偏好优化范式的有效扩展。现有数据集还存在低分辨率、提示多样性有限、分布不平衡等问题，亟需从算法鲁棒性和数据质量两方面解决视觉偏好优化的扩展瓶颈。

Method: 提出Poly-DPO，在标准DPO目标函数中引入额外的多项式项，该多项式项可根据数据集特征动态调整模型置信度，从而在不同数据分布下实现有效学习。同时构建ViPO大规模偏好数据集：包含100万1024px图像对（5个类别）和30万720p+视频对（3个类别），利用SOTA生成模型和多样化提示确保可靠偏好信号和平衡分布。

Result: 在噪声数据集Pick-a-Pic V2上，Poly-DPO在GenEval指标上比Diffusion-DPO提升6.87（SD1.5）和2.32（SDXL）；在ViPO数据集上，模型性能远超现有开源偏好数据集训练的结果；且高质量数据集上Poly-DPO的最优配置收敛到标准DPO，验证了数据质量的重要性。

Conclusion: 同时解决算法适应性和数据质量是扩展视觉偏好优化的关键：当数据质量足够高时，复杂的优化策略变得不必要；但在不完美数据集上，Poly-DPO等自适应算法仍然具有重要价值。ViPO数据集和Poly-DPO算法共同为大规模视觉偏好优化提供了有效方案。

Original Abstract: While preference optimization is crucial for improving visual generative models, how to effectively scale this paradigm remains largely unexplored. Current open-source preference datasets contain conflicting preference patterns, where winners excel in some dimensions but underperform in others. Naively optimizing on such noisy datasets fails to learn preferences, hindering effective scaling. To enhance robustness against noise, we propose Poly-DPO, which extends the DPO objective with an additional polynomial term that dynamically adjusts model confidence based on dataset characteristics, enabling effective learning across diverse data distributions. Beyond biased patterns, existing datasets suffer from low resolution, limited prompt diversity, and imbalanced distributions. To facilitate large-scale visual preference optimization by tackling data bottlenecks, we construct ViPO, a massive-scale preference dataset with 1M image pairs at 1024px across five categories and 300K video pairs at 720p+ across three categories. State-of-the-art generative models and diverse prompts ensure reliable preference signals with balanced distributions. Remarkably, when applying Poly-DPO to our high-quality dataset, the optimal configuration converges to standard DPO. This convergence validates dataset quality and Poly-DPO's adaptive nature: sophisticated optimization becomes unnecessary with sufficient data quality, yet remains valuable for imperfect datasets. We validate our approach across visual generation models. On noisy datasets like Pick-a-Pic V2, Poly-DPO achieves 6.87 and 2.32 gains over Diffusion-DPO on GenEval for SD1.5 and SDXL, respectively. For ViPO, models achieve performance far exceeding those trained on existing open-source preference datasets. These results confirm that addressing both algorithmic adaptability and data quality is essential for scaling visual preference optimization.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管偏好优化对于提升视觉生成模型至关重要，但如何有效扩展这一范式仍鲜有探索。当前的开源偏好数据集存在冲突的偏好模式——优胜者在某些维度表现优异但在其他维度却表现不佳。在这种含噪数据集上直接进行朴素优化无法有效学习偏好，阻碍了有效的扩展。为增强对噪声的鲁棒性，我们提出Poly-DPO，该方法在DPO目标函数中引入了一个额外的多项式项，该多项式项根据数据集特征动态调整模型置信度，从而能够在多样化的数据分布下实现有效学习。除有偏模式外，现有数据集还面临低分辨率、提示多样性有限和分布不平衡等问题。为通过攻克数据瓶颈来促进大规模视觉偏好优化，我们构建了ViPO——一个大规模偏好数据集，包含100万对1024px分辨率的图像对（覆盖五个类别）和30万对720p+分辨率的视频对（覆盖三个类别）。最先进的生成模型和多样化提示确保了可靠的偏好信号和平衡的数据分布。值得注意的是，当将Poly-DPO应用于我们的高质量数据集时，最优配置收敛到标准DPO。这一收敛验证了数据集质量和Poly-DPO的自适应特性：在数据质量足够高时，复杂的优化变得不再必要，但对于不完美的数据集仍然具有重要价值。我们在视觉生成模型上验证了我们的方法。在Pick-a-Pic V2等噪声数据集上，Poly-DPO在GenEval指标上分别比Diffusion-DPO在SD1.5和SDXL上取得了6.87和2.32的提升。对于ViPO，模型性能远超在现有开源偏好数据集上训练的结果。这些结果确认了同时解决算法适应性和数据质量对于扩展视觉偏好优化至关重要。

</details>


### [9] [Exploring Remote Photoplethysmography for Neonatal Pain Detection from Facial Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25680)
*Ashutosh Dhamaniya,Anup Kumar Gupta,Trishna Saikia,Puneet Gupta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于远程光电容积描记术（rPPG）的非接触式新生儿疼痛检测方法，通过引入质量参数和信噪比参数优化信号提取，结合音频特征实现多模态融合，实验表明蓝色通道rPPG信号最有效，多模态融合优于单模态。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 新生儿未缓解的疼痛会导致发育迟缓和体重增长减缓等不良影响，而传统接触式生理参数监测方法不适用于长期监护且存在疾病传播风险（如COVID-19），因此需要一种更客观、可靠且非接触的疼痛评估方法。

Method: 1) 采用远程光电容积描记术（rPPG）以非接触方式估计脉搏信号；2) 引入质量参数选择受皮肤形变影响最小的感兴趣区域（ROI）的时间信号；3) 采用信噪比（SNR）作为适应度参数，提取受噪声影响最小的rPPG信号片段；4) 将rPPG特征与音频特征进行多模态融合用于疼痛检测。

Result: 1) rPPG信号为新生儿疼痛检测提供了有效信息；2) 蓝色颜色通道提取的信号优于其他颜色通道；3) 将rPPG与音频特征结合的多模态方法优于单一模态方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于rPPG的非接触式方法能够有效用于新生儿疼痛检测，其中蓝色通道信号最优，且多模态（rPPG+音频）融合策略可进一步提升检测性能。

Original Abstract: Unaddressed pain in neonates can lead to adverse effects, including delayed development and slower weight gain, emphasising the need for more objective and reliable pain assessment methods. Hence, automated methods using behavioural and physiological pain indicators have been developed to aid healthcare professionals in the Neonatal ICU. Traditional contact-based methods for physiological parameter estimation are unsuitable for long-term monitoring and increase the risk of spreading diseases like COVID-19. We introduce a novel approach using remote photoplethysmography (rPPG) to estimate pulse signals in a non-contact manner and employ them for neonatal pain detection. The temporal signals acquired from regions-of-interest (ROIs) affected by skin deformations may exhibit lower quality and provide erroneous rPPG signals. Therefore, we incorporated a quality parameter to select the temporal signals obtained from ROIs that are least affected by skin deformations. Further, we employed signal-to-noise ratio as a fitness parameter to extract the rPPG signal corresponding to the clip that is least affected by noise. Experimental findings demonstrate that the rPPG signals provide useful information for neonatal pain detection, and signals extracted from the blue colour channel outperform those extracted from other colour channels. We also show that combining rPPG and audio features provides better results than individual modalities.

中文摘要翻译: 新生儿未得到缓解的疼痛会导致不良后果，包括发育迟缓和体重增长减缓，这凸显了对更客观、可靠的疼痛评估方法的需求。为此，研究人员开发了基于行为和生理疼痛指标的自动化方法，以辅助新生儿重症监护病房（NICU）的医护人员。传统的接触式生理参数估计方法不适用于长期监测，并且会增加COVID-19等疾病的传播风险。本文提出了一种新颖的方法，利用远程光电容积描记术（rPPG）以非接触方式估计脉搏信号，并将其应用于新生儿疼痛检测。从受皮肤形变影响的感兴趣区域（ROI）获取的时间信号可能质量较低，并提供错误的rPPG信号。因此，我们引入了一个质量参数来选择受皮肤形变影响最小的ROI所对应的时间信号。此外，我们采用信噪比（SNR）作为适应度参数，提取受噪声影响最小的片段对应的rPPG信号。实验结果表明，rPPG信号为新生儿疼痛检测提供了有用信息，并且从蓝色颜色通道提取的信号优于从其他颜色通道提取的信号。我们还证明，将rPPG与音频特征相结合比单一模态能获得更好的检测结果。

### [10] [Beyond Accuracy: Benchmarking Cross-Task Consistency in Unified Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25072)
*Weixing Wang,Liudvikas Zekas,Anton Hackl,Constantin Alexander Auga,Parisa Shahabinejad,Jona Otholt,Antonio Rueda-Toicen,Gerard de Melo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出XTC-Bench评估框架，通过场景图驱动的跨任务视觉语义一致性测试，发现统一多模态模型的高性能不保证生成与理解任务间的语义对齐，一致性由学习目标耦合程度决定而非架构统一本身。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有统一多模态模型的评估独立测试视觉理解与生成能力，未考察两者间的语义对齐程度，因此无法判断模型是否学到了真正一致的统一表示。

Method: 提出XTC-Bench框架，基于结构化场景图同时派生出生成提示和理解查询，实现对象、属性、关系层面的事实级对齐分析；并设计连续跨任务一致性（CCTA）细粒度指标，通过比对匹配原子事实上的生成与理解语义一致性来隔离内部一致性与独立任务准确性。

Result: 在8个开源和1个商业统一模型上的实验表明，高生成或理解性能并不意味着强跨任务对齐；架构分析发现，一致性由跨模态学习目标的耦合紧密程度决定，而非仅靠架构统一。

Conclusion: XTC-Bench提供了一种可复现、模型无关的诊断框架，可用于检测表示层面的跨任务语义失调，为超越孤立任务性能推进统一多模态建模提供了具体方向。

Original Abstract: Unified Multimodal Models (uMMs) aim to support both visual understanding and visual generation within a shared representation. However, existing evaluation protocols assess these two capabilities independently and do not examine whether they are semantically aligned. As a result, it remains unclear whether current uMMs learn coherent unified representations that remain consistent across tasks given a visual concept. We introduce XTC-Bench, a scene-graph-grounded evaluation framework that measures cross-task visual semantic consistency. By deriving both generation prompts and understanding queries from a structured scene graph, our framework enables fact-level alignment analysis across objects, attributes, and relations. We propose Continuous Cross-Task Agreement (CCTA), a fine-grained metric that quantifies semantic agreement between generation and understanding over matched atomic facts, isolating internal consistency from standalone task accuracy. Extensive experiments on eight open-source and one commercial unified models reveal that high generation or understanding performance does not imply strong cross-task alignment, and architectural analysis shows consistency is governed by how tightly learning objectives are coupled across modalities, not by architectural unification alone. XTC-Bench provides a reproducible and model-agnostic framework for diagnosing representation-level misalignment, offering a concrete direction for advancing unified multimodal modeling beyond isolated task performance.

中文摘要翻译: 统一多模态模型（uMMs）旨在共享表示空间中同时支持视觉理解和视觉生成。然而，现有的评估协议独立测试这两种能力，并未考察它们是否在语义上对齐。因此，当前uMMs是否真正学习了对于同一视觉概念在跨任务中保持一致的统一表示仍不明确。我们提出了XTC-Bench，一个基于场景图驱动的评估框架，用于衡量跨任务视觉语义一致性。通过从结构化场景图中同时派生出生成提示和理解查询，我们的框架能够在对象、属性和关系层面实现事实级的对齐分析。我们提出了连续跨任务一致性（CCTA），一种细粒度指标，通过对齐匹配的原子事实上的生成与理解语义一致性来量化语义一致性，从而将内部一致性与独立任务准确性分离开来。在8个开源和1个商业统一模型上的大量实验表明，高生成或理解性能并不意味着强跨任务对齐；架构分析显示，一致性取决于跨模态学习目标的耦合紧密程度，而非仅由架构统一决定。XTC-Bench提供了一个可复现且模型无关的诊断框架，用于检测表示层面的失调，为超越孤立任务性能推进统一多模态建模提供了具体方向。

### [11] [M$^3$-VQA: A Benchmark for Multimodal, Multi-Entity, Multi-Hop Visual Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25122)
*Jiatong Ma,Longteng Guo,Yuchen Liu,Zijia Zhao,Dongze Hao,Xuanxu Lin,Jing Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: M$^3$-VQA是一个新颖的基于知识的VQA基准，旨在评估多模态大模型在细粒度多实体理解和复杂多跳推理方面的能力。实验表明，现有模型在该基准上表现不佳，但提供精确证据和推理感知的检索可以显著提升性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有VQA数据集多关注粗粒度类别和单实体简单推理，缺乏对多实体、多文档、多跳推理的评估，因此需要构建一个更具挑战性的基准来推动多模态大模型在多模态推理能力上的发展。

Method: 构建M$^3$-VQA基准，包含多实体问题，要求模型从视觉和文本来源中同时进行序列型和并行型多跳推理；提供可追溯的详细证据和 curated 多模态知识库；在无外部知识、有黄金证据、检索增强输入三种设置下评估16个主流MLLM。

Result: 16个主流MLLM在M$^3$-VQA上表现普遍较差；无外部知识时模型性能低下，提供精确证据后显著提升；推理感知的智能体检索优于启发式检索方法，表明结构化推理对复杂多模态理解的重要性。

Conclusion: M$^3$-VQA为评估多模态大模型在多实体理解和复杂多跳推理方面提出了更具挑战性的基准，揭示了当前模型在知识获取与推理方面的显著不足，并强调了结构化推理对于复杂多模态理解的重要性。

Original Abstract: We present M$^3$-VQA, a novel knowledge-based Visual Question Answering (VQA) benchmark, to enhance the evaluation of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) in fine-grained multimodal entity understanding and complex multi-hop reasoning. Unlike existing VQA datasets that focus on coarse-grained categories and simple reasoning over single entities, M$^3$-VQA introduces diverse multi-entity questions involving multiple distinct entities from both visual and textual sources. It requires models to perform both sequential and parallel multi-hop reasoning across multiple documents, supported by traceable, detailed evidence and a curated multimodal knowledge base. We evaluate 16 leading MLLMs under three settings: without external knowledge, with gold evidence, and with retrieval-augmented input. The poor results reveal significant challenges for MLLMs in knowledge acquisition and reasoning. Models perform poorly without external information but improve markedly when provided with precise evidence. Furthermore, reasoning-aware agentic retrieval surpasses heuristic methods, highlighting the importance of structured reasoning for complex multimodal understanding. M$^3$-VQA presents a more challenging evaluation for advancing the multimodal reasoning capabilities of MLLMs. Our code and dataset are available at https://github.com/CASIA-IVA-Lab/M3VQA.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了M$^3$-VQA，一个新颖的基于知识的视觉问答（VQA）基准，旨在增强对多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在细粒度多实体理解和复杂多跳推理方面的评估。与现有聚焦于粗粒度类别和单实体简单推理的VQA数据集不同，M$^3$-VQA引入了涉及视觉和文本来源中多个不同实体的多样化多实体问题。它要求模型在多个文档上执行序列型和并行型多跳推理，并配备可追溯的详细证据和一个精选的多模态知识库。我们在三种设置下评估了16个主流MLLM：无外部知识、提供黄金证据、以及检索增强输入。较差的结果揭示了MLLMs在知识获取和推理方面面临的重大挑战。模型在没有外部信息时表现不佳，但在提供精确证据后显著提升。此外，推理感知的智能体检索优于启发式方法，突显了结构化推理对于复杂多模态理解的重要性。M$^3$-VQA为推进MLLMs的多模态推理能力提供了更具挑战性的评估。我们的代码和数据集可在https://github.com/CASIA-IVA-Lab/M3VQA获取。

</details>


### [12] [ResetEdit: Precise Text-guided Editing of Generated Image via Resettable Starting Latent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25128)
*Hanyi Wang,Han Fang,Zheng Wang,Shilin Wang,Ee-Chien Chang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ResetEdit 是一种主动扩散编辑框架，通过将可恢复的潜在信息嵌入生成过程，解决现有反演方法在图像编辑中起始噪声不理想的问题，实现高质量局部编辑。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于反演的编辑方法（如 DDIM 反演）得到的起始潜在编码质量不佳，导致编辑保真度下降和结构不一致；理想的起始点应为生成过程中使用的原始潜在编码，但存储所有图像的原始潜在编码不切实际。

Method: 在扩散过程中将干净潜在与加噪潜在之间的差异注入扩散轨迹；在反演时提取该差异，重构出接近真实起始状态的可重置潜在编码；同时使用轻量级潜在优化模块补偿 VAE 不对称性带来的重建偏差。

Result: 基于 Stable Diffusion 构建，可无缝集成现有免调优编辑方法，在可控性和视觉保真度上持续优于最先进基线。

Conclusion: ResetEdit 通过主动嵌入可恢复潜在信息，在不增加存储开销的前提下，实现了更高质量、更精确的局部图像编辑。

Original Abstract: Recent advances in diffusion models have enabled high-quality image generation, leading to increasing demand for post-generation editing that modifies local regions while preserving global structure. Achieving such flexible and precise editing requires a high-quality starting point, a latent representation that provides both the freedom needed for diverse modifications and the precision required for fine-grained, region-specific control. However, existing inversion-based approaches such as DDIM inversion often yield unsatisfactory starting latents, resulting in degraded edit fidelity and structural inconsistency. Ideally, the most suitable editing anchor should be the original latent used during the generation process, as it inherently captures the scene's structure and semantics. Yet, storing this latent for every generated image is impractical due to massive storage and retrieval costs. To address this challenge, we propose ResetEdit, a proactive diffusion editing framework that embeds recoverable latent information directly into the generation process. By injecting the discrepancy between the clean and diffused latents into the diffusion trajectory and extracting it during inversion, ResetEdit reconstructs a resettable latent that closely approximates the true starting state. Additionally, a lightweight latent optimization module compensates for reconstruction bias caused by VAE asymmetry. Built upon Stable Diffusion, ResetEdit integrates seamlessly with existing tuning-free editing methods and consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both controllability and visual fidelity.

中文摘要翻译: 扩散模型的最新进展已实现高质量图像生成，这导致了对生成后编辑的日益增长的需求，即修改局部区域同时保持全局结构。实现这种灵活而精确的编辑需要一个高质量的起点，即一个既能提供多样化修改所需的自由度，又能提供细粒度区域特定控制所需精度的潜在表示。然而，现有的基于反演的方法（如 DDIM 反演）通常产生不令人满意的起始潜在编码，导致编辑保真度下降和结构不一致。理想情况下，最合适的编辑锚点应为生成过程中使用的原始潜在编码，因为它固有地捕捉了场景的结构和语义。然而，由于巨大的存储和检索成本，为每个生成图像存储该潜在编码是不切实际的。为应对这一挑战，我们提出 ResetEdit，一种主动扩散编辑框架，它将可恢复的潜在信息直接嵌入生成过程。通过将干净潜在与加噪潜在之间的差异注入扩散轨迹并在反演过程中提取该差异，ResetEdit 重构出一个紧密逼近真实起始状态的可重置潜在编码。此外，一个轻量级潜在优化模块补偿了由 VAE 不对称性引起的重建偏差。基于 Stable Diffusion 构建，ResetEdit 能够与现有免调优编辑方法无缝集成，并在可控性和视觉保真度上持续优于最先进的基线方法。

### [13] [IAM: Identity-Aware Human Motion and Shape Joint Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25164)
*Wenqi Jia,Zekun Li,Abhay Mittal,Chengcheng Tang,Chuan Guo,Lezi Wang,James Matthew Rehg,Lingling Tao,Size An*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种身份感知的运动生成框架IAM，通过多模态信号（语言描述和视觉线索）显式建模身体形态与运动动力学之间的关系，并采用联合运动-形状生成范式，实现更真实、身份一致的运动序列合成。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有文本驱动运动生成方法大多假设身份中性的运动，使用标准人体表征生成动作，忽略了身体形态（如身体比例、质量分布、年龄）对运动动力学的显著影响，导致生成的物理运动不一致。

Method: 提出身份感知运动生成框架IAM，使用多模态信号（自然语言描述和视觉线索）表示身份而非显式几何测量；引入联合运动-形状生成范式，同时合成运动序列和身体形状参数，使身份线索直接调制运动动力学。

Result: 在运动捕捉数据集和大规模真实世界视频上的实验表明，该方法在保持高运动质量的同时，实现了更真实的运动效果和运动-身份一致性。

Conclusion: 显式建模身体形态与运动动力学的耦合关系能够显著提升生成运动的真实性和身份一致性。

Original Abstract: Recent advances in text-driven human motion generation enable models to synthesize realistic motion sequences from natural language descriptions. However, most existing approaches assume identity-neutral motion and generate movements using a canonical body representation, ignoring the strong influence of body morphology on motion dynamics. In practice, attributes such as body proportions, mass distribution, and age significantly affect how actions are performed, and neglecting this coupling often leads to physically inconsistent motions. We propose an identity-aware motion generation framework that explicitly models the relationship between body morphology and motion dynamics. Instead of relying on explicit geometric measurements, identity is represented using multimodal signals, including natural language descriptions and visual cues. We further introduce a joint motion-shape generation paradigm that simultaneously synthesizes motion sequences and body shape parameters, allowing identity cues to directly modulate motion dynamics. Extensive experiments on motion capture datasets and large-scale in-the-wild videos demonstrate improved motion realism and motion-identity consistency while maintaining high motion quality. Project page: https://vjwq.github.io/IAM

中文摘要翻译: 文本驱动的行人运动生成领域的最新进展使得模型能够根据自然语言描述合成逼真的运动序列。然而，现有大多数方法假设身份中性的运动，并使用标准人体表征生成动作，忽略了身体形态对运动动力学的强烈影响。实际上，身体比例、质量分布和年龄等属性会显著影响动作的执行方式，忽视这种耦合关系往往导致物理上不一致的运动。我们提出了一种身份感知的运动生成框架，显式建模身体形态与运动动力学之间的关系。不同于依赖显式几何测量，身份通过多模态信号表示，包括自然语言描述和视觉线索。我们进一步引入了一种联合运动-形状生成范式，同时合成运动序列和身体形状参数，使得身份线索能够直接调制运动动力学。在运动捕捉数据集和大规模真实世界视频上的大量实验表明，该方法在保持高运动质量的同时，实现了更真实的运动效果和运动-身份一致性。项目页面：https://vjwq.github.io/IAM

### [14] [FCMBench-Video: Benchmarking Document Video Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25186)
*Runze Cui,Fangxin Shang,Yehui Yang,Qing Yang,Tao Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FCMBench-Video 是一个面向文档视频理解的基准测试，通过原子采集与组合工作流构建大规模隐私合规数据，评估 Video-MLLM 在文档感知、时间定位和证据推理方面的能力，实验表明该基准能有效区分不同模型能力且未饱和。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有文档理解研究多聚焦于静态图像，而真实信贷审核等场景中的文档视频包含时间冗余、时序证据流和采集过程线索，对防欺诈和真实性审查至关重要，但缺乏专门评估文档视频智能的基准。

Method: 提出原子采集与组合工作流：先录制可复用的单文档原子视频片段并施加受控退化，再组装成长篇多文档视频，配以11,322个专家标注的问答实例，覆盖28种文档类型、20-60秒时长层级和5,960个中文/5,362个英文实例。

Result: 对9个最新Video-MLLM的评估显示：(1)计数是时长最敏感的任务；(2)跨文档验证和基于证据的选择测试了更高级的证据整合能力；(3)视觉提示注入提供了互补的鲁棒性维度；(4)整体得分分布呈宽钟形，基准未被饱和或由琐碎案例主导。

Conclusion: FCMBench-Video 可作为可复现的基准来追踪 Video-MLLM 在文档视频理解上的进展，并探测其在真实性敏感的信用领域应用中的能力边界。

Original Abstract: Document understanding is a critical capability in financial credit review, onboarding, and remote verification, where both decision accuracy and evidence traceability matter. Compared with static document images, document videos present a temporally redundant and sequentially unfolding evidence stream, require evidence integration across frames, and preserve acquisition-process cues relevant to authenticity-sensitive and anti-fraud review. We introduce FCMBench-Video, a benchmark for document-video intelligence that evaluates document perception, temporal grounding, and evidence-grounded reasoning under realistic capture conditions. For privacy-compliant yet realistic data at scale, we organize construction as an atomic-acquisition and composition workflow that records reusable single-document clips, applies controlled degradations, and assembles long-form multi-document videos with prescribed temporal spans. FCMBench-Video is built from 495 atomic videos composed into 1,200 long-form videos paired with 11,322 expert-annotated question--answer instances, covering 28 document types over 20s--60s duration tiers and 5,960 Chinese / 5,362 English instances. Evaluations on nine recent Video-MLLMs show that FCMBench-Video provides meaningful separation across systems and capabilities: counting is the most duration-sensitive task, Cross-Document Validation and Evidence-Grounded Selection probe higher-level evidence integration, and Visual Prompt Injection provides a complementary robustness dimension. The overall score distribution is broad and approximately bell-shaped, indicating a benchmark that is neither saturated nor dominated by trivial cases. Together, these results position FCMBench-Video as a reproducible benchmark for tracking Video-MLLM progress on document-video understanding and probing capability boundaries in authenticity-sensitive credit-domain applications.

中文摘要翻译: 文档理解是金融信贷审核、入职认证和远程核身等场景中的关键能力，这类场景同时对决策准确性和证据可追溯性有严格要求。与静态文档图像相比，文档视频呈现时间上冗余且时序展开的证据流，需要跨帧整合证据，并保留了与真实性敏感和反欺诈审核相关的采集过程线索。我们提出了 FCMBench-Video，一个面向文档视频智能的基准测试，用于评估在逼真采集条件下的文档感知、时间定位和基于证据的推理能力。为了在保护隐私的前提下大规模获取逼真数据，我们设计了一套原子采集与组合工作流：录制可复用的单文档片段、施加受控退化、再组装成具有规定时间跨度的长篇多文档视频。FCMBench-Video 由 495 个原子视频构建成 1,200 个长视频，配以 11,322 个专家标注的问答实例，覆盖 28 种文档类型，时长范围 20-60 秒，包含 5,960 个中文实例和 5,362 个英文实例。对九个最新 Video-MLLM 的评估表明，FCMBench-Video 能够有效区分不同系统和能力之间的差异：计数是时长最敏感的任务，跨文档验证和基于证据的选择考验了更高级的证据整合能力，视觉提示注入则提供了互补的鲁棒性维度。整体得分分布宽广且近似钟形，说明该基准既未饱和也未由琐碎案例主导。综上，这些结果使 FCMBench-Video 成为一个可复现的基准，用于追踪 Video-MLLM 在文档视频理解上的进展，并探测其在真实性敏感的信用领域应用中的能力边界。

### [15] [When the Forger Is the Judge: GPT-Image-2 Cannot Recognize Its Own Faked Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25213)
*Jiaqi Wu,Yuchen Zhou,Dennis Tsang Ng,Xingyu Shen,Kidus Zewde,Ankit Raj,Tommy Duong,Simiao Ren*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发布了一个包含3,066张GPT-Image-2伪造文档图像的数据集AIForge-Doc v2，并评估了人类 inspectors（准确率0.501，等同随机猜测）和三种计算检测器（TruFor 0.599、DocTamper 0.585、自判断0.532）对AI编辑文档图像的检测能力，发现所有方法均无法有效区分GPT-Image-2伪造的收据与真实收据。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: OpenAI的GPT-Image-2模型已经能够以极低的成本在数秒内替换文档图像中的数字（如收据金额），模糊了真实与AI编辑文档之间的视觉边界。现有取证方法是否能够检测这种新型AI编辑文档成为一个亟待回答的问题。

Method: 构建了3,066张GPT-Image-2文档伪造图像数据集，采用像素级精确掩膜注释；设计四类检测方案进行基准测试：(1) 人类 inspectors（通过2AFC网站进行120人、365组配对投票）；(2) 通用取证模型TruFor；(3) 文档专用取证模型DocTamper；(4) GPT-Image-2模型本身作为零样本自判断。同时构建同域传统篡改校准集以排除检测器在源域失效的可能性。

Result: 人类2AFC准确率为0.501，与随机猜测无异；TruFor准确率0.599、DocTamper为0.585、自判断为0.532。自判断在5种提示策略和4种模糊响应处理策略下AUC均未超过0.59。在传统篡改上，TruFor AUC达0.962，DocTamper达0.852，但切换到GPT-Image-2修复后分别下降0.27-0.36。

Conclusion: GPT-Image-2生成的文档伪造对当前所有检测手段——包括人类 inspectors、通用取证模型、文档专用模型乃至生成模型本身——均构成了重大挑战，存在一个特定于GPT-Image-2修复的检测缺口。

Original Abstract: OpenAI's GPT-Image-2 has effectively erased the visual boundary between authentic and AI-edited document images: a single number on a receipt can be replaced in under a second for a few cents. We release AIForge-Doc v2, a paired dataset of 3,066 GPT-Image-2 document forgeries with pixel-precise masks in DocTamper-compatible format, and benchmark four lines of defence: human inspectors (N=120, n=365 pair-votes via the public 2AFC site CanUSpotAI.com), TruFor (generic forensic), DocTamper (qcf-568, document-specific), and the same GPT-Image-2 model as a zero-shot self-judge -- asked, to avoid the trivial "image is mostly real" reading, whether any region was generated or edited by an AI image model. Human 2AFC accuracy is 0.501, indistinguishable from chance: even side-by-side, inspectors cannot tell GPT-Image-2 receipt forgeries from authentic counterparts. The three computational judges sit only modestly above (TruFor 0.599, DocTamper 0.585, self-judge 0.532). The self-judge fails consistently, not by chance: across five prompt strategies and four policies for handling ambiguous responses, AUC never rises above 0.59. To rule out the possibility that the two forensic detectors are broken on our source domain rather than blind to AI inpainting, we calibrate each on a same-domain traditional-tampering set built for its training distribution: TruFor reaches AUC 0.962 on cross-camera splicing of our dataset, DocTamper reaches 0.852 on cross-document OCR-token splicing with two-pass JPEG re-encoding. Both retain near-published performance on traditional tampering; switching to GPT-Image-2 inpainting drops AUC by 0.27-0.36 (0.962->0.599 TruFor; 0.852->0.585 DocTamper), isolating a detection gap specific to GPT-Image-2 inpainting. We release the dataset, pipeline, four-judge protocol, and calibration sets.

中文摘要翻译: OpenAI的GPT-Image-2有效地抹去了真实文档图像与AI编辑文档图像之间的视觉边界：收据上的单个数字可以在不到一秒内以几美分的成本被替换。我们发布了AIForge-Doc v2，这是一个包含3,066张GPT-Image-2文档伪造图像的数据集，配有像素级精度的掩膜，采用DocTamper兼容格式，并对四类检测方案进行了基准测试：人类 inspectors（N=120，n=365组配对投票，通过公开的2AFC网站CanUSpotAI.com进行）、TruFor（通用取证）、DocTamper（qcf-568，文档专用）以及同一个GPT-Image-2模型作为零样本自判断——该方法被要求判断是否存在任何区域是由AI图像模型生成或编辑的，以避免琐碎的"图像大部分是真实的"解读。人类2AFC准确率为0.501，与随机猜测无法区分：即使在并列对比的情况下，检查人员也无法区分GPT-Image-2伪造的收据与真实收据。三种计算判断器的表现仅略高于随机水平（TruFor 0.599，DocTamper 0.585，自判断0.532）。自判断并非偶然地持续失败：在五种提示策略和四种处理模糊响应的策略下，AUC从未超过0.59。为了排除两个取证检测器在我们的源域上失效而非对AI修复图像失明的可能性，我们在为其训练分布构建的同域传统篡改集上对每个检测器进行了校准：TruFor在数据集内跨相机拼接任务上达到AUC 0.962，DocTamper在跨文档OCR令牌拼接加两遍JPEG重编码任务上达到0.852。两者在传统篡改上均保持了接近已发表性能的水平；切换至GPT-Image-2修复后，AUC下降了0.27-0.36（TruFor从0.962降至0.599；DocTamper从0.852降至0.585），分离出一个特定于GPT-Image-2修复的检测缺口。我们发布了该数据集、流水线、四判断器协议以及校准集。

</details>


### [16] [DRAGON: A Benchmark for Evidence-Grounded Visual Reasoning over Diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25231)
*Anirudh Iyengar Kaniyar Narayana Iyengar,Tampu Ravi Kumar,Gaurav Najpande,Manan Suri,Dinesh Manocha,Puneet Mathur,Vivek Gupta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出DRAGON基准，用于评估图表问答中模型能否定位支持答案的视觉证据区域，而非仅关注答案正确性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在图表问答上虽能获得高正确率，但正确回答并不保证模型真正基于图示区域的视觉证据进行推理，模型可能依赖文本相关性或数据集伪影，导致推理评估不可靠且可解释性差。

Method: 构建DRAGON数据集：从六个图表QA数据集（ChartQA、Circuit-VQA、InfographicsVQA、MapIQ、MapWise、AI2D）收集11,664个带注释的问题实例，并发布2,445个含人工验证证据标注的测试集及标准化评估框架，要求模型预测支持答案的视觉元素边界框。

Result: 评估了8个近期视觉语言模型，分析了它们在不同图表领域中定位推理证据的能力，结果表明DRAGON能够系统性地评估图表推理的证据定位能力。

Conclusion: DRAGON能够支持对图表视觉推理的系统性评估，为未来研究提供模型在视觉证据上实现预测可解释性的基础。

Original Abstract: Diagram question answering (DQA) requires models to interpret structured visual representations such as charts, maps, infographics, circuit schematics, and scientific diagrams. Recent vision-language models (VLMs) often achieve high answer accuracy on these tasks, yet correct answers do not guarantee that models ground their reasoning in the diagram regions that support the prediction. Models may instead rely on textual correlations or dataset artifacts without identifying the visual evidence required to verify the answer. This limitation prevents reliable evaluation of diagram reasoning and reduces interpretability. We introduce DRAGON, a benchmark for evaluating evidence-grounded visual reasoning in diagrams. Given a diagram, a question, and the correct answer, a model must predict bounding boxes that correspond to the visual elements required to justify the answer. These evidence regions may include answer-bearing components, textual labels, legends, axes, connectors, and other supporting structures involved in the reasoning process. The DRAGON dataset contains 11,664 annotated question instances collected from six diagram QA datasets: ChartQA, Circuit-VQA, InfographicsVQA, MapIQ, MapWise, and AI2D. We release a 2,445-instance benchmark test set with human-verified reasoning evidence annotations and a standardized evaluation framework. We evaluate eight recent VLMs and analyze their ability to localize reasoning evidence across diverse diagram domains. DRAGON enables systematic evaluation of diagram reasoning and supports future research on models that ground their predictions in visual evidence.

中文摘要翻译: 图表问答（DQA）要求模型解释结构化视觉表示，如图表、地图、信息图、电路原理图和科学示意图。近期视觉语言模型（VLM）在这些任务上往往能达到较高的答案准确率，但正确答案并不能保证模型将推理过程定位于支持预测的图表区域。模型可能依赖文本相关性或数据集伪影，而无需识别验证答案所需的视觉证据。这一局限性阻碍了对图表推理的可靠评估，并降低了可解释性。我们提出DRAGON，一个用于评估图表中基于证据的视觉推理的基准。给定一个图表、一个问题以及正确的答案，模型必须预测对应于证明答案所需的视觉元素的边界框。这些证据区域可能包括承载答案的组件、文本标签、图例、坐标轴、连接线以及其他参与推理过程的支持性结构。DRAGON数据集包含从六个图表QA数据集（ChartQA、Circuit-VQA、InfographicsVQA、MapIQ、MapWise和AI2D）收集的11,664个带注释的问题实例。我们发布了一个包含2,445个实例的基准测试集，带有经人工验证的推理证据标注及标准化评估框架。我们评估了八个最近的VLM，并分析了它们在不同图表领域中定位推理证据的能力。DRAGON使得对图表推理的系统性评估成为可能，并支持未来将预测基于视觉证据的模型研究。

</details>


### [17] [Personalized Cross-Modal Emotional Correlation Learning for Speech-Preserving Facial Expression Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25255)
*Tianshui Chen,Yujie Zhu,Jianman Lin,Zhijing Yang,Chunmei Qing,Feng Gao,Liang Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种个性化跨模态情感关联学习算法(PCMECL)，通过个性化提示学习和特征差分对齐，解决了语音保留面部表情操控中因配对数据稀缺而导致的视觉-语义监督信号不对齐问题，可作为即插即用模块提升现有模型性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 语音保留面部表情操控面临配对数据稀缺的挑战，现有视觉-语言模型(VLM)虽能提供监督信号，但存在两个关键问题：(1) 标准VLM为每种情绪使用单一通用提示，无法捕捉个体间的表达差异；(2) 视觉特征与语义特征之间存在固有的模态分布差异，导致监督信号不对齐。

Method: 提出个性化跨模态情感关联学习(PCMECL)算法，包含两个核心改进：(1) 基于个体视觉信息学习个性化提示(personalized prompts)，建立更细粒度的视觉-语义关联；(2) 采用特征差分(feature differencing)方法，通过匹配视觉特征变化与语义特征变化来桥接模态差异，提供更精确对齐的监督信号。该方法可作为即插即用模块集成到现有SPFEM模型中。

Result: 在多个数据集上的大量实验表明，所提算法具有优越的性能。

Conclusion: PCMECL通过学习个性化提示和特征差分对齐，有效解决了VLM监督信号在SPFEM任务中的不对齐问题，作为即插即用模块能提升现有模型性能。

Original Abstract: Speech-preserving facial expression manipulation (SPFEM) aims to enhance human expressiveness without altering mouth movements tied to the original speech. A primary challenge in this domain is the scarcity of paired data, namely aligned frames of the same individual with identical speech but different expressions, which impedes direct supervision for emotional manipulation. While current Visual-Language Models (VLMs) can extract aligned visual and semantic features, making them a promising source of supervision, their direct application is limited. To this end, we propose a Personalized Cross-Modal Emotional Correlation Learning (PCMECL) algorithm that refines VLM-based supervision through two major improvements. First, standard VLMs rely on a single generic prompt for each emotion, failing to capture expressive variations among individuals. PCMECL addresses this limitation by conditioning on individual visual information to learn personalized prompts, thereby establishing more fine-grained visual-semantic correlations. Second, even with personalization, inherent discrepancies persist between the visual and semantic feature distributions. To bridge this modality gap, PCMECL employs feature differencing to correlate the modalities, providing more precisely aligned supervision by matching the change in visual features to the change in semantic features. As a plug-and-play module, PCMECL can be seamlessly integrated into existing SPFEM models. Extensive experiments across various datasets demonstrate the superior efficacy of our algorithm.

中文摘要翻译: 语音保留面部表情操控(Speech-preserving facial expression manipulation, SPFEM)旨在增强人类表现力，同时不改变与原始语音相关的口部运动。该领域的一个主要挑战是配对数据的稀缺性，即同一人在相同语音下具有不同表情的对齐帧，这阻碍了对情感操控的直接监督。虽然当前的视觉-语言模型(VLMs)可以提取对齐的视觉和语义特征，使其成为一种有前景的监督来源，但其直接应用受到限制。为此，我们提出了一种个性化跨模态情感关联学习(Personalized Cross-Modal Emotional Correlation Learning, PCMECL)算法，通过两项主要改进来优化基于VLM的监督。首先，标准VLM依赖每种情绪的单一通用提示，未能捕捉个体间的表达变化。PCMECL通过基于个体视觉信息学习个性化提示来解决这一限制，从而建立更细粒度的视觉-语义关联。其次，即使经过个性化处理，视觉和语义特征分布之间仍然存在固有差异。为了弥合这一模态差距，PCMECL采用特征差分来关联模态，通过匹配视觉特征变化与语义特征变化来提供更精确对齐的监督。作为一个即插即用模块，PCMECL可以无缝集成到现有的SPFEM模型中。在多个数据集上进行的大量实验证明了我们算法的优越性能。

</details>


### [18] [Combating Visual Neglect and Semantic Drift in Large Multimodal Models for Enhanced Cross-Modal Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25273)
*Guosheng Zhang,Linkai Liu,Keyao Wang,Haixiao Yue,Zhiwen Tan,Xiao Tan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对统一多模态检索中现有方法忽视主体级语义、导致语义对齐偏差和视觉模态忽视的问题，提出SSA-ME框架，通过显著性感知建模、特征重校准等机制提升细粒度表示学习，在MMEB基准上达到SOTA性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于LMM的统一多模态检索方法仅通过对比学习关注样本级目标，忽略了关键的主体级语义，导致模型无法在复杂多模态查询中对语义一致的主体进行分组，出现语义对齐偏差（无法精确定位文本所指的视觉区域）以及视觉模态忽视（过度依赖文本线索，视觉知识利用不足）的问题。

Method: 提出SSA-ME框架，包括：1）利用LMM和视觉专家识别并强调图像-文本对中的显著视觉概念；2）引入显著性引导目标，更好地对齐跨模态注意力与语义有意义的区域；3）特征重生成模块，基于显著性图重新校准视觉特征，确保跨模态的平衡且语义一致的集成。

Result: 在MMEB基准上达到最先进性能，大量定性分析进一步验证了方法的可解释性和有效性。

Conclusion: 融入主体级建模能显著提升多模态检索性能。

Original Abstract: Despite significant progress in Unified Multimodal Retrieval (UMR) powered by Large Multimodal Models (LMMs), existing embedding methods primarily focus on sample-level objectives via contrastive learning while overlooking the crucial subject-level semantics. This limitation hinders the model's ability to group semantically coherent subjects in complex multimodal queries, manifesting as semantic alignment deviation--where models fail to accurately localize salient text-referred regions in visual content. Moreover, without explicit guidance to model salient visual subjects, LMMs tend to over-rely on textual cues, resulting in visual modality neglect and suboptimal utilization of visual knowledge. To this end, we propose Salient Subject-Aware Multimodal Embedding (SSA-ME), a novel framework designed to enhance fine-grained representation learning through saliency-aware modeling. SSA-ME leverages LMMs and visual experts to identify and emphasize salient visual concepts in image-text pairs, and introduces a saliency-guided objective to better align cross-modal attention with semantically meaningful regions. Additionally, a feature regeneration module recalibrates visual features based on the derived saliency maps, ensuring a balanced and semantically coherent integration across modalities. Extensive experiments show that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on the MMEB benchmark, demonstrating that incorporating subject-level modeling substantially improves multimodal retrieval. Comprehensive qualitative analyses further illustrate the interpretability and effectiveness of our approach.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管基于大型多模态模型（LMM）的统一多模态检索（UMR）取得了显著进展，但现有的嵌入方法主要通过对比学习关注样本级目标，而忽略了关键的主体级语义。这一局限性阻碍了模型在复杂多模态查询中对语义一致的主体进行分组，表现为语义对齐偏差——模型无法精确定位视觉内容中文本所指的显著区域。此外，由于缺乏对显著视觉主体建模的显式指导，LMM倾向于过度依赖文本线索，导致视觉模态忽视以及视觉知识利用欠佳。为此，我们提出了显著主体感知多模态嵌入（SSA-ME），一种通过显著性感知建模来增强细粒度表示学习的新型框架。SSA-ME利用LMM和视觉专家来识别并强调图像-文本对中的显著视觉概念，并引入一个显著性引导目标以更好地将跨模态注意力与语义有意义的区域对齐。此外，特征重生成模块基于推导出的显著性图重新校准视觉特征，确保跨模态的平衡且语义一致的集成。大量实验表明，我们的方法在MMEB基准上达到了最先进的性能，证明了融入主体级建模能显著提升多模态检索。全面的定性分析进一步展示了我们方法的可解释性和有效性。

</details>


### [19] [OmniVTG: A Large-Scale Dataset and Training Paradigm for Open-World Video Temporal Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25276)
*Minghang Zheng,Zihao Yin,Yi Yang,Yuxin Peng,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出OmniVTG大规模数据集和自校正思维链训练范式，通过语义覆盖迭代扩展管道构建数据集，并利用MLLM理解能力超越直接定位能力的观察，设计三阶段训练（SFT、CoT微调、强化学习）提升开放世界视频时序定位性能，在四个现有基准上达到零样本SOTA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视频时序定位数据集规模有限、语义多样性不足，导致常见概念与罕见概念之间存在性能差距，难以应对开放世界场景。

Method: (1) 构建OmniVTG数据集：采用语义覆盖迭代扩展管道，识别现有数据集词汇缺口，收集含目标概念的视频，并利用MLLM擅长密集字幕标注而非直接定位的特点，设计字幕中心数据引擎生成带时间戳的密集描述。(2) 提出自校正思维链训练范式：三阶段流程——有监督微调、思维链微调、强化学习，训练MLLM先预测再反思和修正自身预测。

Result: 在OmniVTG数据集上开放世界定位表现优异，在四个现有VTG基准上达到零样本SOTA性能。

Conclusion: 自校正思维链训练范式有效弥合了MLLM视频理解能力与直接定位能力之间的差距，显著提升了开放场景下的泛化能力。

Original Abstract: Video Temporal Grounding (VTG), the task of localizing video segments from text queries, struggles in open-world settings due to limited dataset scale and semantic diversity, causing performance gaps between common and rare concepts. To overcome these limitations, we introduce OmniVTG, a new large-scale dataset for open-world VTG, coupled with a Self-Correction Chain-of-Thought (CoT) training paradigm designed to enhance the grounding capabilities of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). Our OmniVTG is constructed via a novel Semantic Coverage Iterative Expansion pipeline, which first identifies gaps in the vocabulary of existing datasets and collects videos that are highly likely to contain these target concepts. For high-quality annotation, we leverage the insight that modern MLLMs excel at dense captioning more than direct grounding and design a caption-centric data engine to prompt MLLMs to generate dense, timestamped descriptions. Beyond the dataset, we observe that simple supervised finetuning (SFT) is insufficient, as a performance gap between rare and common concepts still persists. We find that MLLMs' video understanding ability significantly surpasses their direct grounding ability. Based on this, we propose a Self-Correction Chain-of-Thought (CoT) training paradigm. We train the MLLM to first predict, then use its understanding capabilities to reflect on and refine its own predictions. This capability is instilled via a three-stage pipeline of SFT, CoT finetuning, and reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments show our approach not only excels at open-world grounding in our OmniVTG dataset but also achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot performance on four existing VTG benchmarks. Code is available at https://github.com/oceanflowlab/OmniVTG.

中文摘要翻译: 视频时序定位（VTG）任务旨在从文本查询中定位视频片段，但由于数据集规模和语义多样性的限制，在开放世界场景中面临挑战，导致常见概念与罕见概念之间存在性能差距。为克服这些局限，我们引入了OmniVTG——一个面向开放世界VTG的大规模新数据集，并搭配了自校正思维链训练范式，旨在增强多模态大语言模型的定位能力。我们的OmniVTG通过一种新颖的语义覆盖迭代扩展管道构建，该管道首先识别现有数据集词汇中的缺口，然后收集极可能包含这些目标概念的视频。为实现高质量标注，我们利用现代MLLM擅长密集字幕标注而非直接定位这一洞察，设计了一个字幕中心数据引擎，提示MLLM生成带时间戳的密集描述。除数据集外，我们观察到简单的有监督微调（SFT）并不足够，罕见概念与常见概念之间的性能差距依然存在。我们发现MLLM的视频理解能力显著超越其直接定位能力。基于此，我们提出了一种自校正思维链（CoT）训练范式。我们训练MLLM先进行预测，然后利用其理解能力反思并修正自身的预测。这一能力通过SFT、CoT微调和强化学习三阶段流程来灌输。大量实验表明，我们的方法不仅在我们OmniVTG数据集的开放世界定位中表现出色，而且在四个现有VTG基准上达到了最先进的零样本性能。代码开源在 https://github.com/oceanflowlab/OmniVTG。

</details>


### [20] [Edge-Cloud Collaborative Reconstruction via Structure-Aware Latent Diffusion for Downstream Remote Sensing Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25319)
*Yun Li,Xianju Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对高分辨率遥感数据下传带宽瓶颈导致高频细节丢失、下游任务性能下降的问题，提出非对称边缘-云协同的结构感知潜扩散（SALD）框架。边缘端将图像解耦为低频载荷与轻量结构先验以减少传输量；云端通过结构门控大核卷积模块和语义引导引擎抑制生成幻觉。在极端带宽约束下，SALD在MSCM和UCMerced数据集上取得了更优的感知质量与下游任务性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 高分辨率遥感数据爆发式增长，但卫星到地面的下行链路带宽有限，导致必须采用极高压缩比压缩，不可逆地破坏了目标检测等下游机器感知任务所需的高频结构细节。现有超分辨率方法中，基于回归的方法产生过度平滑纹理，而生成式扩散模型则经常引入误导检测系统的结构幻觉。需要一种既能节省带宽又能恢复高质量结构细节的方法。

Method: 提出结构感知潜扩散（SALD）框架，一种非对称边缘-云协同超分辨率系统。边缘端将图像解耦为高度压缩的低频载荷和轻量软结构先验，减少传输带宽。云端引入结构门控大核卷积模块（SGLK）和语义引导引擎（SGE），利用传输的结构先验门控大核卷积，捕获航拍场景的长程依赖关系并主动抑制生成幻觉。

Result: 在MSCM和UCMerced数据集上的大量实验表明，即使在极端带宽约束下，SALD在感知质量（LPIPS）上达到更优，并显著提升了场景分类和小目标检测的下游性能。

Conclusion: 提出SALD框架有效解决了遥感图像下传带宽瓶颈与下游感知任务精度之间的权衡问题，通过边缘-云协同和结构感知的扩散模型，在极端压缩条件下仍能保持高质量感知性能。

Original Abstract: The exponential surge in high-resolution remote sensing data faces a severe bottleneck in satellite-to-ground transmission. Limited downlink bandwidth forces the use of extreme high-ratio compression, which irreversibly destroys high-frequency structural details essential for downstream machine perception tasks like object detection. While current super-resolution techniques attempt to recover these details, regression-based methods often yield over-smoothed textures, and generative diffusion models frequently introduce structural hallucinations that mislead detection systems. To address this trade-off, we propose the Structure-Aware Latent Diffusion (SALD) framework, an asymmetric edge-cloud collaborative SR system. At the resource-constrained edge, the system decouples imagery into a highly compressed low-frequency payload and a lightweight soft structural prior. Transmitting this decoupled representation minimizes bandwidth consumption. On the powerful cloud side, we introduce a Structure-Gated Large Kernel (SGLK) module and a Semantic-Guidance Engine (SGE) within the diffusion backbone. These modules leverage the transmitted structural priors to gate large-kernel convolutions, effectively capturing long-range dependencies inherent in aerial scenes while actively suppressing generative hallucinations. Extensive experiments on both the MSCM and UCMerced datasets demonstrate that, even under extreme bandwidth constraints, SALD achieves superior perceptual quality (LPIPS) and significantly enhances downstream performance in both scene classification and small-target detection.

中文摘要翻译: 高分辨率遥感数据的指数级增长面临着卫星到地面传输的严重瓶颈。有限的下行链路带宽迫使使用极高压缩比压缩，这不可逆地破坏了目标检测等下游机器感知任务所必需的高频结构细节。虽然当前超分辨率技术试图恢复这些细节，但基于回归的方法往往产生过度平滑的纹理，而生成式扩散模型则经常引入误导检测系统的结构幻觉。为解决这一权衡问题，我们提出结构感知潜扩散（SALD）框架，一种非对称边缘-云协同的超分辨率系统。在资源受限的边缘端，系统将图像解耦为高度压缩的低频载荷和轻量软结构先验。传输这种解耦表示最大限度地减少了带宽消耗。在强大的云端，我们在扩散主干中引入结构门控大核卷积（SGLK）模块和语义引导引擎（SGE）。这些模块利用传输的结构先验来门控大核卷积，有效捕获航拍场景中固有的长程依赖关系，同时主动抑制生成幻觉。在MSCM和UCMerced数据集上的大量实验表明，即使在极端带宽约束下，SALD也能达到更优的感知质量（LPIPS），并在场景分类和小目标检测中显著提升下游性能。

</details>


### [21] [Assessment of the quantitative impact of occlusal positioning splints on temporomandibular joint conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25322)
*Agnieszka Anna Tomaka,Krzysztof Domino,Dariusz Pojda,Michał Tarnawski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出并验证了一种基于咬合定位牙合垫的颞下颌关节（TMJ）构型定量分析方法，通过多模态数据融合和刚体变换误差分析，利用单一解剖模型评估不同下颌位置的关节空间变化，减少重复影像需求。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 减少评估不同下颌位置时TMJ构型变化所需的重复影像学检查，提供一种间接但可量化的分析手段。

Method: 将定位牙合垫建模为下颌预定义刚体变换的物理实现；融合CBCT、面部运动采集和牙科扫描等多模态数据至统一坐标系；设计并制造对应选定下颌位置的牙合垫；通过石膏模型重复扫描评估定位精度；将误差表示为刚体运动空间中的变换并进行统计分析；将估计变换传播至分割的TMJ结构，实现关节空间变化的仿真评估。

Result: 通过变换误差分析和表面距离度量，量化了计划配置与实际配置之间的差异，验证了该方法的定位精度和可重复性。

Conclusion: 提出的方法能够利用单一解剖模型和变换数据间接评估TMJ构型，减少重复成像需求；本研究为方法论演示，未进行临床验证。

Original Abstract: A computational method for quantitative analysis of temporomandibular joint (TMJ) configuration using occlusal positioning splints is proposed and demonstrated. The method models a positioning splint as a physical realization of a predefined rigid transformation of the mandible, derived from multimodal data, including CBCT, facial motion acquisition, and dental scans integrated within a common coordinate system. Splints corresponding to selected mandibular positions are designed and fabricated, and their positioning accuracy is evaluated using repeated scans of plaster models. Discrepancies are represented as error transformations and analyzed statistically in the space of rigid motions. The estimated transformations are propagated to segmented TMJ structures, enabling simulation-based evaluation of joint space changes. Transformation-based error analysis and surface distance metrics are used to quantify differences between planned and achieved configurations. The method enables indirect assessment of TMJ configuration using a single anatomical model and transformation data, reducing the need for repeated imaging across multiple mandibular positions. This study is intended as a methodological demonstration, supported by a clear step-by-step graphical presentation, and does not aim to provide clinical validation.

中文摘要翻译: 本文提出并验证了一种利用咬合定位牙合板对颞下颌关节（TMJ）构型进行定量分析的计算方法。该方法将定位牙合板建模为下颌骨预定义刚体变换的物理实现，该变换源于多模态数据（包括锥形束CT、面部运动采集和牙科扫描），所有数据均集成于同一坐标系中。设计并制造了对应选定下颌位置的牙合板，并通过石膏模型的重复扫描评估其定位精度。偏差被表示为误差变换，并在刚体运动空间中进行统计分析。估计的变换被传播至分割后的TMJ结构，从而实现对关节空间变化的仿真评估。采用基于变换的误差分析和表面距离度量来量化计划配置与实现配置之间的差异。该方法能够利用单一解剖模型和变换数据间接评估TMJ构型，减少了针对多个下颌位置进行重复成像的需求。本研究旨在作为方法论演示，辅以清晰的逐步图示说明，不提供临床验证。

### [22] [Benchmarking Layout-Guided Diffusion Models through Unified Semantic-Spatial Evaluation in Closed and Open Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25358)
*Luca Parolari,Nicla Faccioli,Lamberto Ballan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了C-Bench和O-Bench两个基准，分别用于受控和开放场景下评估布局引导的文本到图像生成模型，并建立了统一的评估协议，对六种最新模型进行了大规模评估和排名。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基准缺乏对布局引导的文本到图像生成模型的全面评估，标注成本高、规模受限，难以进行有效的模型比较和排名。

Method: 提出C-Bench（闭集基准，控制生成能力与复杂度）和O-Bench（开集基准，使用真实提示和布局），并设计统一的评估协议将语义准确度和空间准确度合并为单一评分。

Result: 对六种最新布局引导扩散模型进行了大规模评估，生成了319,086张图像，建立了模型排名，并提供了文本和布局对齐的详细分解分析。

Original Abstract: Evaluating layout-guided text-to-image generative models requires assessing both semantic alignment with textual prompts and spatial fidelity to prescribed layouts. Assessing layout alignment requires collecting fine-grained annotations, which is costly and labor-intensive. Consequently, current benchmarks rarely provide comprehensive layout evaluation and often remain limited in scale or coverage, making model comparison, ranking, and interpretation difficult. In this work, we introduce a closed-set benchmark (C-Bench) designed to isolate key generative capabilities while providing varying levels of complexity in both prompt structure and layout. To complement this controlled setting, we propose an open-set benchmark (O-Bench) that evaluates models using real-world prompts and layouts, offering a measure of semantic and spatial alignment in the wild. We further develop a unified evaluation protocol that combines semantic and spatial accuracy into a single score, ensuring consistent model ranking. Using our benchmarks, we conduct a large-scale evaluation of six state-of-the-art layout-guided diffusion models, totaling 319,086 generated and evaluated images. We establish a model ranking based on their overall performance and provide detailed breakdowns for text and layout alignment to enhance interpretability. Fine-grained analyses across scenarios and prompt complexities highlight the strengths and limitations of current models. Code is available at https://github.com/lparolari/cobench.

中文摘要翻译: 评估布局引导的文本到图像生成模型需要衡量与文本提示的语义对齐以及指定布局的空间保真度。评估布局对齐需要收集细粒度的标注，这既昂贵又劳动密集。因此，当前的基准很少提供全面的布局评估，通常规模或覆盖范围有限，使得模型比较、排名和解释变得困难。在这项工作中，我们引入了一个闭集基准（C-Bench），旨在隔离关键的生成能力，同时在提示结构和布局方面提供不同层次的复杂度。为了补充这种受控设置，我们提出了一个开集基准（O-Bench），使用真实世界的提示和布局来评估模型，提供了自然场景中语义和空间对齐的度量。我们进一步开发了一个统一的评估协议，将语义准确度和空间准确度合并为单一评分，确保一致的模型排名。使用我们的基准，我们对六种最先进的布局引导扩散模型进行了大规模评估，共生成和评估了319,086张图像。我们基于整体性能建立了模型排名，并提供了文本和布局对齐的详细分解以增强可解释性。跨场景和提示复杂度的细粒度分析突显了当前模型的优势和局限。代码可在 https://github.com/lparolari/cobench 获取。

### [23] [HuM-Eval: A Coarse-to-Fine Framework for Human-Centric Video Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25361)
*Bingzi Zhang,Kaisi Guan,Ruihua Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HuM-Eval是一个面向生成人体运动视频的人类中心评估框架，采用从粗到细的策略，通过VLM进行全局质量评估，再结合2D姿态和3D运动进行细粒度分析，平均人类相关性达58.2%，优于现有方法。同时提出了包含1000个多样化提示的基准HuM-Bench。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有评估指标主要关注全局场景统计，忽视细粒度的人体细节，无法与人类主观偏好对齐，因此亟需一个能够准确评估生成人体运动视频质量的人类中心评估框架。

Method: 采用从粗到细的两阶段策略：首先利用视觉语言模型（VLM）对视频全局质量进行粗略评估；然后进行细粒度分析，使用2D姿态验证解剖学正确性，并使用3D人体运动评估运动稳定性。

Result: HuM-Eval的平均人类相关性达到58.2%，超越了当前最先进的基线方法。此外，构建了包含1000个多样化提示的综合基准HuM-Bench，并对现有文本到视频模型进行了详细评估。

Conclusion: HuM-Eval作为一个人类中心的评估框架，有效弥补了现有指标在细粒度人体细节评估上的不足，为下一代人体运动生成技术的发展提供了评估基础。

Original Abstract: Video generation models have developed rapidly in recent years, where generating natural human motion plays a pivotal role. However, accurately evaluating the quality of generated human motion video remains a significant challenge. Existing evaluation metrics primarily focus on global scene statistics, often overlooking fine-grained human details and consequently failing to align with human subjective preference. To bridge this gap, we propose HuM-Eval, a novel human-centric evaluation framework that adopts a coarse-to-fine strategy. Specifically, our framework first utilizes a Vision Language Model to perform a coarse assessment of global video quality. It then proceeds to a fine-grained analysis, using 2D pose to verify anatomical correctness and 3D human motion to evaluate motion stability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that HuM-Eval achieves an average human correlation of 58.2%, outperforming state-of-the-art baselines. Furthermore, we introduce HuM-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark comprising 1,000 diverse prompts, and conduct a detailed evaluation of existing text-to-video models, paving the way for next-generation human motion generation.

中文摘要翻译: 近年来，视频生成模型发展迅速，其中生成自然的人体运动扮演着关键角色。然而，准确评估生成人体运动视频的质量仍然是一个重大挑战。现有的评估指标主要关注全局场景统计，往往忽视细粒度的人体细节，因此无法与人类主观偏好对齐。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出HuM-Eval，一个新颖的人类中心评估框架，采用从粗到细的策略。具体而言，我们的框架首先利用视觉语言模型对视频全局质量进行粗略评估；然后进行细粒度分析，使用2D姿态验证解剖学正确性，并使用3D人体运动评估运动稳定性。大量实验表明，HuM-Eval的平均人类相关性达到58.2%，超越了当前最先进的基线方法。此外，我们引入了HuM-Bench，一个包含1000个多样化提示的综合基准，并对现有文本到视频模型进行了详细评估，为下一代人体运动生成铺平了道路。

### [24] [GPT-Image-2 in the Wild: A Twitter Dataset of Self-Reported AI-Generated Images from the First Week of Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25370)
*Kidus Zewde,Simiao Ren,Xingyu Shen,Jenny Wu,Yuchen Zhou,Tommy Duong,Zikang Zhang,Ethan Traister*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出了GPT-Image-2 Twitter数据集——首个公开的GPT-image-2生成图像数据集，包含从Twitter/X采集的10,217张确认图像，并分析了其视觉特征（内容分类、OCR文本、人脸检测、语义聚类），同时发现C2PA内容凭证在上传过程中被Twitter CDN系统性剥离，导致加密溯源不可行。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: GPT-image-2的发布使得AI生成图像与真实照片的界限变得极其模糊，但目前缺乏公开的GPT-image-2生成图像数据集来支撑相关研究（如检测、溯源、社会影响分析）。作者旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过Twitter API v2采集2026年4月21日发布后六天内的27,662条记录；采用多阶段筛选流程：多语言文本启发式筛选（英、日、中）、浏览器自动化验证Twitter“Made with AI”徽章、模型名称变体匹配；最终确认10,217张GPT-image-2图像。随后进行四项分析：CLIP零样本主题分类、OCR文本可读性检测、人脸检测、语义聚类（CLIP ViT-L/14）。

Result: 1) 从27,662条记录中筛选出10,217张确认图像；2) 82.0%的图像包含可检测文本；3) 59.2%的图像检测到人脸，共22,583张人脸；4) CLIP ViT-L/14聚类得到137个语义簇；5) 关键负结果：C2PA内容凭证在上传至Twitter时被CDN系统性移除，加密溯源对社交媒体来源的AI图像不可行。

Conclusion: GPT-Image-2 Twitter数据集为AI生成图像研究提供了首个规模化公开资源；C2PA凭证被社交媒体平台剥离的问题对AI内容溯源提出了严峻挑战，需探索替代的验证与检测方法。

Original Abstract: The release of GPT-image-2 by OpenAI marks a watershed moment in AI-generated imagery: the boundary between photographic reality and synthetic content has never been more difficult to discern. We introduce the GPT-Image-2 Twitter Dataset, the first published dataset of GPT-image-2 generated images, sourced from publicly available Twitter/X posts in the immediate aftermath of the model's April 21, 2026 release. Leveraging the Twitter API v2 and a multi-stage curation pipeline spanning multilingual text heuristics (English, Japanese, and Chinese), browser-automated Twitter "Made with AI" badge verification, and model name variant matching, we curate 10,217 confirmed GPT-image-2 images from 27,662 collected records over a six-day window.
  We characterize the dataset across four analyses: CLIP-based zero-shot subject taxonomy, OCR text legibility (82.0% of images contain detectable text), face detection (59.2% of images, 22,583 total faces), and semantic clustering (137 CLIP ViT-L/14 clusters).
  A key negative result is that C2PA content credentials are systematically stripped by Twitter's CDN on upload, rendering cryptographic provenance verification infeasible for social-media-sourced AI images. The dataset and all curation code are released publicly.

中文摘要翻译: OpenAI 发布的 GPT-image-2 标志着 AI 生成图像领域的一个分水岭：摄影真实与合成内容之间的界限从未如此难以分辨。我们提出了 GPT-Image-2 Twitter 数据集，这是首个公开的 GPT-image-2 生成图像数据集，来源于该模型于 2026 年 4 月 21 日发布后立即在公开 Twitter/X 平台上发布的帖子。利用 Twitter API v2 以及一个涵盖多语言文本启发式筛选（英语、日语和中文）、浏览器自动化的 Twitter“Made with AI”徽章验证以及模型名称变体匹配的多阶段筛选流程，我们在六天窗口期内从 27,662 条采集记录中筛选出 10,217 张确认为 GPT-image-2 的图像。我们通过四项分析来刻画该数据集：基于 CLIP 的零样本主题分类、OCR 文本可读性（82.0% 的图像包含可检测文本）、人脸检测（59.2% 的图像，共 22,583 张人脸）以及语义聚类（137 个 CLIP ViT-L/14 聚类）。一个关键的负结果是，C2PA 内容凭证在上传时被 Twitter 的 CDN 系统性剥离，导致对于社交媒体来源的 AI 图像，加密溯源证明不可行。该数据集及所有筛选代码均已公开发布。

### [25] [CoRE: Concept-Reasoning Expansion for Continual Brain Lesion Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25376)
*Qianqian Chen,Anglin Liu,Jingyang Zhang,Yudong Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出概念推理扩展（CoRE）框架，通过将视觉特征与结构化概念对齐来模拟临床推理，指导动态模型扩展，在12项顺序脑病变MRI任务上实现SOTA性能，同时提高可解释性和知识复用效率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有持续学习范式存在容量限制或参数冗余增长问题，且动态方法多依赖图像感知策略，难以处理脑成像中显著的病理异质性和多模态异质性。

Method: CoRE框架建立联合决策机制，将图像token与层次化概念库对齐以模拟临床推理，实现可解释的专家路由和基于需求的自适应模型增长，在临床先验指导下进行模型演化，避免冗余参数扩展并最大化知识复用。

Result: 在12项顺序脑病变MRI任务上的全面评估表明，CoRE达到SOTA性能，提供了高效未来适应的高知识起点，并展现出优越的小样本迁移能力和临床可解释性。

Conclusion: CoRE框架通过概念驱动的动态增长机制有效管理非平稳临床数据流，为脑病变分割的持续学习提供了兼具高性能和临床可解释性的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Accurate brain lesion segmentation in MRI is vital for effective clinical diagnosis and treatment planning. Due to high annotation costs and strict data privacy regulations, universal models require employing Continual Learning (CL) to adapt to evolving clinical tasks without losing previously acquired knowledge. However, existing CL paradigms often suffer from capacity limits or redundant parameter growth, and even advanced dynamic methods rely mostly on image-perception strategies that struggle to handle the substantial pathological and multimodal heterogeneity inherent in brain imaging. To address this issue, we propose Concept-Reasoning Expansion (CoRE) framework, which establishes a joint decision-making mechanism by integrating visual features with structured concepts. Through the alignment of image tokens with a hierarchical concept library, CoRE simulates clinical reasoning to guide both interpretable expert routing and demand-based model growth. This collaborative process ensures model evolution is grounded in clinical priors, preventing redundant parameter expansion while maximizing knowledge reuse. Extensive evaluations across 12 sequential brain lesion MRI tasks demonstrate that CoRE achieves state-of-the-art performance and provides a high knowledge starting point for efficient future adaptation. Its superior few-shot transferability and clinical interpretability further validate its effectiveness in managing non-stationary clinical data streams. Our code will be released soon.

中文摘要翻译: 脑部MRI中的精确病灶分割对于有效的临床诊断和治疗规划至关重要。由于高昂的标注成本和严格的数据隐私法规，通用模型需要采用持续学习（CL）来适应不断变化的临床任务，同时不遗忘先前获得的知识。然而，现有的CL范式常常面临容量限制或参数冗余增长的问题，即使先进的动态方法也多依赖于图像感知策略，难以处理脑成像中固有的显著病理异质性和多模态异质性。为解决这一问题，我们提出了概念推理扩展（CoRE）框架，该框架通过将视觉特征与结构化概念相整合，建立了一种联合决策机制。通过将图像token与层次化概念库对齐，CoRE模拟临床推理过程，以指导可解释的专家路由和基于需求的模型增长。这一协作过程确保模型演化以临床先验知识为基础，在最大化知识复用的同时防止冗余参数扩展。在12项顺序脑病变MRI任务上的广泛评估表明，CoRE达到了最先进的性能，并为高效的未来自适应提供了高知识起点。其卓越的小样本迁移能力和临床可解释性进一步验证了其在管理非平稳临床数据流方面的有效性。我们的代码将很快发布。

### [26] [Benchmarking and Improving GUI Agents in High-Dynamic Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25380)
*Enqi Liu,Liyuan Pan,Zhi Gao,Yan Yang,Chenrui Shi,Yang Liu,Jingrong Wu,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对GUI智能体在高动态环境中的部分可观测问题，提出了动态GUI基准DynamicGUIBench和动态界面智能体DynamicUI，该智能体以屏幕录制视频为输入，通过动态感知器、精炼策略和反思模块提升在动态环境中的决策性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有GUI智能体依赖操作后单张截图进行决策，导致在高动态GUI环境中面临部分可观测（甚至不可观测）马尔可夫决策过程问题，关键界面状态信息无法被充分捕获，这一问题尚未被系统探索。

Method: 提出DynamicUI智能体，以交互过程的屏幕录制视频为输入，包含三个组件：(1) 动态感知器：对GUI视频帧进行聚类、生成质心描述，并迭代选取最具信息量的帧作为显著动态上下文；(2) 精炼策略：采用动作条件过滤机制，消除所选帧与智能体文本上下文之间的不一致性和噪声，缓解思想-动作不一致与冗余问题；(3) 反思模块：基于精炼后的智能体轨迹，为后续动作提供有效准确的引导。

Result: 在提出的DynamicGUIBench基准上，DynamicUI在动态GUI环境中性能显著提升，同时在其他公开基准上保持有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 动态GUI环境中的部分可观测问题可以通过以视频作为输入并设计动态感知、精炼与反思组件来有效缓解，该方法在动态场景下表现优异且不损失通用场景的竞争力。

Original Abstract: Recent advancements in Graphical User Interface (GUI) agents have predominantly focused on training paradigms like supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). However, the challenge of high-dynamic GUI environments remains largely underexplored. Existing agents typically rely on a single screenshot after each action for decision-making, leading to a partially observable (or even unobservable) Markov decision process, where the key GUI state including important information for actions is often inadequately captured. To systematically explore this challenge, we introduce DynamicGUIBench, a comprehensive online GUI benchmark spanning ten applications and diverse interaction scenarios characterized by important interface changes between actions. Furthermore, we present DynamicUI, an agent designed for dynamic interfaces, which takes screen-recording videos of the interaction process as input and consists of three components: a dynamic perceiver, a refinement strategy, and a reflection. Specifically, the dynamic perceiver clusters frames of the GUI video, generates captions for the centroids, and iteratively selects the most informative frames as the salient dynamic context. Considering that there may be inconsistencies and noise between the selected frames and the textual context of the agent, the refinement strategy employs an action-conditioned filtering to refine thoughts to mitigate thought-action inconsistency and redundancy. Based on the refined agent trajectories, the reflection module provides effective and accurate guidance for further actions. Experiments on DynamicGUIBench demonstrate that DynamicUI significantly improves the performance in dynamic GUI environments, while maintaining competitive performance on other public benchmarks.

中文摘要翻译: 近期图形用户界面（GUI）智能体的研究进展主要集中在监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）等训练范式上。然而，高动态GUI环境的挑战在很大程度上仍未得到充分探索。现有智能体通常依赖每次操作后的单张截图进行决策，这导致了一个部分可观测（甚至不可观测）的马尔可夫决策过程，其中包含操作所需关键信息的重要GUI状态往往无法被充分捕获。为了系统性地探索这一挑战，我们引入了DynamicGUIBench，一个涵盖十个应用及多种交互场景的综合性在线GUI基准测试，其特点是操作间存在重要的界面变化。此外，我们提出了DynamicUI，一种专为动态界面设计的智能体，它以交互过程的屏幕录制视频作为输入，由三个组件构成：动态感知器、精炼策略和反思模块。具体而言，动态感知器对GUI视频帧进行聚类，为聚类质心生成描述，并迭代地选取信息量最丰富的帧作为显著的动态上下文。考虑到所选帧与智能体文本上下文之间可能存在不一致性和噪声，精炼策略采用动作条件过滤机制来精炼思维，以缓解思想-动作不一致与冗余问题。基于精炼后的智能体轨迹，反思模块为后续动作提供有效且准确的引导。在DynamicGUIBench上的实验表明，DynamicUI在动态GUI环境中显著提升了性能，同时在其它公开基准上保持了有竞争力的表现。

### [27] [COMPASS: COmpact Multi-channel Prior-map And Scene Signature for Floor-Plan-Based Visual Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25388)
*Muhammad Shaheer,Miguel Fernandez-Cortizas,Asier Bikandi-Noya,Holger Voos,Jose Luis Sanchez-Lopez*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: COMPASS利用建筑平面图中的几何与语义先验（墙壁、窗户、开口），通过多通道径向描述符实现双鱼眼相机机器人的跨模态定位，并在Hilti-Trimble SLAM Challenge 2026数据集上验证了可行性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有定位方法大多忽略建筑平面图中丰富的语义信息（如墙壁、窗户等），仅利用几何信息，导致跨模态定位精度受限。

Method: 设计多通道径向描述符，从平面图通过360度射线投射编码五通道信息（归一化距离、结构命中类型、距离梯度、逆距离、局部距离方差）；从鱼眼图像中检测结构元素（提出基于线段检测和垂直边缘聚类的窗户检测算法），生成相同结构的视觉描述符，实现跨模态匹配。

Result: 在Hilti-Trimble SLAM Challenge 2026数据集上，从单个已知位姿生成两种描述符，鱼眼图像提取的墙壁-窗户模式与平面图描述符高度吻合，验证了跨模态结构匹配的可行性。

Conclusion: 融合几何与语义先验的跨模态描述符可以有效地从鱼眼图像中匹配建筑平面图，为全跨模态定位提供了可行方案。

Original Abstract: Architectural floor plans are widely available priors which contain not only geometry but also the semantic information of the environment, yet existing localization methods largely ignore this semantic information. To address this, we present COMPASS, an algorithm that exploits both geometric and semantic priors from floor plans to estimate the pose of a robot equipped with dual fisheye cameras. Inspired by scan context descriptor from LiDAR-based place recognition, we design a multi-channel radial descriptor that encodes the geometric layout surrounding a position. From the floor plan, rays are cast in 360 azimuth bins and the results are encoded into five channels: normalized range, structural hit type (wall, window, or opening), range gradient, inverse range, and local range variance. From the image side, the same descriptor structure is populated by detecting structural elements in the fisheye imagery. As a first step toward full cross-modal matching, we present a window detection algorithm for fisheye images that uses a line segment detector to identify window frames via vertical edge clustering and brightness verification. Detected windows are projected to azimuthal bearings through the fisheye camera model, producing the hit-type channel of the visual descriptor. As a proof of concept, we generate both descriptors at a single known pose from the Hilti-Trimble SLAM Challenge 2026 dataset and demonstrate that the wall-window pattern extracted from the first frame of each camera closely matches the floor plan descriptor, validating the feasibility of cross-modal structural matching.

中文摘要翻译: 建筑平面图是广泛可用的先验信息，不仅包含环境的几何结构，还包含语义信息，然而现有的定位方法大多忽略了这些语义信息。为解决这一问题，我们提出了COMPASS算法，该算法利用平面图中的几何和语义先验来估计配备双鱼眼相机的机器人的位姿。受基于激光雷达场景识别的扫描上下文描述符启发，我们设计了一种多通道径向描述符，用于编码某个位置周围的几何布局。从平面图出发，在360个方位角区间内投射射线，并将结果编码为五个通道：归一化距离、结构命中类型（墙壁、窗户或开口）、距离梯度、逆距离和局部距离方差。在图像方面，通过检测鱼眼图像中的结构元素来填充相同的描述符结构。作为迈向全跨模态匹配的第一步，我们提出了一种针对鱼眼图像的窗户检测算法，该算法使用线段检测器通过垂直边缘聚类和亮度验证来识别窗户框架。检测到的窗户通过鱼眼相机模型投影到方位角方向，生成视觉描述符的命中类型通道。作为概念验证，我们从Hilti-Trimble SLAM Challenge 2026数据集中的一个已知位姿生成两种描述符，并证明从每个相机的第一帧提取的墙壁-窗户模式与平面图描述符高度吻合，验证了跨模态结构匹配的可行性。

### [28] [Beyond Fidelity: Semantic Similarity Assessment in Low-Level Image Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25408)
*Runjie Wang,Weiling Chen,Tiesong Zhao,Chang Wen Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向低层图像处理的语义相似性评估任务，并设计了基于三元组的语义相似性分数（T3S），通过前景实体、背景实体及其关系建模图像语义，弥补了传统图像质量评估在语义层面上的不足。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 随着深度学习和生成模型的发展，处理后的图像可能在保持感知质量的同时改变语义内容，传统基于视觉保真度的图像质量评估（IQA）不足以评估语义层面的变化，因此需要一种新的语义级评估指标。

Method: 提出三元组语义相似性分数（T3S），通过语义实体提取、前景-背景解耦以及开放世界类别/关系建模，将图像语义建模为前景实体、背景实体和关系三元组，从而评估处理前后图像的语义相似性。

Result: 在COCO和SPA-Data数据集上，T3S持续优于现有的保真度导向指标和代表性语义级基线，并能更好地反映多种退化条件下渐进式语义变化。

Conclusion: 语义评估在现代低层视觉任务中具有重要价值，T3S作为新的语义相似性度量标准能够有效弥补传统IQA的不足。

Original Abstract: Low-level image processing has long been evaluated mainly from the perspective of visual fidelity. However, with the rise of deep learning and generative models, processed images may preserve perceptual quality while altering semantic content, making conventional Image Quality Assessment (IQA) insufficient for semantic-level assessment. In this paper, we formalize \textit{Semantic Similarity} as a new evaluation task for low-level image processing, aimed at measuring whether semantic content is preserved after processing. We further present a structured formulation of image semantics based on semantic entities and their relations, and discuss the desired properties and constraints of a valid semantic similarity index. Based on this formulation, we propose Triplet-based Semantic Similarity Score (T3S), which models image semantics through foreground entities, background entities, and relations. T3S combines semantic entity extraction, foreground-background disentanglement, and open-world class/relation modeling. Experiments on COCO and SPA-Data show that T3S consistently outperforms existing fidelity-oriented metrics and representative semantic-level baselines, while better reflecting progressive semantic changes under diverse degradations. These results highlight the importance of semantic assessment in modern low-level vision.

中文摘要翻译: 低层图像处理长期以来主要从视觉保真度的角度进行评估。然而，随着深度学习和生成模型的兴起，处理后的图像可能在保持感知质量的同时改变语义内容，这使得传统的图像质量评估（IQA）不足以进行语义层面的评估。在本文中，我们将语义相似性形式化为低层图像处理的一项新评估任务，旨在衡量处理后语义内容是否得到保留。我们进一步提出了一种基于语义实体及其关系的图像语义结构化表述，并讨论了有效语义相似性指数应具备的期望属性和约束条件。基于该表述，我们提出了三元组语义相似性分数（T3S），通过前景实体、背景实体和关系对图像语义进行建模。T3S结合了语义实体提取、前景-背景解耦以及开放世界类别/关系建模。在COCO和SPA-Data上的实验表明，T3S持续优于现有的保真度导向指标和代表性语义级基线，同时能更好地反映多种退化条件下渐进式的语义变化。这些结果突显了语义评估在现代低层视觉中的重要性。
