### [29] [A Systematic Post-Train Framework for Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25427)
*Zeyue Xue,Siming Fu,Jie Huang,Shuai Lu,Haoran Li,Yijun Liu,Yuming Li,Xiaoxuan He,Mengzhao Chen,Haoyang Huang,Nan Duan,Ping Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向视频扩散模型的统一后训练框架，通过监督微调、基于GRPO的强化学习、提示增强和推理优化四个阶段，系统性地提升模型在指令遵循、视觉质量、时间一致性和推理效率方面的表现，弥合预训练模型与真实部署之间的差距。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有大规模视频扩散模型虽能生成高分辨率、语义丰富的内容，但在实际部署中存在提示敏感性、时间不一致性以及推理成本过高等关键问题，预训练性能与现实需求之间存在显著差距。

Method: 提出一个包含四个协同阶段的统一后训练框架：(1) 监督微调 (SFT)，将基模型转化为稳定的指令遵循策略；(2) 基于人类反馈的强化学习 (RLHF)，采用专为视频扩散定制的分组相对策略优化 (GRPO) 提升感知质量和时间连贯性；(3) 通过专用语言模型进行提示增强，优化用户输入；(4) 推理优化，提升系统效率。

Result: 大量实验表明，该统一流水线有效减轻了常见伪影，在严格遵守采样成本约束的条件下，显著提升了可控性和视觉美感。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种构建可扩展、稳定、适应性强且实际部署有效的后训练流水线的实用方案，能够在保持预训练所得可控性的同时，系统性地提升视觉质量、时间连贯性和指令遵循能力。

Original Abstract: While large-scale video diffusion models have demonstrated impressive capabilities in generating high-resolution and semantically rich content, a significant gap remains between their pretraining performance and real-world deployment requirements due to critical issues such as prompt sensitivity, temporal inconsistency, and prohibitive inference costs. To bridge this gap, we propose a comprehensive post-training framework that systematically aligns pretrained models with user intentions through four synergistic stages: we first employ Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) to transform the base model into a stable instruction-following policy, followed by a Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) stage that utilizes a novel Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) method tailored for video diffusion to enhance perceptual quality and temporal coherence; subsequently, we integrate Prompt Enhancement via a specialized language model to refine user inputs, and finally address system efficiency through Inference Optimization. Together, these components provide a systematic approach to improving visual quality, temporal coherence, and instruction following, while preserving the controllability learned during pretraining. The result is a practical blueprint for building scalable post-training pipelines that are stable, adaptable, and effective in real-world deployment. Extensive experiments demonstrate that this unified pipeline effectively mitigates common artifacts and significantly improves controllability and visual aesthetics while adhering to strict sampling cost constraints.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管大规模视频扩散模型在生成高分辨率和语义丰富的内容方面展现了令人印象深刻的能力，但由于提示敏感性、时间不一致性以及高昂的推理成本等关键问题，其预训练性能与现实部署需求之间仍存在显著差距。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了一种全面的后训练框架，通过四个协同阶段系统性地将预训练模型与用户意图对齐：首先，我们采用监督微调将基模型转化为稳定的指令遵循策略；随后，引入基于人类反馈的强化学习阶段，利用一种专为视频扩散定制的新型分组相对策略优化方法来提升感知质量和时间连贯性；接着，我们通过专用语言模型集成提示增强模块以优化用户输入；最后，通过推理优化解决系统效率问题。这些组件共同提供了一种系统化的方法，在保持预训练所习得可控性的同时，提升视觉质量、时间连贯性和指令遵循能力。其结果是为构建可扩展、稳定、适应性强且在实际部署中有效的后训练流水线提供了一份实用蓝图。大量实验表明，该统一流水线有效减轻了常见伪影，并在严格遵守采样成本约束的条件下显著提升了可控性和视觉美感。

### [30] [SARU: A Shadow-Aware and Removal Unified Framework for Remote Sensing Images with New Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25432)
*Zi-Yang Bo,Wei Lu,Hongruixuan Chen,Si-Bao Chen,Bin Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 SARU 框架，将阴影检测与去除统一为两阶段流程，通过无需训练的非遮挡区域物理算法实现单图像阴影去除，并引入两个新基准数据集，在公共和自建数据集上达到最优性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有遥感影像阴影处理方法将检测与去除分离为级联任务，流程繁琐且易产生误差累积；同时大多数深度学习方法依赖成对的阴影/非阴影训练图像，实际场景中难以获取。

Method: 提出 SARU 两阶段框架：第一阶段使用双分支检测模块 DBCSF-Net，融合多色彩空间与语义特征生成高保真阴影掩膜；第二阶段提出无需训练的无遮挡区域物理算法 N$^2$SGSR，通过从输入图像中相邻非阴影区域转移光照属性来恢复照度。

Result: 在公共 AISD 数据集及新构建的 RSISD 和 SiSRB 基准数据集上，SARU 达到最先进性能水平。

Conclusion: SARU 通过整体式集成阴影检测与去除减轻误差传播，并消除对成对训练数据的依赖，为真实遥感影像分析建立了鲁棒且实用的框架。

Original Abstract: Shadows are a prevalent problem in remote sensing imagery (RSI), degrading visual quality and severely limiting the performance of downstream tasks like object detection and semantic segmentation. Most prior works treat shadow detection and removal as separate, cascaded tasks, which can lead to cumbersome process and error accumulation. Furthermore, many deep learning methods rely on paired shadow and non-shadow images for training, which are often unavailable in practice. To address these challenges, we propose Shadow-Aware and Removal Unified (SARU) Framework , a cohesive two-stage framework. First, its dual-branch detection module (DBCSF-Net) fuses multi-color space and semantic features to generate high-fidelity shadow masks, effectively distinguishing shadows from dark objects. Then, leveraging these masks, a novel, training-free physical algorithm (N$^2$SGSR) restores illumination by transferring properties from adjacent non-shadow regions within the single input image. To facilitate rigorous evaluation and foster future work, we also introduce two new benchmark datasets: the RSI Shadow Detection (RSISD) dataset and the Single-image Shadow Removal Benchmark (SiSRB). Extensive experiments demonstrate that SARU achieves state-of-the-art performance on both the public AISD dataset and our newly introduced benchmarks. By holistically integrating shadow detection and removal to mitigate error propagation and eliminating the dependency on paired training data, SARU establishes a robust, practical framework for real-world RSI analysis. The source code and datasets are publicly available at: https://github.com/AeroVILab-AHU/SARU-Framework.

中文摘要翻译: 阴影是遥感影像中普遍存在的问题，它会降低视觉质量，并严重限制目标检测和语义分割等下游任务的性能。以往的大多数工作将阴影检测和去除视为独立的级联任务，这可能导致流程繁琐和误差累积。此外，许多深度学习方法依赖于成对的阴影和非阴影图像进行训练，而这些图像在实际中往往难以获取。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了阴影感知与去除统一（SARU）框架，这是一个紧凑的两阶段框架。首先，其双分支检测模块（DBCSF-Net）融合多色彩空间和语义特征，生成高保真阴影掩膜，有效区分阴影与暗色物体。然后，利用这些掩膜，一种新颖的、无需训练的物理算法（N$^2$SGSR）通过从单幅输入图像中的相邻非阴影区域转移光照属性来恢复照度。为了促进严格评估并推动未来工作，我们还引入了两个新的基准数据集：RSI 阴影检测（RSISD）数据集和单图像阴影去除基准（SiSRB）。大量实验表明，SARU 在公共 AISD 数据集和我们新引入的基准数据集上均达到了最先进的性能。通过整体式集成阴影检测与去除以减轻误差传播，并消除对成对训练数据的依赖，SARU 为真实世界的遥感影像分析建立了一个鲁棒且实用的框架。源代码和数据集已在 https://github.com/AeroVILab-AHU/SARU-Framework 公开。

</details>


### [31] [GramSR: Visual Feature Conditioning for Diffusion-Based Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25457)
*Fabio D'Oronzio,Federico Putamorsi,Leonardo Zini,Marcella Cornia,Lorenzo Baraldi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出GramSR，一种基于一步式扩散模型的单图像超分辨率方法，通过使用DINOv3提取的密集视觉特征替代文本条件，并采用三阶段LoRA架构（像素级、语义级、纹理级）来弥合语义抽象与视觉细节之间的表示差距，在标准SR基准上优于现有一步式扩散方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于扩散模型的超分辨率方法依赖文本条件（语义描述），但文本仅提供高层语义，缺乏空间对齐的视觉细节信息，导致抽象语义与视觉细节之间存在表示差距，影响图像保真度重建。

Method: GramSR采用一步式扩散框架，使用预训练DINOv3编码器从低分辨率输入中提取密集视觉特征替代传统文本条件；采用三阶段LoRA架构：像素级LoRA（ℓ2损失，去除退化）、语义级LoRA（LPIPS和CSD损失，增强感知细节）、纹理级LoRA（基于DINOv3特征的Gram矩阵损失，保持纹理一致性）；推理时使用独立引导尺度灵活控制各阶段效果。

Result: 在标准超分辨率基准上的大量实验表明，GramSR在结构保真度和纹理真实感方面持续优于现有的一步式扩散超分辨率方法。

Conclusion: 通过密集视觉特征替代文本条件，并结合三阶段LoRA分步优化的方式，GramSR有效弥合了语义与视觉细节之间的表示差距，实现了更优的超分辨率重建效果。

Original Abstract: Despite recent advances, single-image super-resolution (SR) remains challenging, especially in real-world scenarios with complex degradations. Diffusion-based SR methods, particularly those built on Stable Diffusion, leverage strong generative priors but commonly rely on text conditioning derived from semantic captioning. Such textual descriptions provide only high-level semantics and lack the spatially aligned visual information required for faithful restoration, leading to a representation gap between abstract semantics and spatially aligned visual details. To address this limitation, we propose GramSR, a one-step diffusion-based SR framework that replaces text conditioning with dense visual features extracted from the low-resolution input using a pre-trained DINOv3 encoder. GramSR adopts a three-stage LoRA architecture, where pixel-level, semantic-level, and texture-level LoRA modules are trained sequentially. The pixel-level module focuses on degradation removal using $\ell_2$ loss, the semantic-level module enhances perceptual details via LPIPS and CSD losses, and the texture-level module enforces feature correlation consistency through a Gram matrix loss computed from DINOv3 features. At inference, independent guidance scales enable flexible control over degradation removal, semantic enhancement, and texture preservation. Extensive experiments on standard SR benchmarks demonstrate that GramSR consistently outperforms existing one-step diffusion-based methods, achieving superior structural fidelity and texture realism. The code for this work is available at: https://github.com/aimagelab/GramSR.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管近期取得了进展，单图像超分辨率在现实世界中存在复杂退化的场景下仍然具有挑战性。基于扩散的超分辨率方法，特别是那些建立在Stable Diffusion之上的方法，利用强大的生成先验，但通常依赖于从语义描述中获得的文本条件。这类文本描述仅提供高层级语义，缺乏空间对齐的视觉信息以进行保真重建，导致抽象语义与空间对齐的视觉细节之间存在表示差距。为解决这一局限，我们提出了GramSR，一种一步式扩散超分辨率框架，该框架使用预训练的DINOv3编码器从低分辨率输入中提取的密集视觉特征替代文本条件。GramSR采用三阶段LoRA架构，依次训练像素级、语义级和纹理级LoRA模块。像素级模块使用ℓ₂损失专注于退化去除，语义级模块通过LPIPS和CSD损失增强感知细节，纹理级模块通过基于DINOv3特征计算的Gram矩阵损失强制特征相关性一致性。在推理时，独立的引导尺度能够灵活控制退化去除、语义增强和纹理保持。在标准超分辨率基准上的大量实验表明，GramSR持续优于现有的一步式扩散方法，实现了卓越的结构保真度和纹理真实感。本工作的代码可在以下地址获取：https://github.com/aimagelab/GramSR。

</details>


### [32] [Image Compression with Bubble-Aware Frame Rate Adaptation for Energy-Efficient Video Capsule Endoscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25464)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 视频胶囊内窥镜尺寸受限导致电池寿命短，而图像采集和传输能耗高，两者之间存在根本性矛盾，亟需在保持诊断图像质量的前提下减少传输数据量和能耗。

Method: 提出了一种图像压缩流水线，利用压缩过程特征识别主要由气泡导致的低诊断价值帧，无需额外图像分析；并针对低可视性帧设计了动态气泡感知帧率自适应策略，在低可视阶段减少图像采集和传输。

Result: 在RISC-V平台上使用Kvasir-Capsule和Galar数据集评估：压缩比达5.748（82.6%），PSNR为40.3 dB；系统平均能耗降低20.58%；气泡感知帧率自适应使能耗降低最高达40%。

Original Abstract: Video Capsule Endoscopy (VCE) is a promising method for improving the medical examination of the small intestine in the gastrointestinal tract. A key challenge is their limited size, resulting in a short battery lifetime which conflicts with high energy consumption for image capturing and transmission to an on-body device. Thus, we propose an image compression pipeline that substantially reduces the transmitted data while preserving diagnostic image quality. Furthermore, we exploit characteristics of the compression process to identify frames with low diagnostic value mainly caused by bubbles, without requiring additional image analysis. For low-visibility frames, a dynamic bubble-aware frame rate adaptation strategy reduces image acquisition and transmission during these phases while preserving sensitivity to potential anomalies. The compression method achieves a compression ratio of 5.748 (82.6%) at a peak signal-to-noise ratio of 40.3 dB, indicating negligible loss of visual quality. These results demonstrate the potential of our method to increase the applicability of VCE.

中文摘要翻译: 视频胶囊内窥镜（VCE）是一种用于改善胃肠道中小肠医学检查的有前景的方法。一个关键挑战是其有限的尺寸导致电池寿命短，这与图像采集和向体外设备传输的高能耗相冲突。因此，我们提出了一种图像压缩流水线，能够在保持诊断图像质量的同时大幅减少传输数据量。此外，我们利用压缩过程的特征来识别主要由气泡导致的低诊断价值帧，而无需额外的图像分析。对于低可视性帧，一种动态气泡感知帧率自适应策略可减少这些阶段的图像采集和传输，同时保持对潜在异常的敏感度。所提出的压缩和帧率自适应方法在基于RISC-V的平台上使用Kvasir-Capsule和Galar数据集进行评估。该压缩方法在峰值信噪比为40.3 dB时实现了5.748（82.6%）的压缩比，表明视觉质量损失可忽略不计。压缩使整个系统的平均能耗降低了20.58%。此外，所提出的气泡感知帧率自适应方法将能耗降低高达40%。这些结果证明了我们的方法在提高VCE应用可行性方面的潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先从每个视角编码潜在嵌入，通过预测的深度图将其反投影到共享3D空间；然后基于跨视图注意力机制，对属于同一身体部位的特征进行重新校准，解决空间模糊性，实现3D高斯的精确定位。

Original Abstract: Recently, generalizable human Gaussian splatting from sparse-view inputs has been actively studied for the photorealistic human rendering. Most existing methods rely on explicit geometric constraints or predefined structural representations to accurately position 3D Gaussians. Although these approaches have shown the remarkable progress in this field, they still suffer from inconsistent feature representations across multi-view inputs due to complex articulations of the human body and limited overlaps between different views. To address this problem, we propose a novel method to accurately localize 3D Gaussians and ultimately improve the quality of human rendering. The key idea is to unproject latent embeddings encoded from each viewpoint into a shared 3D space through predicted depth maps and recalibrate them belonging to the same body part based on cross-view attention. This helps the model resolve the spatial ambiguity occurring in highly textured regions as well as occluded body parts, thus leading to the accurate localization of 3D Gaussians. Experimental results on benchmark datasets show that the proposed method efficiently improves the performance of generalizable human Gaussian splatting from sparse-view inputs.

### [34] [DDA-Thinker: Decoupled Dual-Atomic Reinforcement Learning for Reasoning-Driven Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25477)
*Hanqing Yang,Qiang Zhou,Yongchao Du,Sashuai Zhou,Zhibin Wang,Jun Song,Tiezheng Ge,Cheng Yu,Bo Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DDA-Thinker框架，通过解耦的Thinker-Editor架构和双原子强化学习（认知原子奖励+视觉原子奖励），在固定生成模型上独立优化规划模块，显著提升需要复杂推理的图像编辑任务性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有图像编辑模型虽视觉保真度高，但在需要复杂推理的任务中表现不佳。作者希望独立优化一个规划模块（Thinker），使其在固定生成模型（Editor）的约束下提升推理驱动的图像编辑能力。

Method: 提出DDA-Thinker框架：(1) Thinker-Editor解耦架构，Thinker负责推理规划，Editor固定不变；(2) 双原子强化学习框架，包含认知原子奖励（评估规划质量）和视觉原子奖励（评估最终图像质量）；(3) 基于可验证检查表的奖励机制；(4) 结合源图像、用户指令和参考描述的三元组检查表合成策略；(5) 两阶段数据流水线：先合成多样化推理数据集，再经困难感知精炼构建训练课程。

Result: 在RISE-Bench和KRIS-Bench等推理驱动图像编辑基准上，该方法显著提升整体性能，使社区模型能够与强闭源模型竞争。

Conclusion: 解耦的Thinker-centric优化范式在固定Editor设置下具有实际潜力，能够有效提升推理驱动的图像编辑性能。

Original Abstract: Recent image editing models have achieved strong visual fidelity but often struggle with tasks requiring complex reasoning. To investigate and enhance the reasoning-grounded planning for image editing, we propose DDA-Thinker, a Thinker-centric framework designed for the independent optimization of a planning module (Thinker) over a fixed generative model (Editor). This decoupled Thinker-centric paradigm facilitates a controlled analysis of the planning module and makes its contribution under a fixed Editor easier to assess. To effectively guide this Thinker, we introduce a dual-atomic reinforcement learning framework. This framework decomposes feedback into two distinct atomic rewards implemented through verifiable checklists: a cognitive-atomic reward to directly assess the quality of the Thinker's executable plan, which serves as the actionable outcome of the Thinker's reasoning, and a visual-atomic reward to assess the final image quality. To improve checklist quality, our checklist synthesis is grounded not only in the source image and user instruction but also in a rational reference description of the ideal post-edit scene. To support this training, we further develop a two-stage data curation pipeline that first synthesizes a diverse and reasoning-focused dataset, then applies difficulty-aware refinement to curate an effective training curriculum for reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments on reasoning-driven image editing benchmarks, including RISE-Bench and KRIS-Bench, demonstrate that our approach substantially improves overall performance. Our method enables a community model to achieve results competitive with strong proprietary models, highlighting the practical potential of Thinker-centric optimization under a fixed-editor setting.

中文摘要翻译: 近期的图像编辑模型已实现了强大的视觉保真度，但在需要复杂推理的任务中常常表现不佳。为探究和增强图像编辑中基于推理的规划能力，我们提出了DDA-Thinker，一个以Thinker为中心的框架，专门用于在固定生成模型（Editor）上独立优化规划模块（Thinker）。这种解耦的Thinker-centric范式便于对规划模块进行受控分析，并使其在固定Editor下的贡献更易于评估。为有效引导该Thinker，我们引入了一种双原子强化学习框架。该框架通过可验证检查表将反馈分解为两个不同的原子奖励：认知原子奖励直接评估Thinker可执行计划的质量——该计划是Thinker推理的可操作输出，以及视觉原子奖励评估最终图像质量。为提升检查表质量，我们的检查表合成不仅基于源图像和用户指令，还基于理想编辑后场景的合理参考描述。为支持该训练，我们进一步开发了一个两阶段数据构建流水线：首先合成多样化的、以推理为中心的数据集，然后应用困难感知精炼来构建用于强化学习的有效训练课程。在推理驱动的图像编辑基准（包括RISE-Bench和KRIS-Bench）上进行的大量实验表明，我们的方法显著提升了整体性能。我们的方法使社区模型能够达到与强闭源模型竞争的结果，突显了在固定Editor设置下以Thinker为中心的优化的实际潜力。

### [35] [The Forensic Cost of Watermark Removal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25491)
*Gautier Evennou,Ewa Kijak*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文指出现有水印去除方法仅从攻击成功率和感知质量两个维度评估是不充分的，因为它们会留下可被检测的统计伪影。作者提出了“水印移除检测”（WRD）作为第三个评估维度，并证明现有方法均无法在攻击成功率、感知质量和法医可检测性三者间取得平衡。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有水印去除方法的评估仅关注攻击成功率和感知质量，忽略了去除操作会留下可被检测的统计伪影这一安全问题，导致水印去除方法缺乏法医隐身性。

Method: 作者提出“水印移除检测”（WRD）作为第三个评估维度，并训练了一个现代分类器来检测水印去除过程中遗留的统计伪影。

Result: 在10^{-3}假阳性率下，该分类器对所有测试的去除方法均达到了最优检测率；现有水印去除方法均无法在攻击成功率、感知质量和法医可检测性三者间取得平衡。

Conclusion: 法医隐身性（forensic stealthiness）应成为水印去除的必要条件，现有方法在这一维度上存在明显缺失。

Original Abstract: Current watermark removal methods are evaluated on two axes: attack success rate and perceptual quality. We show this is insufficient. While state-of-the-art attacks successfully degrade the watermark signal without visible distortion, they leave distinct statistical artifacts that betray the removal attempt. We name this overlooked axis Watermark Removal Detection (WRD) and demonstrate that a modern classifier trained on these artifacts achieves state-of-the-art detection rates at $10^{-3}$ FPR across every removal method tested. No existing attack accounts for this forensic leakage. We benchmark leading watermarking schemes against standard removal pipelines under the extended evaluation triple of attack success, perceptual quality, and forensic detectability, and find that no current method balances all three. Our results establish forensic stealthiness as a necessary requirement for watermark removal.

中文摘要翻译: 当前的水印去除方法从两个维度进行评估：攻击成功率和感知质量。我们指出这是不充分的。尽管最先进的攻击方法能够在不引入可见失真的情况下成功削弱水印信号，但它们会留下明显的统计伪影，暴露了去除尝试。我们将这一被忽视的维度命名为"水印移除检测"（Watermark Removal Detection, WRD），并证明使用基于这些伪影训练的现代分类器，在10^{-3}的假阳性率下，对所有测试的去除方法均能达到最优的检测率。现有攻击方法均未考虑这种法医学泄漏。我们在扩展的评估三元组——攻击成功率、感知质量和法医可检测性——下对领先的水印方案和标准去除流程进行了基准测试，发现当前没有方法能够平衡所有三个维度。我们的结果确立了法医隐身性作为水印去除的必要条件。

### [36] [The Surprising Effectiveness of Canonical Knowledge Distillation for Semantic Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25530)
*Muhammad Ali,Kevin Alexander Laube,Madan Ravi Ganesh,Lukas Schott,Niclas Popp,Thomas Brox*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文揭示语义分割知识蒸馏中，基于迭代次数的比较具有误导性；在匹配计算预算（墙钟时间）后，简单经典的logit和特征蒸馏方法实际上优于近年提出的复杂分割专用蒸馏方法。进一步发现，通过延长训练时间，特征蒸馏即可达到当前最优水平，表明设计重点应从复杂手工目标转向扩展训练规模。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有语义分割知识蒸馏方法追求复杂的手工设计目标，但仅在固定迭代次数下评估，忽略了不同方法的单次迭代计算成本差异，导致公平性缺失。本文旨在纠正这种不公平的比较范式，重新审视简单经典方法在公平计算预算下的真实表现。

Method: 在匹配墙钟时间（wall-clock compute）的训练预算下，系统比较经典logit蒸馏、特征蒸馏与近年提出的分割专用复杂蒸馏方法的性能。同时探索延长训练时间对特征蒸馏效果的影响。

Result: 1) 基于迭代次数的比较具有误导性；2) 在计算预算匹配时，经典logit和特征蒸馏优于近年分割专用复杂方法；3) 延长训练后，特征蒸馏在Cityscapes和ADE20K上达到ResNet-18最优性能；4) PSPNet ResNet-18学生仅用教师1/4参数量，在Cityscapes上达到教师79.0 vs 79.8的mIoU（99%），在ADE20K上达到92%。

Conclusion: 语义分割中的知识蒸馏无需任务特定的复杂机制，扩展训练规模（scaling）比设计复杂手工目标更应指导未来方法设计。

Original Abstract: Recent knowledge distillation (KD) methods for semantic segmentation introduce increasingly complex hand-crafted objectives, yet are typically evaluated under fixed iteration schedules. These objectives substantially increase per-iteration cost, meaning equal iteration counts do not correspond to equal training budgets. It is therefore unclear whether reported gains reflect stronger distillation signals or simply greater compute. We show that iteration-based comparisons are misleading: when wall-clock compute is matched, \textit{canonical} logit- and feature-based KD outperform recent segmentation-specific methods. Under extended training, feature-based distillation achieves state-of-the-art ResNet-18 performance on Cityscapes and ADE20K. A PSPNet ResNet-18 student closely approaches its ResNet-101 teacher despite using only one quarter of the parameters, reaching 99\% of the teacher's mIoU on Cityscapes (79.0 vs.\ 79.8) and 92\% on ADE20K. Our results challenge the prevailing assumption that KD for segmentation requires task-specific mechanisms and suggest that scaling, rather than complex hand-crafted objectives, should guide future method design.

中文摘要翻译: 近年来，用于语义分割的知识蒸馏（KD）方法引入了日益复杂的精心设计的目标函数，但这些方法通常在固定的迭代次数安排下进行评估。这些目标函数显著增加了每次迭代的计算成本，这意味着相等的迭代次数并不对应相等的训练预算。因此，尚不清楚所报告的性能提升是源于更强的蒸馏信号，还是仅仅源于更多的计算量。我们表明，基于迭代次数的比较具有误导性：当匹配墙钟时间（wall-clock compute）时，经典的logit和特征蒸馏方法优于近期提出的分割专用方法。在延长训练的情况下，基于特征的蒸馏在Cityscapes和ADE20K数据集上以ResNet-18架构达到了当前最优性能。一个PSPNet ResNet-18学生模型仅使用其教师模型四分之一的参数量，便在Cityscapes上达到了教师模型mIoU的99%（79.0对79.8），在ADE20K上达到了92%。我们的结果挑战了“语义分割中的知识蒸馏需要任务特定机制”这一主流假设，并表明扩展训练规模（scaling），而非复杂的手工设计目标，应指导未来的方法设计。

</details>


### [37] [DualGeo: A Dual-View Framework for Worldwide Image Geo-localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25533)
*Junchao Cui,Wenqi Shi,Shaoyong Du,Hang He,Xuanzi Ma,Hao Tang,Xiangyang Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DualGeo是一个两阶段全球图像地理定位框架，先通过双向交叉注意力融合图像与语义分割特征进行视觉-地理对比学习建库，再通过地理聚类重排序和大多模态模型精炼预测坐标，在多个基准上显著超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有全球图像地理定位方法依赖的视觉特征对环境变化（光照、季节、天气等）敏感，且缺乏有效的后处理机制来过滤异常候选结果，导致定位精度受限。

Method: 两阶段框架：（1）地理表征构建阶段：通过双向交叉注意力融合图像特征与语义分割特征，再通过双视图对比学习与GPS坐标对齐，构建全局检索数据库；（2）地理认知精炼阶段：先利用地理聚类对检索候选进行重排序，再输入大型多模态模型（LMMs）进行最终坐标预测。

Result: 在IM2GPS、IM2GPS3k和YFCC4k数据集上，DualGeo在街道级（<1 km）定位精度提升3.6%-16.58%，城市级（<25 km）定位精度提升1.29%-8.77%，均优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: 通过融合语义特征与视觉特征构建鲁棒的地理表征，并引入基于地理聚类的重排序和LMM精炼作为后处理，有效提升了全球图像地理定位的精度。

Original Abstract: Worldwide image geo-localization aims to infer the geographic location of an image captured anywhere on Earth, spanning street, city, regional, national, and continental scales. Existing methods rely on visual features that are sensitive to environmental variations (e.g., lighting, season, and weather) and lack effective post-processing to filter outlier candidates, limiting localization accuracy. To address these limitations, we propose DualGeo, a two-stage framework for worldwide image geo-localization. First, it establishes a geo-representational foundation by fusing image and semantic segmentation features via bidirectional cross-attention. The fused features are then aligned with GPS coordinates through dual-view contrastive learning to build a global retrieval database. Second, it performs geo-cognitive refinement by re-ranking retrieved candidates using geographic clustering. It then feeds them into large multimodal models (LMMs) for final coordinate prediction. Experiments on IM2GPS, IM2GPS3k, and YFCC4k show that DualGeo outperforms state-of-the-art methods, improving street-level (<1 km) and city-level (<25 km) localization accuracy by 3.6%-16.58% and 1.29%-8.77%, respectively. Our code and datasets are available : https://github.com/CJ310177/DualGeo.

中文摘要翻译: 全球图像地理定位旨在推断地球上任意位置拍摄的图像的地理位置，涵盖街道、城市、区域、国家和大陆尺度。现有方法依赖对环境变化（如光照、季节和天气）敏感的视觉特征，且缺乏有效的后处理来过滤异常候选，限制了定位精度。为解决这些局限，我们提出DualGeo，一个用于全球图像地理定位的两阶段框架。首先，通过双向交叉注意力融合图像特征和语义分割特征，建立地理表征基础；然后通过双视图对比学习将融合特征与GPS坐标对齐，构建全局检索数据库。其次，通过地理聚类对检索候选进行重排序，执行地理认知精炼，再将其输入大型多模态模型（LMMs）进行最终坐标预测。在IM2GPS、IM2GPS3k和YFCC4k上的实验表明，DualGeo优于现有最先进方法，街道级（<1 km）和城市级（<25 km）定位精度分别提升3.6%-16.58%和1.29%-8.77%。我们的代码和数据集已在https://github.com/CJ310177/DualGeo开源。

### [38] [Vision SmolMamba: Spike-Guided Token Pruning for Energy-Efficient Spiking State-Space Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25570)
*Dewei Bai,Hongxiang Peng,Yunyun Zeng,Ziyu Zhang,Hong Qu,Yi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Vision SmolMamba，一种脉冲状态空间架构，通过脉冲引导的时空令牌剪枝器实现线性时间选择性循环，在视觉任务中取得优异精度-效率权衡，能耗相比脉冲Transformer降低至少1.5倍。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有脉冲Transformer中二次方令牌交互与脉冲神经计算的稀疏、事件驱动特性本质不匹配，亟需一种更高效的长程视觉建模架构。

Method: 核心是Spike-Guided Spatio-Temporal Token Pruner (SST-TP)，利用脉冲激活强度和首次脉冲延迟估计令牌重要性，渐进去除冗余令牌；在此基础上，SmolMamba模块将脉冲事件直接融入双向状态空间递归，构成脉冲状态空间视觉骨干。

Result: 在ImageNet-1K、CIFAR10/100、CIFAR10-DVS、DVS128 Gesture基准上取得优异精度-效率权衡；与脉冲Transformer和Spiking Mamba变体相比，估计能耗降低至少1.5倍，同时保持竞争性或更优的精度。

Conclusion: 将脉冲引导的令牌稀疏性与状态空间建模相结合，为脉冲视觉系统提供了一种可扩展且节能的新范式。

Original Abstract: Spiking Transformers have shown strong potential for long-range visual modeling through spike-driven self-attention. However, their quadratic token interactions remain fundamentally misaligned with the sparse and event-driven nature of spiking neural computation. To address this limitation, we propose Vision SmolMamba, an energy-efficient spiking state-space architecture that integrates spike-driven dynamics with linear-time selective recurrence. The key idea is a Spike-Guided Spatio-Temporal Token Pruner (SST-TP), which estimates token importance using both spike activation strength and first-spike latency. This mechanism progressively removes redundant tokens while preserving salient spatio-temporal information, enabling efficient scaling with token sparsity. Based on this mechanism, the proposed SmolMamba block incorporates spike events directly into bidirectional state-space recurrence, forming a spiking state-space vision backbone for efficient long-range modeling. Extensive experiments on both static and event-based benchmarks, including ImageNet-1K, CIFAR10/100, CIFAR10-DVS, and DVS128 Gesture, demonstrate that Vision SmolMamba consistently achieves superior accuracy-efficiency trade-offs. In particular, it reduces the estimated energy cost by at least 1.5x compared with prior spiking Transformer baselines and a Spiking Mamba variant while maintaining competitive or improved accuracy. These results demonstrate that combining spike-guided token sparsity with state-space modeling offers a scalable and energy-efficient paradigm for spiking vision systems.

中文摘要翻译: 脉冲Transformer通过脉冲驱动自注意力机制在长程视觉建模中展现出强大潜力。然而，其二次方令牌交互本质上与脉冲神经计算的稀疏、事件驱动特性不匹配。为解决这一局限，我们提出了Vision SmolMamba，一种能效高效的脉冲状态空间架构，将脉冲驱动动力学与线性时间选择性递归相结合。其核心是一个脉冲引导的时空令牌剪枝器（SST-TP），该剪枝器利用脉冲激活强度和首次脉冲延迟来估计令牌重要性。该机制逐步去除冗余令牌，同时保留关键的时空信息，从而实现随令牌稀疏性的高效扩展。基于该机制，所提出的SmolMamba模块将脉冲事件直接融入双向状态空间递归，形成用于高效长程建模的脉冲状态空间视觉骨干。在静态和事件驱动基准（包括ImageNet-1K、CIFAR10/100、CIFAR10-DVS和DVS128 Gesture）上的大量实验表明，Vision SmolMamba始终实现了优异的精度-效率权衡。特别地，与先前的脉冲Transformer基线及Spiking Mamba变体相比，其估计能耗降低了至少1.5倍，同时保持了有竞争力或更高的精度。这些结果表明，将脉冲引导的令牌稀疏性与状态空间建模相结合，为脉冲视觉系统提供了一种可扩展且节能的新范式。

### [39] [Control Your Queries: Heterogeneous Query Interaction for Camera-Radar Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25574)
*Jialong Wu,Yihan Wang,Matthias Rottmann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ConFusion的相机-雷达3D目标检测新范式，通过异质查询交互（含图像查询、雷达查询和可学习世界查询）以及两种关键技术——异质查询混合（QMix）和交互式查询交换采样（QSwap），在nuScenes数据集上达到了最先进的性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有相机-雷达融合方法主要依赖输入混合、特征图混合或基于查询的特征采样，未能充分利用不同模态查询之间的互补信息，缺乏显式的跨类型交互机制。

Method: 提出ConFusion检测器，包含三个核心设计：(1) 将图像查询、雷达查询和分布在3D空间中的可学习世界查询相结合以改进查询初始化和目标覆盖；(2) 异质查询混合（QMix），在特征采样后进行专门的跨类型注意力以整合互补物体证据；(3) 交互式查询交换采样（QSwap），允许相关查询在注意力与几何约束下交换信息特征令牌以改进特征采样。

Result: 在nuScenes数据集上，验证集达到59.1 mAP和65.6 NDS，测试集达到61.6 mAP和67.9 NDS，均达到当时最先进水平。

Conclusion: 通过异质查询交互范式，ConFusion有效融合了相机和雷达的互补信息，显著提升了3D目标检测的性能，验证了跨类型查询交互在多模态融合中的有效性。

Original Abstract: In autonomous driving, camera-radar fusion offers complementary sensing and low deployment cost. Existing methods perform fusion through input mixing, feature map mixing, or query-based feature sampling. We propose a new fusion paradigm, termed heterogeneous query interaction, and present ConFusion, a camera-radar 3D object detector. ConFusion combines image queries, radar queries, and learnable world queries distributed in 3D space to improve query initialization and object coverage. To encourage cross-type interaction among heterogeneous queries, we introduce heterogeneous query mixing (QMix), which performs dedicated cross-type attention after feature sampling to consolidate complementary object evidence. We further propose interactive query swap sampling (QSwap), which improves feature sampling by allowing related queries to exchange informative feature tokens under attention and geometric constraints. Experiments on the nuScenes dataset show that ConFusion achieves state-of-the-art performance, reaching 59.1 mAP and 65.6 NDS on the validation set, and 61.6 mAP and 67.9 NDS on the test set.

中文摘要翻译: 在自动驾驶中，相机-雷达融合具有互补感知和低部署成本的优势。现有方法通过输入混合、特征图混合或基于查询的特征采样进行融合。我们提出了一种新的融合范式，称为异质查询交互，并提出了ConFusion——一个相机-雷达3D目标检测器。ConFusion结合了图像查询、雷达查询和分布在3D空间中的可学习世界查询，以改进查询初始化和物体覆盖。为了促进异质查询之间的跨类型交互，我们引入了异质查询混合（QMix），它在特征采样后执行专门的跨类型注意力，以整合互补的物体证据。我们进一步提出了交互式查询交换采样（QSwap），它允许相关查询在注意力和几何约束下交换信息特征令牌，从而改进特征采样。在nuScenes数据集上的实验表明，ConFusion达到了最先进的性能，在验证集上实现了59.1 mAP和65.6 NDS，在测试集上实现了61.6 mAP和67.9 NDS。

### [40] [Refinement via Regeneration: Enlarging Modification Space Boosts Image Refinement in Unified Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25636)
*Jiayi Guo,Linqing Wang,Jiangshan Wang,Yang Yue,Zeyu Liu,Zhiyuan Zhao,Qinglin Lu,Gao Huang,Chunyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Refinement via Regeneration (RvR)框架，将文本到图像生成中的精炼过程从“编辑”重构为“条件再生”，通过语义token条件而非编辑指令实现更完整的语义对齐和更大修改空间，显著提升生成质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有统一多模态模型（UMMs）在文本到图像（T2I）任务中采用精炼-通过-编辑（RvE）范式，存在两个局限：1）编辑指令只能粗略描述提示-图像不对齐，导致精炼不完整；2）像素级保留虽对编辑必要，却不必要地限制了精炼的有效修改空间。因此需要一种能突破这些限制的新范式。

Method: 提出RvR（Refinement via Regeneration）框架，将精炼重新表述为条件图像再生而非编辑。具体地，模型以目标提示和初始图像的语义token为条件进行图像再生，而非依赖编辑指令和强制内容保留，从而获得更大的修改空间和更完整的语义对齐。

Result: 在Geneval上从0.78提升至0.91，DPGBench从84.02提升至87.21，UniGenBench++从61.53提升至77.41，三个基准均取得显著改进。

Conclusion: RvR框架通过将精炼任务从编辑范式转变为条件再生范式，有效克服了现有方法的局限性，在多个T2I基准上取得了大幅性能提升，验证了方法有效性。

Original Abstract: Unified multimodal models (UMMs) integrate visual understanding and generation within a single framework. For text-to-image (T2I) tasks, this unified capability allows UMMs to refine outputs after their initial generation, potentially extending the performance upper bound. Current UMM-based refinement methods primarily follow a refinement-via-editing (RvE) paradigm, where UMMs produce editing instructions to modify misaligned regions while preserving aligned content. However, editing instructions often describe prompt-image misalignment only coarsely, leading to incomplete refinement. Moreover, pixel-level preservation, though necessary for editing, unnecessarily restricts the effective modification space for refinement. To address these limitations, we propose Refinement via Regeneration (RvR), a novel framework that reformulates refinement as conditional image regeneration rather than editing. Instead of relying on editing instructions and enforcing strict content preservation, RvR regenerates images conditioned on the target prompt and the semantic tokens of the initial image, enabling more complete semantic alignment with a larger modification space. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of RvR, improving Geneval from 0.78 to 0.91, DPGBench from 84.02 to 87.21, and UniGenBench++ from 61.53 to 77.41.

中文摘要翻译: 统一多模态模型（UMMs）在单一框架内整合了视觉理解与生成能力。对于文本到图像（T2I）任务，这种统一能力使得UMMs能够在初始生成后对输出进行精炼，从而可能扩展性能上界。当前基于UMM的精炼方法主要遵循精炼-通过-编辑（RvE）范式，即UMMs生成编辑指令来修改不对齐区域，同时保留已对齐内容。然而，编辑指令通常仅能粗略地描述提示-图像不对齐，导致精炼不完整。此外，像素级保留虽对编辑而言是必要的，却不必要地限制了精炼的有效修改空间。为应对这些局限，我们提出Refinement via Regeneration（RvR），一种将精炼重新表述为条件图像再生而非编辑的新框架。RvR不依赖编辑指令和强制内容保留，而是以目标提示和初始图像的语义token为条件进行图像再生，从而在更大的修改空间内实现更完整的语义对齐。大量实验证明了RvR的有效性，在Geneval上从0.78提升至0.91，DPGBench从84.02提升至87.21，UniGenBench++从61.53提升至77.41。

</details>


### [41] [Prefill-Time Intervention for Mitigating Hallucination in Large Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25642)
*Chengsheng Zhang,Chenghao Sun,Xinyan Jiang,Wei Li,Xinmei Tian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Prefill-Time Intervention (PTI)，一种在预填充阶段对KV缓存进行单次干预的新范式，通过模态感知的分离式干预(引导Key聚焦视觉对象、Value过滤背景噪声)，从源头纠正幻觉倾向的表征，显著缓解LVLM中的幻觉问题，且能与现有解码阶段方法正交集成。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于引导向量(steering vectors)的解码阶段干预方法虽然能减少幻觉，但会意外放大残留幻觉的严重程度。作者归因于这些方法仅关注解码阶段，错误会在自回归过程中累积并逐步恶化后续的幻觉输出。因此需要一种在错误累积之前就从源头进行干预的方法。

Method: 提出Prefill-Time Intervention (PTI)，一种在预填充阶段仅干预一次的引导范式。PTI是模态感知的，为视觉和文本表示推导出不同的方向。干预被解耦为：引导Key朝向视觉上有依据的对象，引导Value过滤背景噪声，从而在源头纠正易产生幻觉的表征。

Result: 大量实验表明PTI在缓解幻觉方面具有显著性能，并且在不同解码策略、LVLM模型和基准测试上具有良好的泛化性。PTI与现有解码阶段方法正交，可实现即插即用集成并进一步提升性能。

Conclusion: PTI通过在预填充阶段从源头干预KV缓存，有效解决了以往解码阶段干预方法中错误累积导致残留幻觉加重的问题，为LVLM幻觉缓解提供了新的有效范式。

Original Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have achieved remarkable progress in visual-textual understanding, yet their reliability is critically undermined by hallucinations, i.e., the generation of factually incorrect or inconsistent responses. While recent studies using steering vectors demonstrated promise in reducing hallucinations, a notable challenge remains: they inadvertently amplify the severity of residual hallucinations. We attribute this to their exclusive focus on the decoding stage, where errors accumulate autoregressively and progressively worsen subsequent hallucinatory outputs. To address this, we propose Prefill-Time Intervention (PTI), a novel steering paradigm that intervenes only once during the prefill stage, enhancing the initial Key-Value (KV) cache before error accumulation occurs. Specifically, PTI is modality-aware, deriving distinct directions for visual and textual representations. This intervention is decoupled to steer keys toward visually-grounded objects and values to filter background noise, correcting hallucination-prone representations at their source. Extensive experiments demonstrate PTI's significant performance in mitigating hallucinations and its generalizability across diverse decoding strategies, LVLMs, and benchmarks. Moreover, PTI is orthogonal to existing decoding-stage methods, enabling plug-and-play integration and further boosting performance. Code is available at: https://github.com/huaiyi66/PTI.

中文摘要翻译: 大型视觉-语言模型在视觉-文本理解方面取得了显著进展，但其可靠性因幻觉(即生成事实上不正确或不一致的响应)而受到严重损害。虽然最近使用引导向量的研究在减少幻觉方面展现出前景，但一个显著的挑战依然存在：它们会无意中放大残留幻觉的严重程度。我们将此归因于它们仅关注解码阶段，错误在自回归过程中累积并逐步恶化后续的幻觉输出。为解决这一问题，我们提出了预填充时间干预(PTI)，一种新颖的引导范式，仅在预填充阶段进行一次干预，在错误累积之前增强初始键值(KV)缓存。具体而言，PTI是模态感知的，为视觉和文本表示推导出不同的方向。这种干预是解耦的，引导Key朝向视觉上有依据的对象，引导Value过滤背景噪声，在源头纠正易产生幻觉的表征。大量实验表明PTI在缓解幻觉方面具有显著性能，并且在不同解码策略、LVLM和基准测试上具有良好的泛化性。此外，PTI与现有解码阶段方法是正交的，可实现即插即用集成并进一步提升性能。代码已在 https://github.com/huaiyi66/PTI 开源。

</details>


### [42] [SAMe: A Semantic Anatomy Mapping Engine for Robotic Ultrasound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25646)
*Jing Zhang,Duojie Chen,Wentao Jiang,Zihan Lou,Jianxin Liu,Xinwu Cui,Qinghong Zhao,Bo Du,Christoph F. Dietrich,Dacheng Tao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SAMe是一种语义解剖映射引擎，为机器人超声提供显式解剖先验层，通过目标-解剖-动作流程解决扫描初始化问题，无需术前CT/MRI即可实现6-DoF探头初始化，在肝脏和肾脏初始化中分别达到97.3%和81.7%的器官命中率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前机器人超声系统缺乏理解患者个体解剖结构的能力，无法自主确定扫描目标、起始位置及适应个体差异，仍然依赖专家干预来启动扫描流程。

Method: SAMe将扫描初始化建模为目标-解剖-动作过程：首先将模糊的临床主诉映射为结构化目标器官，然后从单张外部身体图像实例化患者特定的解剖表示，最后将该表示转化为控制端6自由度探头初始化状态，无需术前CT或MRI配准。

Result: 在真实机器人实验中，SAMe的肝脏初始化器官命中率达97.3%，肾脏初始化达81.7%；即使在限制到质心目标时，SAMe也优于基于表面启发式的基线方法；单器官推理仅需0.08秒。

Conclusion: SAMe建立了显式解剖先验层，有效解决了扫描初始化问题，为基于临床主诉的、解剖学 informed 的自主机器人超声扫描提供了解剖基础，可支持更广泛的下游自主扫描流程。

Original Abstract: Robotic ultrasound has advanced local image-driven control, contact regulation, and view optimization, yet current systems lack the anatomical understanding needed to determine what to scan, where to begin, and how to adapt to individual patient anatomy. These gaps make systems still reliant on expert intervention to initiate scanning. Here we present SAMe, a semantic anatomy mapping engine that provides robotic ultrasound with an explicit anatomical prior layer. SAMe addresses scan initiation as a target-to-anatomy-to-action process: it grounds under-specified clinical complaints into structured target organs, instantiates a patient-specific anatomical representation for the grounded targets from a single external body image, and translates this representation into control-facing 6-DoF probe initialization states without any additional registration using preoperative CT or MRI. The anatomical representation maintained by SAMe is explicit, lightweight (single-organ inference in 0.08s), and compatible with downstream control by design. Across semantic grounding, anatomical instantiation, and real-robot evaluation, SAMe shows strong performance across the full initialization pipeline. In real-robot experiments, SAMe achieved overall organ-hit rates of 97.3% for liver initialization and 81.7% for kidney initialization across the evaluated target sets. Even when restricted to the centroid target, SAMe outperformed the surface-heuristic baseline for both liver and kidney initialization. These results establish an explicit anatomical prior layer that addresses scan initialization and is designed to support broader downstream autonomous scanning pipelines, providing the anatomical foundation for complaint-driven, anatomically informed robotic ultrasonography.

中文摘要翻译: 机器人超声在局部图像驱动控制、接触调节和视图优化方面取得了进展，但现有系统缺乏理解患者个体解剖结构的能力，无法确定扫描目标、起始位置以及如何适应个体患者解剖结构。这些缺陷使得系统仍然依赖专家干预来启动扫描。本文提出SAMe（语义解剖映射引擎），为机器人超声提供显式解剖先验层。SAMe将扫描初始化建模为目标-解剖-动作过程：它将模糊的临床主诉归结为结构化的目标器官，从单张外部身体图像针对所归结的目标实例化患者特定的解剖表示，并在无需术前CT或MRI配准的情况下将此表示转化为面向控制的6自由度探头初始化状态。SAMe维护的解剖表示是显式的、轻量级的（单器官推理耗时0.08秒），并且设计上与下游控制兼容。在语义归结、解剖实例化和真实机器人评估中，SAMe在整个初始化流程中均表现出强劲性能。在真实机器人实验中，SAMe在评估的目标集上，肝脏初始化的总体器官命中率达到97.3%，肾脏初始化达到81.7%。即使在限制到质心目标时，SAMe在肝脏和肾脏初始化中均优于基于表面启发式的基线方法。这些结果建立了一个显式解剖先验层，解决了扫描初始化问题，并旨在支持更广泛的下游自主扫描流程，为基于临床主诉的、解剖学 informed 的自主机器人超声检查提供了解剖基础。

### [43] [Toward Multimodal Conversational AI for Age-Related Macular Degeneration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25720)
*Ran Gu,Benjamin Hou,Mélanie Hébert,Asmita Indurkar,Yifan Yang,Emily Y. Chew,Tiarnán D. L. Keenan,Zhiyong Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了OcularChat，一个基于Qwen2.5-VL微调的多模态大语言模型，通过模拟医患对话在彩色眼底照片上进行年龄相关性黄斑变性(AMD)诊断。该模型在AREDS和AREDS2数据集上显著优于现有MLLMs，并在三位独立眼科医生的临床评估中获得了更高评分，兼具强分类性能、诊断推理能力和交互式对话能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有深度学习模型在视网膜疾病检测中表现良好，但大多产生静态预测，缺乏临床推理和交互式解释能力，无法有效支持临床决策和患者咨询。

Method: 从Qwen2.5-VL基础模型出发，使用705,850条模拟医患对话对（配对46,167张CFP）进行微调，训练OcularChat通过视觉问答方式识别AMD关键特征并生成带推理的诊断预测。

Conclusion: 多模态大语言模型能够实现准确、可解释且临床有用的基于图像的AMD诊断与分类，OcularChat展示了提供诊断推理、临床相关解释和交互式对话的能力。

Original Abstract: Despite strong performance of deep learning models in retinal disease detection, most systems produce static predictions without clinical reasoning or interactive explanation. Recent advances in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) integrate diagnostic predictions with clinically meaningful dialogue to support clinical decision-making and patient counseling. In this study, OcularChat, an MLLM, was fine-tuned from Qwen2.5-VL using simulated patient-physician dialogues to diagnose age-related macular degeneration (AMD) through visual question answering on color fundus photographs (CFPs). Beyond strong objective performance in AMD severity classification, OcularChat demonstrated the ability to provide diagnostic reasoning, clinically relevant explanations, and interactive dialogue, with high performance in subjective ophthalmologist evaluation. These findings suggest that MLLMs may enable accurate, interpretable, and clinically useful image-based diagnosis and classification of AMD.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管深度学习模型在视网膜疾病检测中表现强劲，但大多数系统只能产生静态预测，缺乏临床推理或交互式解释能力。多模态大语言模型的最新进展将诊断预测与临床上有意义的对话相结合，以支持临床决策和患者咨询。在本研究中，OcularChat——一个多模态大语言模型——从Qwen2.5-VL出发，通过模拟患者-医生对话进行微调，利用彩色眼底照片上的视觉问答来诊断年龄相关性黄斑变性。共生成705,850条模拟对话（配对46,167张彩色眼底照片）用于训练OcularChat识别关键AMD特征并产生带推理的预测。OcularChat在AREDS数据集上表现出强大的分类性能，在晚期AMD、色素异常和玻璃膜疣大小三个诊断任务中分别达到0.954、0.849和0.678的准确率，显著优于现有MLLMs。在AREDS2上，OcularChat在所有任务中保持最优性能。在三位独立眼科医生的评估中，基于5分临床评分量表，OcularChat在晚期AMD（3.503 vs. 2.833）、色素异常（3.272 vs. 2.828）、玻璃膜疣大小（3.064 vs. 2.433）和总体印象（2.978 vs. 2.464）方面的平均得分均高于强基线模型。除了在AMD严重程度分类中表现出色的客观性能外，OcularChat还展示了提供诊断推理、临床相关解释和交互式对话的能力，并在主观眼科医生评估中表现优异。这些发现表明，多模态大语言模型可能实现准确、可解释且临床有用的基于图像的AMD诊断与分类。

### [44] [Sketch2Arti: Sketch-based Articulation Modeling of CAD Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25781)
*Yi Yang,Hao Pan,Yijing Cui,Alla Sheffer,Changjian Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Sketch2Arti是一个基于草图的三维CAD物体关节建模系统，用户通过简单2D草图即可指定部件的运动方式，系统自动识别可动部件并预测运动参数，支持复杂物体的多关节迭代建模和外壳模型内部结构补全，且无需物体类别信息，泛化能力强。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 设计师通过轻量级草图（如箭头和笔画）自然地表达关节运动意图，但将此类草图转化为可交互的关节化3D模型仍主要依赖手动操作，亟需一种自动化的草图驱动关节建模方法。

Method: 给定CAD模型和用户从选定视角绘制的2D草图，系统自动发现对应的可动部件并预测其运动参数；采用类别无关的训练方式，无需物体类别信息；对于缺乏内部结构的外壳模型，通过用户草图引导实现可控的内部结构补全。

Result: 综合实验和用户评估证明了Sketch2Arti在有效性、可控性和泛化性方面的优越表现，能够泛化到现有关节数据集之外的各类物体。

Conclusion: Sketch2Arti成功弥合了概念草图与关节化3D模型之间的鸿沟，为CAD物体的交互式动画、仿真和形状编辑提供了高效的草图驱动解决方案。

Original Abstract: Articulation modeling aims to infer movable parts and their motion parameters for a 3D object, enabling interactive animation, simulation, and shape editing. In this paper, we present Sketch2Arti, the first sketch-based articulation modeling system for CAD objects. Our key observation is that designers naturally communicate articulation intent through lightweight sketches (e.g., arrows and strokes) that indicate how parts should move, yet translating such sketches into articulated 3D models remains largely manual. Sketch2Arti bridges this gap by enabling users to specify articulation through simple 2D sketches drawn from a chosen viewpoint. Given a CAD model and user sketches, our approach automatically discovers the corresponding movable parts and predicts their motion parameters, allowing iterative modeling of multiple articulations on complex objects with fine-grained control. Importantly, Sketch2Arti is trained in a category-agnostic manner without requiring object category information, leading to strong generalization to diverse objects beyond existing articulation datasets. Moreover, for shell models lacking interior structures, Sketch2Arti supports controllable internal completion guided by user sketches, generating plausible internal components consistent with the existing geometry and predicted motion constraints. Comprehensive experiments and user evaluations demonstrate the effectiveness, controllability, and generalization of Sketch2Arti. The code, dataset, and the prototype system are at https://arlo-yang.github.io/Sketch2Arti.

中文摘要翻译: 关节建模旨在推断3D物体的可动部件及其运动参数，从而实现交互式动画、仿真和形状编辑。本文提出Sketch2Arti，这是首个基于草图的CAD物体关节建模系统。我们的关键观察是，设计师通过轻量级草图（如箭头和笔画）自然地传达关节运动意图，表明部件应如何运动，然而将此类草图转化为关节化3D模型目前仍主要依赖手动操作。Sketch2Arti弥合了这一鸿沟，使用户能够通过从选定视角绘制的简单2D草图来指定关节。给定CAD模型和用户草图，我们的方法自动发现对应的可动部件并预测其运动参数，支持对复杂物体进行多关节的迭代建模，实现细粒度的控制。重要的是，Sketch2Arti采用类别无关的方式进行训练，无需物体类别信息，从而对现有关节数据集之外的各类物体展现出强大的泛化能力。此外，针对缺乏内部结构的外壳模型，Sketch2Arti支持由用户草图引导的可控内部补全，生成与现有几何结构和预测运动约束一致的合理内部组件。综合实验和用户评估证明了Sketch2Arti的有效性、可控性和泛化性。代码、数据集和原型系统详见https://arlo-yang.github.io/Sketch2Arti。

### [45] [Instruction-Evidence Contrastive Dual-Stream Decoding for Grounded Vision-Language Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25809)
*Yashwant Pravinrao Bangde,Debaditya Roy*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出IECD²解码框架，通过指令驱动与证据驱动双流对比解码，自适应平衡语言信息量与视觉忠实度，在多个VLM任务上有效减少幻觉并提升性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: VLM在指令遵循和开放视觉推理中表现优异，但常生成视觉证据不足的流畅输出；指令提示进一步放大了语言先验偏差，尤其在视觉信号模糊时，导致幻觉加剧。

Method: 提出指令-证据对比双流解码（IECD²），在每步解码中维护两条并行概率分布：指令驱动流促进信息丰富响应，证据驱动流强制图像接地；通过对称KL散度对比门自适应融合，抑制语言先验偏爱但无视觉支持的token，保留两者一致的token。

Result: 在POPE、MME、VQAv2、AMBER、MS-COCO、LLaVA-Bench等多个数据集上，IECD²在任务准确率、推理性能上持续提升，并在所有评估指标上显著减少幻觉，优于现有最先进解码方法。

Conclusion: 通过双流对比解码显式平衡语言信息性与视觉忠实度，能有效缓解VLM的幻觉问题，提升视觉接地能力，是一种通用且有效的解码框架。

Original Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) exhibit strong performance in instruction following and open-ended vision-language reasoning, yet they frequently generate fluent outputs that are weakly grounded in visual evidence. Prior works have shown that instruction prompting further worsens this issue by amplifying language priors, especially when the visual signal is uncertain or ambiguous. To address this challenge, we propose a decoding framework that explicitly balances linguistic informativeness and visual faithfulness during generation. Our method, Instruction-Evidence Contrastive Dual-Stream Decoding (IECD2), maintains two parallel probability distributions of tokens at each decoding step: an instruction-driven stream that promotes expressive and informative responses, and an evidence-driven stream that enforces strict grounding in the image. These two streams are adaptively fused using a symmetric KL-based contrast-based gate, which suppresses tokens favored by language priors but unsupported by visual evidence, while preserving them when both distributions agree. We evaluate IECD2 on multiple datasets spanning various generative vision-language reasoning tasks such as captioning and visual question answering, including POPE, MME, VQAv2, AMBER, MS-COCO, and LLaVA-Bench. IECD2 demonstrates consistent improvements in task accuracy and reasoning performance, alongside a substantial reduction in hallucination across all evaluation metrics compared to state-of-the-art decoding approaches.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言模型（VLM）在指令遵循和开放式的视觉-语言推理方面表现出强大的性能，但它们经常生成流畅但视觉证据不足的输出。先前的研究表明，指令提示会进一步加剧这一问题，尤其是在视觉信号不确定或模糊时，它会放大语言先验偏差。为应对这一挑战，我们提出一种解码框架，在生成过程中显式地平衡语言信息性与视觉忠实度。我们的方法——指令-证据对比双流解码（Instruction-Evidence Contrastive Dual-Stream Decoding, IECD²）——在每步解码中维护两条并行的token概率分布：一条为指令驱动流，促进表达性和信息丰富的响应；另一条为证据驱动流，强制严格接地于图像。这两条流通过一个基于对称KL散度的对比门进行自适应融合，该门会抑制那些受语言先验偏爱但缺乏视觉证据支持的token，同时在两条分布一致时保留这些token。我们在多个涵盖生成式视觉-语言推理任务（如图像描述和视觉问答）的数据集上评估了IECD²，包括POPE、MME、VQAv2、AMBER、MS-COCO和LLaVA-Bench。实验结果表明，与当前最先进的解码方法相比，IECD²在任务准确率和推理性能上均取得持续提升，并在所有评估指标上显著减少了幻觉现象。

</details>


### [46] [Magnification-Invariant Image Classification via Domain Generalization and Stable Sparse Embedding Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25817)
*Ifeanyi Ezuma,Olusiji Medaiyese*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究了组织病理学分类中由于放大倍数变化导致的域偏移问题，提出了一种基于梯度反转的域泛化模型，在不增加架构复杂度的前提下学习校准、紧凑且可迁移的特征表示，在BreaKHis数据集上显著优于基线方法和GAN增强方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 组织病理学分类模型在一种成像放大倍数下训练后，往往难以泛化到其他放大倍数，放大倍数偏移是阻碍模型鲁棒部署的主要障碍。

Method: 采用患者隔离的留一放大倍数交叉验证协议，比较了三种方法：监督基线、DCGAN生成补丁增强的基线、以及基于梯度反转的域泛化模型——该模型在保留判别信息的同时抑制放大倍数特异性变异。

Result: 域泛化模型在所有留出放大倍数上取得最强判别性能，在200X留出时增益最明显；GAN增强效果不一致。域泛化模型Brier得分最低（0.063 vs 基线0.089），嵌入稀疏性分析显示其特征签名平均维度从1,074降至306（减少3倍以上），同时保持等效预测性能（AUC: 0.967 vs 0.965; F1: 0.930 vs 0.931），跨折签名Jaccard重叠从基线近零提升至0.99。

Conclusion: 无需增加架构复杂度即可学习到校准、紧凑且可迁移的表示，对计算病理学模型在异构采集环境中的可靠部署具有明确意义。

Original Abstract: Magnification shift is a major obstacle to robust histopathology classification, because models trained on one imaging scale often generalize poorly to another. Here, we evaluated this problem on the BreaKHis dataset using a strict patient-disjoint leave-one-magnification-out protocol, comparing supervised baseline, baseline augmented with DCGAN-generated patches, and a gradient-reversal domain-general model designed to preserve discriminative information while suppressing magnification-specific variation. Across held-out magnifications, the domain-general model achieved the strongest overall discrimination and its clearest gain was observed when 200X was held out. By contrast, GAN augmentation produced inconsistent effects, improving some folds but degrading others, particularly at 400X. The domain-general model also yielded the lowest Brier score at 0.063 vs 0.089 at baseline. Sparse embedding analysis further revealed that domain-general training reduced average signature size more than three-fold (306 versus 1,074 dimensions) while preserving equivalent predictive performance (AUC: 0.967 vs 0.965; F1: 0.930 vs 0.931). It also increased cross-fold signature reproducibility from near-zero Jaccard overlap in the baseline to 0.99 between the 100X and 200X folds. These findings show that calibrated, compact, and transferable representations can be learned without added architectural complexity, with clear implications for the reliable deployment of computational pathology models across heterogeneous acquisition settings.

中文摘要翻译: 放大倍数偏移是阻碍鲁棒组织病理学分类的主要障碍，因为在一个成像尺度上训练的模型往往难以泛化到另一尺度。本文在BreaKHis数据集上采用严格的、患者隔离的留一放大倍数交叉验证协议评估了该问题，比较了监督基线、使用DCGAN生成补丁增强的基线，以及一种基于梯度反转的域泛化模型——该模型旨在保留判别信息的同时抑制放大倍数特异性变异。在留出的各个放大倍数上，域泛化模型取得了最强的整体判别性能，其最显著的增益出现在200X被留出时。相比之下，GAN增强的效果不一致，在某些折上有所改善但在其他折上出现退化，尤以400X为甚。域泛化模型还取得了最低的Brier分数（0.063，基线为0.089）。稀疏嵌入分析进一步揭示，域泛化训练将平均特征签名尺寸降低至原来的三分之一以上（306维对比1,074维），同时保持了等效的预测性能（AUC: 0.967对比0.965；F1: 0.930对比0.931）。它还将跨折的签名可重复性从基线的接近零的Jaccard重叠提升至100X和200X折之间的0.99。这些发现表明，可以在不增加架构复杂度的前提下学习到校准、紧凑且可迁移的表示，这对于计算病理学模型在异构采集环境中的可靠部署具有明确的意义。

</details>


### [47] [Mutual Forcing: Dual-Mode Self-Evolution for Fast Autoregressive Audio-Video Character Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25819)
*Yupeng Zhou,Lianghua Huang,Zhifan Wu,Jiabao Wang,Yupeng Shi,Biao Jiang,Daquan Zhou,Yu Liu,Ming-Ming Cheng,Qibin Hou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Mutual Forcing框架，用于快速自回归音视频生成与长程同步。通过两阶段训练（先单模态再联合）和单模型内多步/少步自蒸馏，在4-8步内达到甚至超越需50步的强基线模型的效果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有流式音视频生成方法通常先训练双向模型，再通过多阶段蒸馏转换为因果生成器，流程复杂、开销大；且缺乏原生快速因果音视频模型。本文旨在直接构建原生自回归音视频模型，简化训练流程并提升效率。

Method: 1）两阶段训练：先分别训练音频和视频的单模态生成器，再耦合为统一模型在配对数据上联合训练。2）Mutual Forcing：基于原生自回归模型，在单一权重共享模型中集成少步（few-step）和多步（multi-step）生成模式。多步模式通过自蒸馏提升少步模式质量；少步模式在训练时生成历史上下文以改善训练-推理一致性。两种模式共享参数，相互增强，无需额外双向教师模型。

Result: Mutual Forcing在仅需4-8个采样步数的情况下，匹配或超越了需要约50个采样步数的强基线模型，在效率和生成质量上均展现出显著优势。

Conclusion: Mutual Forcing通过原生自回归架构和单模型内多步/少步相互蒸馏的设计，有效解决了快速音视频联合生成与长程同步问题，简化了训练流程，降低了开销，并在少步数下取得了优越性能。

Original Abstract: In this work, we propose Mutual Forcing, a framework for fast autoregressive audio-video generation with long-horizon audio-video synchronization. Our approach addresses two key challenges: joint audio-video modeling and fast autoregressive generation. To ease joint audio-video optimization, we adopt a two-stage training strategy: we first train uni-modal generators and then couple them into a unified audio-video model for joint training on paired data. For streaming generation, we ask whether a native fast causal audio-video model can be trained directly, instead of following existing streaming distillation pipelines that typically train a bidirectional model first and then convert it into a causal generator through multiple distillation stages. Our answer is Mutual Forcing, which builds directly on native autoregressive model and integrates few-step and multi-step generation within a single weight-shared model, enabling self-distillation and improved training-inference consistency. The multi-step mode improves the few-step mode via self-distillation, while the few-step mode generates historical context during training to improve training-inference consistency; because the two modes share parameters, these two effects reinforce each other within a single model. Compared with prior approaches such as Self-Forcing, Mutual Forcing removes the need for an additional bidirectional teacher model, supports more flexible training sequence lengths, reduces training overhead, and allows the model to improve directly from real paired data rather than a fixed teacher. Experiments show that Mutual Forcing matches or surpasses strong baselines that require around 50 sampling steps while using only 4 to 8 steps, demonstrating substantial advantages in both efficiency and quality. The project page is available at https://mutualforcing.github.io.

中文摘要翻译: 在本工作中，我们提出Mutual Forcing，一个用于快速自回归音视频生成并实现长程音视频同步的框架。我们的方法解决了两个关键挑战：联合音视频建模与快速自回归生成。为简化联合音视频优化，我们采用两阶段训练策略：首先训练单模态生成器，然后将其耦合为统一的音视频模型，在配对数据上进行联合训练。针对流式生成，我们探究能否直接训练原生的快速因果音视频模型，而非遵循现有的流式蒸馏流程——后者通常先训练双向模型，再通过多个蒸馏阶段将其转换为因果生成器。我们的答案是Mutual Forcing，它直接构建于原生自回归模型之上，并在单一权重共享模型内集成少步与多步生成，从而实现自蒸馏并改善训练-推理一致性。多步模式通过自蒸馏提升少步模式的质量，而少步模式在训练期间生成历史上下文以改善训练-推理一致性；由于两种模式共享参数，这两种效应在单一模型内相互增强。与Self-Forcing等先前方法相比，Mutual Forcing无需额外的双向教师模型，支持更灵活的训练序列长度，降低了训练开销，并允许模型直接从真实配对数据而非固定教师模型中改进。实验表明，Mutual Forcing在使用仅4至8个采样步数的情况下，匹配或超越了需要约50个采样步数的强基线模型，在效率和生成质量上均展现出显著优势。项目页面见https://mutualforcing.github.io。

</details>


### [48] [SIEVES: Selective Prediction Generalizes through Visual Evidence Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25855)
*Hector G. Rodriguez,Marcus Rohrbach*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SIEVES提出通过视觉证据评分实现多模态大语言模型的选择性预测，在OOD场景下将覆盖率提升至三倍，且无需访问私有模型的权重或logits即可迁移。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统VQA基准趋于饱和，但多模态大模型在真实世界分布外（OOD）场景中仍难以满足低容错要求。现有方法缺乏可靠的视觉定位证据来支持选择性预测，导致模型在OOD场景下覆盖率低、泛化能力差。

Method: SIEVES包含两个组件：(1) 推理器（reasoner）在回答问题同时生成局部化的视觉证据；(2) 选择器（selector）显式学习评估推理器提供的视觉定位质量，据此对低置信度答案进行弃权，从而实现满足用户定义风险水平下的最大覆盖率。

Result: 在V* Bench、HR-Bench-8k、MME-RealWorld-Lite、VizWiz和AdVQA五个OOD基准上，SIEVES相比无定位基线的覆盖率提升高达三倍。该方法可迁移至o3、Gemini-3-Pro等闭源推理器，且无需访问其权重或logits。

Conclusion: SIEVES通过显式建模视觉定位质量，实现了跨五个OOD数据集和三种推理器（Pixel-Reasoner、o3、Gemini-3-Pro）的通用泛化，无需针对特定基准或推理器进行训练或适配。

Original Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) achieve ever-stronger performance on visual-language tasks. Even as traditional visual question answering benchmarks approach saturation, reliable deployment requires satisfying low error tolerances in real-world out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios. Precisely, selective prediction aims to improve coverage, i.e. the share of inputs the system answers, while adhering to a user-defined risk level. This is typically achieved by assigning a confidence score to each answer and abstaining on those that fall below a certain threshold. To enable reliable generalization, we require reasoner models to produce localized visual evidence while answering, and design a selector that explicitly learns to estimate the quality of the localization provided by the reasoner. We show that SIEVES (Selective Prediction through Visual Evidence Scoring) improves coverage by up to three times on challenging OOD benchmarks (V* Bench, HR-Bench-8k, MME-RealWorld-Lite, VizWiz, and AdVQA), compared to non-grounding baselines. Beyond better generalization to OOD tasks, the design of the SIEVES selector enables transfer to proprietary reasoners without access to their weights or logits, such as o3 and Gemini-3-Pro, providing coverage boosts beyond those attributable to accuracy alone. We highlight that SIEVES generalizes across all five tested OOD datasets and reasoner models (Pixel-Reasoner, o3, and Gemini-3-Pro), without benchmark- or reasoner-specific training or adaptation.

中文摘要翻译: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在视觉-语言任务上取得了越来越强的性能。即使传统视觉问答基准逐渐趋于饱和，在实际部署中仍需要满足真实世界分布外（OOD）场景下的低容错要求。具体而言，选择性预测旨在提高覆盖率（即系统回答的输入比例），同时遵守用户定义的风险水平。这通常通过为每个答案分配置信度分数，并对低于特定阈值的答案进行弃权来实现。为了实现可靠的泛化，我们要求推理器模型在回答问题的同时生成局部化的视觉证据，并设计一个选择器，使其显式学习评估推理器所提供的定位质量。我们证明，SIEVES（通过视觉证据评分实现选择性预测）在具有挑战性的OOD基准（V* Bench、HR-Bench-8k、MME-RealWorld-Lite、VizWiz和AdVQA）上，相比无定位基线将覆盖率提升了至多三倍。除了在OOD任务上实现更好的泛化外，SIEVES选择器的设计使其能够迁移至无法访问权重或logits的专有推理器（如o3和Gemini-3-Pro），提供远超单纯准确率提升所带来的覆盖率增益。我们强调，SIEVES在所有五个测试的OOD数据集和推理器模型（Pixel-Reasoner、o3和Gemini-3-Pro）上均实现了泛化，且无需任何针对基准或推理器的特定训练或适配。

### [49] [No Pedestrian Left Behind: Real-Time Detection and Tracking of Vulnerable Road Users for Adaptive Traffic Signal Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25887)
*Anas Gamal Aly,Hala ElAarag*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出NPLB系统，通过实时监测行人行为自适应延长信号灯时长，将弱势道路使用者被困率从9.10%降至2.60%，安全性提升71.4%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有行人过街信号灯采用固定定时策略，无法根据行人行为调整，导致老年人、残障人士等弱势道路使用者（VRUs）在信号灯切换时被困在路中。

Method: NPLB系统集成三个组件：1）基于BGVP数据集微调的YOLOv12目标检测模型（mAP@0.5达0.756）；2）ByteTrack多目标跟踪算法；3）自适应控制器，当剩余时间低于临界阈值时自动延长行人相位。

Result: 通过10,000次蒙特卡洛模拟，NPLB将VRU安全性提升71.4%，被困率从9.10%降至2.60%，且仅在12.1%的过街周期中触发信号延长。

Conclusion: NPLB系统在极小干预频率下显著提升了弱势道路使用者的过街安全性，验证了实时自适应交通信号系统的有效性。

Original Abstract: Current pedestrian crossing signals operate on fixed timing without adjustment to pedestrian behavior, which can leave vulnerable road users (VRUs) such as the elderly, disabled, or distracted pedestrians stranded when the light changes. We introduce No Pedestrian Left Behind (NPLB), a real-time adaptive traffic signal system that monitors VRUs in crosswalks and automatically extends signal timing when needed. We evaluated five state-of-the-art object detection models on the BGVP dataset, with YOLOv12 achieving the highest mean Average Precision at 50% (mAP@0.5) of 0.756. NPLB integrates our fine-tuned YOLOv12 with ByteTrack multi-object tracking and an adaptive controller that extends pedestrian phases when remaining time falls below a critical threshold. Through 10,000 Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that NPLB improves VRU safety by 71.4%, reducing stranding rates from 9.10% to 2.60%, while requiring signal extensions in only 12.1% of crossing cycles.

中文摘要翻译: 当前行人过街信号灯采用固定定时策略运行，无法根据行人行为进行调整，这可能导致老年人、残障人士或分心行人等弱势道路使用者在信号灯切换时被困在路中。我们提出了"不让任何弱势道路使用者掉队"（NPLB）系统，这是一种实时自适应交通信号系统，能够监测人行横道上的弱势道路使用者并在需要时自动延长信号灯时长。我们在BGVP数据集上评估了五种最先进的目标检测模型，其中YOLOv12实现了最高的50%平均精度（mAP@0.5），达到0.756。NPLB系统集成了我们微调后的YOLOv12模型、ByteTrack多目标跟踪算法以及一个自适应控制器，当剩余时间低于临界阈值时自动延长行人相位。通过10,000次蒙特卡洛模拟，我们证明NPLB将弱势道路使用者的安全性提升了71.4%，被困率从9.10%降至2.60%，而仅在12.1%的过街周期中需要信号延长。

### [50] [GCA-BULF: A Bottom-Up Framework for Short-Term Load Forecasting Using Grouped Critical Appliances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24766)
*Yunhao Yao,Jinwei Fang,Puhan Luo,Zhiqiang Wang,Jiahui Hou,Xiang-Yang Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出GCA-BULF框架，通过分组关键家电进行自下而上的短期负荷预测，显著提升预测精度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统自上而下的预测方法难以捕捉多样混合电器负荷的复杂模式，而自下而上的方法虽精度高但监控所有电器成本高昂，且许多电器对总负荷预测贡献不大。

Method: GCA-BULF框架包含三个核心模块：1) 关键电器筛选模块，根据功耗、开关频率和周期性对电器排序，通过迭代负荷分解识别关键电器；2) 关联电器分组模块，基于时空相关性对关键电器聚类进行组级预测；3) 协同负荷预测模块，融合多组预测结果精化总负荷预测。

Result: 在住宅和办公楼负荷预测任务上，GCA-BULF相比传统自上而下方法提升20.85%-57.88%，相比自下而上方法提升33.03%-92.48%。

Conclusion: 基于分组关键电器的自下而上框架能有效提升短期负荷预测精度，在降低监控成本的同时实现优于传统方法的性能。

Original Abstract: With the rise of time-of-use and tiered electricity pricing, energy consumers are encouraged to adopt peak-shifting strategies by automatically controlling high-power appliances. These help lower energy costs while enhancing the power grid's stability. To support such energy management with high resilience and responsiveness, reliable short-term load forecasting (STLF) plays a critical role. STLF predicts electricity consumption over time horizons ranging from minutes to days, using historical data, temporal patterns, and contextual factors. Traditional top-down forecasting methods struggle to capture the complex consumption patterns of diverse and mixed appliance loads. Although bottom-up methods improve forecasting accuracy by integrating appliance-level data, monitoring all appliances is costly, and many do not meaningfully impact total load prediction. Therefore, we propose GCA-BULF, a bottom-up short-term load forecasting framework based on grouped critical appliances, supported by three key designs. First, the Critical Appliance Filtering module ranks appliances according to their power consumption, switching frequency, and usage pattern periodicity, and identifies critical ones through iterative load decomposition. Next, the Related Appliance Grouping module clusters these appliances based on spatial and temporal correlations for group-level forecasting. Finally, the Collaborative Load Forecasting module refines the total load prediction by combining multiple group-level forecasts. We evaluate GCA-BULF on residential and office building load forecasting tasks. Experimental results reveal that GCA-BULF improves hourly total load forecasting by 20.85%-57.88% compared to existing top-down methods and by 33.03%-92.48% compared to bottom-up methods.

中文摘要翻译: 随着分时电价和阶梯电价的推行，能源消费者被鼓励通过自动控制高功率电器来采用移峰策略。这些措施有助于降低能源成本，同时增强电网的稳定性。为支持具有高弹性和高响应性的能源管理，可靠的短期负荷预测（STLF）发挥着关键作用。STLF利用历史数据、时间模式和上下文因素，预测从分钟到天不等时间范围内的电力消耗。传统的自上而下预测方法难以捕捉多样混合电器负荷的复杂消费模式。尽管自下而上的方法通过整合电器级数据提高了预测准确性，但监控所有电器成本高昂，且许多电器对总负荷预测的贡献并不显著。因此，我们提出GCA-BULF——一种基于分组关键电器的自下而上短期负荷预测框架，该框架由三个关键设计支撑。首先，关键电器筛选模块根据电器的功耗、开关频率和使用模式周期性对其进行排序，并通过迭代负荷分解识别关键电器。其次，关联电器分组模块基于时空相关性对这些电器进行聚类，以实现组级预测。最后，协同负荷预测模块通过融合多个组级预测结果来精化总负荷预测。我们在住宅和办公楼负荷预测任务上评估了GCA-BULF。实验结果表明，与现有自上而下方法相比，GCA-BULF将小时级总负荷预测精度提升了20.85%-57.88%；与自下而上方法相比，提升幅度达33.03%-92.48%。

</details>


### [51] [Automated detection of pediatric congenital heart disease from phonocardiograms using deep and handcrafted feature fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24767)
*Abdul Jabbar,Ethan Grooby,Yang Yi Poh,Khawza I. Ahmad,Md Hassanuzzaman,Raqibul Mostafa,Ahsan H. Khandoker,Faezeh Marzbanrad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种基于深度特征融合的数字听诊器方法，利用心音图（PCG）记录自动早期检测先天性心脏病（CHD），在751名儿童受试者上达到92%准确率、96%AUROC，适用于低资源环境下的成本效益筛查。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 先天性心脏病（CHD）是最常见的出生缺陷，但金标准诊断方法超声心动图成本高、在低资源环境下难以普及，且依赖专家经验导致诊断延迟和判读差异。因此需要一种更易获取、成本更低的早期筛查手段。

Method: 基于深度特征融合方法，整合深度学习特征与手工设计特征，利用数字听诊器采集心音图（PCG）信号，对751名孟加拉国儿科受试者（年龄1个月至16岁）在四个听诊位置（二尖瓣、主动脉瓣、肺动脉瓣、三尖瓣）进行记录，自动区分CHD与非CHD病例。

Result: 在70%训练、20%验证、10%测试的患者独立划分下，模型取得92%准确率、91%灵敏度、91%特异性、96%AUROC和92%F1分数。

Conclusion: 该模型有望作为低资源环境下高效、实时、远程的CHD成本效益筛查工具。

Original Abstract: Congenital heart disease (CHD) is the most common type of birth defect, impacting about 1% of live births worldwide. Echocardiography, the gold-standard diagnostic method, is costly and inaccessible in low-resource settings. Diagnosis is delayed due to limited skilled experts, whose ability to interpret pathological patterns varies significantly, causing inter- and intra-clinician variability. Therefore, we present a new method for a more accessible diagnostic modality, the digital stethoscope, to detect CHDs. Our method is based on deep feature fusion, integrating deep and handcrafted features for the automated early detection of CHDs. For this work, Phonocardiography (PCG) recordings were obtained from 751 pediatric subjects (Age:1 month- 16 years) in Bangladesh, ranging from infants to adults at four auscultation locations: mitral valve (MV), aortic valve (AV), pulmonary valve (PV), and tricuspid valve (TV). These recordings were labeled based on confirmed diagnoses by cardiologists as either cases of CHD or non-CHD. The results demonstrated that our proposed model achieved an accuracy of 92%, a sensitivity of 91%, and a specificity of 91%, based on a patient-wise split of 70% training, 20% validation, and 10% testing. Furthermore, the Area Under the Receiver Operating Characteristic curve (AUROC) of 96%, and an F1-score of 92%. This model promises efficient real-time remote detection of CHDs as a cost-effective screening tool for low-resource settings.

中文摘要翻译: 先天性心脏病（Congenital Heart Disease, CHD）是最常见的出生缺陷类型，影响全球约1%的活产婴儿。超声心动图作为金标准诊断方法，在低资源环境下成本高昂且难以普及。由于缺乏熟练的专家，且专家解读病理模式的能力差异显著，导致诊断延迟以及临床医生间和临床医生内的判读差异。因此，我们提出了一种基于数字听诊器的新方法，作为一种更易获取的诊断手段来检测CHD。我们的方法基于深度特征融合，将深度特征与手工特征相结合，用于CHD的自动化早期检测。本研究从孟加拉国751名儿科受试者（年龄：1个月至16岁，涵盖婴幼儿至成人）中获取心音图（Phonocardiography, PCG）记录，采集位置包括四个听诊区：二尖瓣、主动脉瓣、肺动脉瓣和三尖瓣。这些记录根据心脏病专家确诊结果被标记为CHD病例或非CHD病例。结果表明，在70%训练集、20%验证集和10%测试集的患者独立划分下，我们提出的模型达到了92%的准确率、91%的灵敏度和91%的特异性。此外，受试者工作特征曲线下面积（AUROC）为96%，F1分数为92%。该模型有望作为一种成本效益高的筛查工具，在低资源环境下实现高效、实时的远程CHD检测。

</details>


### [52] [Architecture Determines Observability in Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24801)
*Thomas Carmichael*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现自回归Transformer的激活监控有效性取决于架构和训练方式，并定义了“可观测性”（observability）——从中层激活中线性读取决策质量的能力（控制置信度和激活范数后）。研究发现可观测性并非通用属性，某些配置（如Pythia 24层16头）会完全崩溃，且该崩溃在训练中涌现。不同模型家族表现差异巨大，架构选择本身就是监控决策。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 自回归Transformer会做出过度自信的错误预测，激活监控可以捕获这些错误，但这依赖于模型是否在内部保留了输出置信度未暴露的信号。这种信号保留程度由架构和训练方式决定，现有研究对此缺乏系统性理解。

Method: 定义“可观测性”为：在控制最大softmax置信度和激活范数后，从冻结的中间层激活中线性读出每个token决策质量的能力。通过对13个模型（6个家族）进行系统性的探针实验和部分相关性分析。

Result: (1) 置信度控制平均吸收了57.7%的原始探针信号；(2) Pythia中24层16头配置在所有测试运行中部分相关系数rho_partial约0.10（跨3.5倍参数差距和两种Pile变体），而其他六种配置在0.21-0.38的健康区间；(3) 输出控制残差在同一配置点崩溃，非线性探针和层扫描无法恢复；(4) 崩溃在训练中涌现，早期检查点有信号但训练后消失；(5) 不同模型家族表现各异：Qwen 2.5与Llama在相同3B规模相差2.9倍且探针种子分布无重叠，Mistral 7B保持可观性而Llama 3.1 8B崩溃；(6) WikiText训练的观察器可迁移至下游QA任务，在20%标记率下对9个模型-任务组合中的7个实现了10.9-13.4%的独占错误捕获率。

Conclusion: 可观测性不是Transformer的通用属性，它取决于具体的架构配置和训练方式，且会在某些配置下完全崩溃。架构选择本身就是一个监控决策——不同的架构即使宏观相似，也会导致监控可行性的巨大差异。

Original Abstract: Autoregressive transformers make confident errors, but activation monitoring can catch them only if the model preserves an internal signal that output confidence does not expose. This preservation is determined by architecture and training recipe. We define observability as the linear readability of per-token decision quality from frozen mid-layer activations after controlling for max-softmax confidence and activation norm. The correction is essential. Confidence controls absorb 57.7% of raw probe signal on average across 13 models in 6 families.
  Observability is not a generic property of transformers. In Pythia's controlled suite, every tested run with the 24-layer, 16-head configuration collapses to rho_partial ~0.10 across a 3.5x parameter gap and two Pile variants, while six other configurations occupy a separated healthy band from 0.21 to 0.38. The output-controlled residual collapses at the same points, and neither tested nonlinear probes nor layer sweeps recover healthy-range signal. Checkpoint dynamics show the collapse is emergent during training. Both configurations at matched hidden dimension form the signal at the earliest measured checkpoint, but training erases it in the (24L, 16H) class while predictive loss continues improving.
  Across independent recipes the collapse map changes but the phenomenon persists. Qwen 2.5 and Llama differ by 2.9x at matched 3B scale with probe seed distributions that do not overlap, while Mistral 7B preserves observability where Llama 3.1 8B collapses despite similar broad architecture. A WikiText-trained observer transfers to downstream QA without training on those tasks, catching errors confidence misses. At 20% flag rate, its exclusive catch rate is 10.9-13.4% of all errors in seven of nine model-task cells. Architecture selection is a monitoring decision.

中文摘要翻译: 自回归Transformer会做出过度自信的错误预测，但只有当模型保留了输出置信度未暴露的内部信号时，激活监控才能捕获这些错误。这种信号保留程度由架构和训练方式决定。我们定义了“可观测性”（observability），即在控制最大softmax置信度和激活范数后，从冻结的中间层激活中线性读取每个token决策质量的能力。这一校正至关重要：在6个模型家族的13个模型中，置信度控制平均吸收了57.7%的原始探针信号。可观测性并非Transformer的通用属性。在Pythia的控制实验套件中，24层16头配置的每个测试运行在3.5倍的参数差距和两种Pile变体下，部分相关系数rho_partial均崩溃至约0.10，而其他六种配置则稳定在0.21至0.38的健康区间内。输出控制残差在同一配置点崩溃，且无论采用非线性探针还是层扫描均无法恢复健康区间的信号。检查点动态显示，这种崩溃是在训练过程中涌现的。两种匹配隐藏维度的配置在最早的检查点即形成了信号，但训练在(24L, 16H)类中抹去了该信号，而预测损失仍在持续改善。在不同独立训练方案中，崩溃图谱会发生变化，但该现象本身持续存在。Qwen 2.5和Llama在匹配的3B规模下相差2.9倍，且探针种子分布无重叠；而Mistral 7B保持了可观测性，Llama 3.1 8B却发生崩溃，尽管两者具有相似的宏观架构。一个基于WikiText训练的观察器，无需针对下游任务进行训练即可迁移到问答任务中，捕获了置信度遗漏的错误。在20%的标记率下，对9个模型-任务组合中的7个，其独占错误捕获率达到10.9-13.4%。架构选择本身就是一种监控决策。

</details>


### [53] [Intrinsic Mutual Information as a Modulator for Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24804)
*Peng Liao,Peijia Zheng,Lingbo Li,Shangsong Liang,Lin Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出RMiPO框架，利用响应级互信息进行离线偏好优化，无需额外超参数调优即可提升性能并降低15%以上训练开销。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有离线偏好优化方法（如DPO）虽能有效对齐大语言模型与人类价值观，但通常需要额外的超参数调优，导致大量时间开销；尽管已有改进工作，但仍未完全消除对超参数调优的依赖。

Method: 提出RMiPO框架，通过利用响应级互信息进行偏好优化，结合超参数调制动态解耦偏好贡献，仅需可忽略的额外计算成本。

Result: 大量实验结果表明，RMiPO在性能上持续优于现有方法，同时将训练开销降低15%以上。

Conclusion: RMiPO是一种轻量高效的离线偏好优化框架，在减少超参数调优依赖的同时实现了更优的性能和更低的训练成本。

Original Abstract: Offline preference optimization methods, such as Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), offer significant advantages in aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) with human values. However, achieving optimal performance with these methods typically involves additional hyperparameter tuning, resulting in substantial time overhead. Although prior work has proposed a range of improvements, these methods remain limited in effectiveness and have not fully eliminated reliance on hyperparameter tuning. In this work, we propose RMiPO, a lightweight and efficient framework for offline preference optimization. RMiPO leverages intrinsic Response-level Mutual information for Preference Optimization with hyperparameter modulation, dynamically decoupling preference contributions at negligible additional computational cost. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that RMiPO achieves consistently superior performance over existing methods while reducing training overhead by more than 15\%. Our code is available at https://github.com/liavonpenn/rmipo.

中文摘要翻译: 离线偏好优化方法，如直接偏好优化（DPO），在对齐大语言模型（LLMs）与人类价值观方面具有显著优势。然而，这些方法要达到最优性能通常需要额外的超参数调优，导致大量的时间开销。尽管已有工作提出了一系列改进措施，但这些方法的效果仍然有限，并未完全消除对超参数调优的依赖。在本文中，我们提出了RMiPO，一个轻量且高效的离线偏好优化框架。RMiPO利用响应级互信息进行偏好优化，通过超参数调制动态解耦偏好贡献，且仅需可忽略的额外计算成本。大量实验结果表明，RMiPO在性能上持续优于现有方法，同时将训练开销降低15%以上。我们的代码已开源在https://github.com/liavonpenn/rmipo。

</details>


### [54] [minAction.net: Energy-First Neural Architecture Design -- From Biological Principles to Systematic Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24805)
*Martin G. Frasch*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过2203项实验，系统地研究了能量感知学习在机器学习中的重要性。主要发现包括：架构本身对精度影响极小（部分eta²=0.001），但架构与数据集的交互效应显著（部分eta²=0.44）；通过单参数能量正则化目标函数，内部激活能量可降至基线6%而精度不下降；基于作用量原理的能量优先架构相比传统基线实现了5-33%的训练效率提升。论文将这一研究框架基于经典力学作用泛函、统计物理自由能与变分推断中KL正则化目标之间的结构对应关系。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现代机器学习优化精度时未明确考虑内部计算成本，而物理和生物系统在固有能量约束下运行。本文旨在探索能量感知学习的有效性，并验证不同模态下最优架构的依赖性。

Method: 方法包括：(1) 在2203个实验中跨视觉、文本、神经形态和生理数据集进行10个种子的全因子统计分析；(2) 提出单参数能量正则化目标函数 L = L_CE + λ * E(θ, x)；(3) 基于作用量原理框架设计能量优先架构。

Result: (1) 架构单独解释的精度方差可忽略（部分eta²=0.001），而架构×数据集交互效应显著（部分eta²=0.44, p<0.001）；(2) 在适度λ下内部激活能量降至基线6%而无精度损失；(3) 能量优先架构带来5-33%的模内训练效率提升。

Conclusion: 最优架构关键依赖于任务模态，不存在通用的最佳架构；能量正则化可大幅降低计算成本而不损失精度；基于作用量原理的设计假设为高效学习提供了新方向。

Original Abstract: Modern machine learning optimizes for accuracy without explicitly accounting for internal computational cost, even though physical and biological systems operate under intrinsic energy constraints. We evaluate energy-aware learning across 2,203 experiments spanning vision, text, neuromorphic, and physiological datasets, using 10 seeds per configuration and performing a factorial statistical analysis. Three findings emerge. First, architecture alone explains negligible variance in accuracy (partial eta^2 = 0.001). In contrast, the architecture x dataset interaction is large (partial eta^2 = 0.44, p < 0.001), demonstrating that optimal architecture depends critically on task modality and rejecting the assumption of a universal best architecture. Second, a controlled lambda-sweep over four orders of magnitude validates a single-parameter energy-regularized objective L = L_CE + lambda * E(theta, x): internal activation energy decreases to 6% of baseline at moderate lambda with no accuracy degradation on MNIST. Third, energy-first architectures inspired by an action-principle framework yield 5-33% within-modality training-efficiency gains over conventional baselines. These results emerge from a research program that interprets learning through a structural correspondence between the action functional in classical mechanics, free energy in statistical physics, and KL-regularized objectives in variational inference. We frame this correspondence as a design hypothesis rather than a derivation.

中文摘要翻译: 现代机器学习在优化精度时并未明确考虑内部计算成本，尽管物理和生物系统在固有的能量约束下运行。我们通过2203项实验评估了能量感知学习，涵盖视觉、文本、神经形态和生理数据集，每项配置使用10个种子并进行因子统计分析。三项发现如下：第一，架构单独解释的精度方差可忽略不计（部分eta²=0.001）。相比之下，架构×数据集的交互效应很大（部分eta²=0.44, p<0.001），表明最优架构关键取决于任务模态，并否定了存在通用最佳架构的假设。第二，跨四个数量级的受控λ扫描验证了单参数能量正则化目标L = L_CE + λ * E(θ, x)：在适度λ下内部激活能量降至基线水平的6%，且在MNIST上无精度下降。第三，受作用量原理框架启发的能量优先架构相比传统基线实现了5-33%的模内训练效率提升。这些结果源自一个将学习解释为经典力学中的作用泛函、统计物理学中的自由能与变分推断中KL正则化目标之间结构对应关系的研究项目。我们将这种对应关系定性为设计假设而非推导结果。

</details>


### [55] [Nautile-370M: Spectral Memory Meets Attention in a Small Reasoning Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24809)
*Maixent Chenebaux*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Nautile-370M是一个3.71亿参数的小语言模型，采用混合骨干架构（两个SCA层+一个Transformer层交替），在严格参数和推理预算下实现高效推理。该模型在单个Cloud TPU v4-64和单个NVIDIA DGX Spark上完成训练，理论上证明了SCA读出机制在连续极限下至少与全自注意力具有同等表达能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 在严格的参数规模和推理预算约束下，设计一种既能保持长上下文效率和状态追踪能力（结构化序列模型优势），又能保留注意力机制中表达性token到token路由能力的小语言模型。

Method: 提出Nautile-370M模型，采用混合骨干架构：两个SeqCond Attention (SCA)层（受SeqCondenser启发的线性时间谱序列算子）与一个Transformer层交替堆叠。训练在单个Cloud TPU v4-64上进行，强化学习阶段在单个NVIDIA DGX Spark上完成。

Result: 理论证明了SCA读出机制能够精确检索前缀摘要中的任意单个token，并能作为特例复现softmax注意力的任何输出，确立了SCA在连续极限下至少与全自注意力具有同等表达能力。

Conclusion: SCA层在保持线性时间复杂度的同时，在表达能力上不逊于全自注意力，结合Transformer层形成的混合架构适合在严格预算下进行高效推理。

Original Abstract: We present Nautile-370M, a 371-million-parameter small language model designed for efficient reasoning under strict parameter and inference budgets. Nautile-370M uses a hybrid backbone in which two SeqCond Attention (SCA) layers, a linear-time spectral sequence operator inspired by SeqCondenser, alternate with one transformer layer. This design aims to retain the long-context efficiency and state-tracking benefits of structured sequential models while preserving the expressive token-to-token routing of attention. The model was trained on a single Cloud TPU v4-64 pod slice provided through the Google TPU Research Cloud (TRC) program; the subsequent reinforcement learning stage was carried out on a single NVIDIA DGX Spark. We prove that the SCA readout mechanism can exactly retrieve any individual token from the prefix summary and can reproduce any output of softmax attention as a special case, establishing that SCA is at least as expressive as full self-attention in the continuous limit. We also describe the training data pipeline and outline a reinforcement learning stage specialized for reasoning, verification, and response quality.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了Nautile-370M，一个具有3.71亿参数的小语言模型，专为在严格的参数和推理预算下实现高效推理而设计。Nautile-370M采用混合骨干架构，其中两个SeqCond Attention (SCA)层（一种受SeqCondenser启发的线性时间谱序列算子）与一个Transformer层交替堆叠。该设计旨在保留结构化序列模型的长上下文效率和状态追踪优势，同时保持注意力机制中富有表达力的token到token路由能力。该模型在通过Google TPU研究云(TRC)计划提供的单个Cloud TPU v4-64 pod切片上进行训练；后续的强化学习阶段在单个NVIDIA DGX Spark上完成。我们理论证明了SCA读出机制能够精确检索前缀摘要中的任意单个token，并能作为特例复现softmax注意力的任何输出，从而确立了SCA在连续极限下至少与全自注意力具有同等表达能力。我们还描述了训练数据流水线，并概述了专门针对推理、验证和响应质量优化的强化学习阶段。

### [56] [Heterogeneous Variational Inference for Markov Degradation Hazard Models: Discretized Mixture with Interpretable Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24818)
*Takato Yasuno*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一套结合精细离散化、多维特征工程、可解释性规则和ADVI推断的实用框架，解决贝叶斯有限混合模型在工业设备风险聚类中的三个瓶颈，在280台工业泵数据上验证了ADVI相比NUTS在稳定性、收敛性和计算效率上的显著优势（84倍加速）。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 贝叶斯有限混合模型在识别设备风险聚类（如低风险与高风险设备）时面临三个关键瓶颈：(1) 粗粒度状态离散化导致退化信号不足；(2) 数据本身支持更少聚类数时聚类识别不稳定；(3) MCMC方法（如NUTS）计算耗时过长（每模型7+小时），无法用于生产部署。因此需要一种实用框架来克服上述问题。

Method: (1) 8状态全局百分位离散化，放大退化事件信号；(2) 30维特征工程，融合统计趋势（22维）、连续健康指标和文本嵌入（PCA压缩至3维）；(3) 可解释的模型选择规则，结合WAIC、最小聚类份额和聚类分离度；(4) 使用全秩协方差矩阵的自动微分变分推断（ADVI）替代MCMC，实现稳定快速估计。

Result: 在280台工业泵（104,703条检测记录）上实验发现：(1) 在随机效应基线模型中，ADVI与NUTS估计结果几乎一致，ADVI实现15倍加速；(2) 有限混合模型结合可解释性约束能识别最优聚类数；(3) NUTS出现严重收敛问题和标签切换，而ADVI在84倍更短时间内提供稳定结果。

Conclusion: (1) 首次证明细粒度状态离散化（8状态）对生存分析中混合模型稳定性至关重要；(2) 提出了融合统计、连续和语义信号的综合特征工程策略；(3) 设计了防止自动化模型选择过拟合的实用可解释性规则；(4) 实证表明在有限混合模型中ADVI在收敛性、稳定性和计算效率上优于NUTS。

Original Abstract: Bayesian finite mixture models can identify discrete risk clusters (low-risk vs. high-risk equipment), but face three critical bottlenecks: (1) insufficient degradation signals from coarse state discretization, (2) unstable cluster identification when data inherently supports fewer clusters than explored, and (3) computational infeasibility of Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods for production deployment (7+ hours per model). We propose a practical framework combining (1) 8-state global percentile discretization that amplifies degradation events, (2) 30-dimensional feature engineering integrating statistical trends (22 features), continuous health indicators, and text embeddings (PCA-compressed to 3 dimensions), (3) interpretable model selection rules enforcing minimum cluster share and separation alongside WAIC, and (4) Automatic Differentiation Variational Inference (ADVI) with full-rank covariance for stable, fast estimation. Applied to 280 industrial pump equipment with 104,703 inspection records, we demonstrate: (1) Random effect models (baseline) show ADVI and NUTS produce nearly identical estimates with 15$\times$ speedup, validating ADVI accuracy. (2) Finite mixture models identify optimal number of clusters with interpretability constraints. (3) NUTS exhibits severe convergence issues and label switching, while ADVI provides stable results in 84$\times$ less time. We contributed that (1) First demonstration that fine-grained state discretization (8-state) is essential for mixture model stability in survival analysis.(2) Comprehensive feature engineering strategy combining statistical, continuous, and semantic signals. (3) Practical interpretability rules preventing overfitting in automated model selection. (4) Empirical evidence that ADVI outperforms NUTS for finite mixture models in terms of convergence, stability, and computational efficiency.

中文摘要翻译: 贝叶斯有限混合模型能够识别离散的风险聚类（低风险与高风险设备），但面临三个关键瓶颈：(1) 粗粒度状态离散化导致退化信号不足；(2) 当数据本身支持的聚类数少于探索数时，聚类识别不稳定；(3) 马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法计算量过大，无法用于生产部署（每模型超过7小时）。我们提出一个实用框架，结合了(1) 8状态全局百分位离散化以放大退化事件；(2) 30维特征工程，融合统计趋势（22维）、连续健康指标和文本嵌入（经PCA压缩至3维）；(3) 可解释的模型选择规则，在WAIC基础上强制最小聚类份额和聚类分离度；(4) 使用全秩协方差矩阵的自动微分变分推断（ADVI），实现稳定快速的估计。应用于280台工业泵设备（共104,703条检测记录），我们证明：(1) 在随机效应模型（基线）中，ADVI与NUTS产生几乎一致的估计结果，且速度快15倍，验证了ADVI的准确性。(2) 有限混合模型在可解释性约束下识别出最优聚类数。(3) NUTS表现出严重的收敛问题和标签切换，而ADVI在84倍更短的时间内提供稳定结果。我们的贡献在于：(1) 首次证明细粒度状态离散化（8状态）对生存分析中混合模型稳定性的必要性。(2) 提出了融合统计、连续和语义信号的综合特征工程策略。(3) 设计了防止自动化模型选择过拟合的实用可解释性规则。(4) 实证表明，对于有限混合模型，ADVI在收敛性、稳定性和计算效率方面均优于NUTS。

</details>


### [57] [Negative Ontology of True Target for Machine Learning: Towards Evaluation and Learning under Democratic Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24824)
*Yongquan Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从哲学视角审视了机器学习预测建模中关于“真实目标”存在性假设的转变，提出基于“真实目标不存在”的本体论假设，构建了“民主监督”知识体系，并在此基础上提出了多重不准确真实目标框架，用于机器学习的评估与学习。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前主流机器学习范式通常假设真实目标客观存在，这一假设在哲学上值得反思。作者旨在通过否定这一本体论假设，提出新的学习范式，以应对现实世界中真实目标不可知或不存在的场景，尤其是在教育和专业发展领域。

Method: 采用否定本体论视角，假设真实目标在客观世界中不存在；在此基础上定义民主监督；提出多重不准确真实目标作为民主监督的实例化实现；推导逻辑驱动的MIATT生成与评估原则、逻辑评估公式以及不可定义真实目标学习机制，最终构建EL-MIATTs框架。

Result: 通过一个真实世界应用案例，展示了所提出的EL-MIATTs框架在支持个体教育和专业发展方面的潜力，验证了民主监督思想在机器学习预测建模中的可行性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的民主监督及EL-MIATTs框架为机器学习预测建模提供了新的哲学基础和实用方法，尤其在教育和专业发展领域具有应用价值，拓展了传统监督学习范式的边界。

Original Abstract: This article philosophically examines how shifts in assumptions regarding the existence and non-existence of the true target (TT) give rise to new perspectives and insights for machine learning (ML)-based predictive modeling and, correspondingly, proposes a knowledge system for evaluation and learning under Democratic Supervision. By systematically analysing the existence assumption of the TT in current mainstream ML paradigms, we explicitly adopt a negative ontology perspective, positing that the TT does not objectively exist in the real world, and, grounded in this non-existence assumption, define Democratic Supervision for ML. We further present Multiple Inaccurate True Targets (MIATTs) as an instance-level realization of Democratic Supervision. Building upon MIATTs, we derive principles, for the logic-driven generation and assessment of MIATTs, a logical assessment formulation for evaluation with MIATTs, and undefinable true target learning for learning with MIATTs. Based on these components, we establish the evaluation and learning with MIATTs (EL-MIATTs) framework for ML-based predictive modelling. A real-world application demonstrates the potential of the proposed EL-MIATTs framework in supporting education and professional development for individuals, aligning with prior discussions of Democratic Supervision in the fields of education and professional development.

中文摘要翻译: 本文从哲学角度审视了关于真实目标存在与不存在假设的转变如何为基于机器学习的预测建模带来新的视角和见解，并相应地提出了一个在民主监督下进行评估与学习的知识体系。通过系统分析当前主流机器学习范式中真实目标的存在性假设，我们明确采用否定本体论视角，认为真实目标在客观世界中并不存在，并基于这一不存在假设定义了机器学习中的民主监督。我们进一步提出多重不准确真实目标作为民主监督的实例级实现。基于MIATTs，我们推导了逻辑驱动的MIATT生成与评估原则、基于MIATTs评估的逻辑评估公式，以及用于MIATTs学习的不可定义真实目标学习机制。基于这些组成部分，我们建立了基于MIATTs的评估与学习框架用于机器学习预测建模。一项真实世界应用展示了所提出的EL-MIATTs框架在支持个体教育和专业发展方面的潜力，这与先前在教育与专业发展领域对民主监督的讨论相一致。
