### [58] [Incompressible Knowledge Probes: Estimating Black-Box LLM Parameter Counts via Factual Capacity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24827)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出不可压缩知识探针（IKP），通过测量模型掌握的事实知识量来推断其参数量下限，在89个开源模型上实现了R²=0.917的拟合精度，并发现知识容量随参数量对数线性增长，反驳了“稠密化定律”对知识压缩的预测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 闭源前沿模型不公开参数量，而基于推理经济的估算方法因硬件、批处理和服务栈等外部假设存在2倍以上的不确定性，需要一种更紧的内在边界来估算模型参数量。

Method: 提出不可压缩知识探针（IKP）基准，包含1400个覆盖7个难度层级的事实问题，专门设计用于隔离无法通过推理推导或架构改进压缩的知识。在89个开源模型上校准IKP准确率与参数量的对数线性映射关系。

Result: 在89个开源模型上R²=0.917；留一交叉验证中位数误差1.59倍；MoE模型中总参数量预测知识效果(R²=0.79)远优于激活参数量(R²=0.51)；评估188个模型，估计了所有主要闭源前沿模型的有效知识容量；IKP时间系数为-0.0010/月，与零无显著差异，以p<10⁻¹⁵拒绝了稠密化定律的预测。

Conclusion: 广泛报道的推理基准饱和并不意味着扩展的终结；知识容量继续随参数量对数线性增长，且在不同代际和厂家间保持一致。

Original Abstract: Closed-source frontier labs do not disclose parameter counts, and the standard alternative -- inference economics -- carries $2\times$+ uncertainty from hardware, batching, and serving-stack assumptions external to the model. We exploit a tighter intrinsic bound: storing $F$ facts requires at least $F/$(bits per parameter) weights, so measuring how much a model \emph{knows} lower-bounds how many parameters it \emph{has}. We introduce \textbf{Incompressible Knowledge Probes (IKPs)}, a benchmark of 1{,}400 factual questions spanning 7 tiers of obscurity, designed to isolate knowledge that cannot be derived by reasoning or compressed by architectural improvements.
  We calibrate a log-linear mapping from IKP accuracy to parameter count on 89 open-weight models (135M--1,600B) spanning 19 vendors, achieving $R^2 = 0.917$; leave-one-out cross-validation confirms generalization (median fold error $1.59\times$, $68.5\%$ within $2\times$ and $87.6\%$ within $3\times$). For Mixture-of-Experts models, total parameters predict knowledge ($R^2 = 0.79$) far better than active parameters ($R^2 = 0.51$). We evaluate 188 models from 27 vendors and estimate effective knowledge capacity for all major proprietary frontier models; for heavily safety-tuned models the estimates are lower bounds, since refusal policy can hide tens of percentage points of "refused but known" capacity.
  The widely-reported saturation of reasoning benchmarks does not imply the end of scaling. Procedural capability compresses under the "Densing Law," but across 96 dated open-weight models the IKP time coefficient is $-0.0010$/month (95\% CI $[-0.0031, +0.0008]$) -- indistinguishable from zero, and rejecting the Densing prediction of $+0.0117$/month at $p < 10^{-15}$. Factual capacity continues to scale log-linearly with parameters across generations and across vendors.

中文摘要翻译: 闭源前沿实验室不公开参数量，而标准的替代方案——推理经济学——由于模型外部的硬件、批处理和服务栈假设，存在2倍以上的不确定性。我们利用一个更紧的内在边界：存储F个事实至少需要F/(每参数比特数)个权重，因此测量模型"知道"多少可以为其"拥有"多少参数量提供下界。我们提出了不可压缩知识探针（IKPs），一个包含1400个覆盖7个难度层级的事实问题的基准，专门设计用于隔离无法通过推理推导或架构改进压缩的知识。我们在来自19家厂商的89个开源模型（135M–1600B参数）上校准了IKP准确率与参数量的对数线性映射，实现了R²=0.917；留一交叉验证证实了泛化能力（中位数折叠误差1.59倍，68.5%在2倍以内，87.6%在3倍以内）。对于混合专家（MoE）模型，总参数量预测知识的效果（R²=0.79）远优于激活参数量（R²=0.51）。我们评估了来自27家厂商的188个模型，并估算了所有主要闭源前沿模型的有效知识容量；对于经过重度安全微调的模型，这些估计值为下界，因为拒绝策略可能隐藏数十个百分点的"被拒绝但已知"的知识容量。广泛报道的推理基准饱和并不意味着扩展的终结。程序性能力在"稠密化定律"下被压缩，但在96个带日期的开源模型中，IKP时间系数为-0.0010/月（95%置信区间[-0.0031, +0.0008]）——与零无显著差异，并以p<10⁻¹⁵拒绝了稠密化定律预测的+0.0117/月。事实知识容量继续随参数量对数线性增长，且在不同代际和不同厂家间保持一致。

### [59] [On the Trainability of Masked Diffusion Language Models via Blockwise Locality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24832)
*Yuxiang Wang,Yu Xiang,Baojian Zhou,Qifang Zhao,Keyue Jiang,Yanghua Xiao,Xiaoxiao Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现掩码扩散语言模型（MDMs）在有序生成任务上优化不稳定，相比自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）存在局限性；为此提出两种局部感知的块级模型Jigsaw和Scatter，通过注入从左到右的归纳偏置来平衡稳定性与扩散优势。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准随机掩码的MDMs在有序结构生成（如线性回归、图路径查找）中训练不稳定、方差高，甚至无法可靠学习线性回归，而AR-LLMs在这些任务上表现稳定。这促使作者探索更优的掩码策略。

Method: 提出两种局部感知的块级模型：Jigsaw和Scatter。它们在块内注入从左到右的自回归归纳偏置（保持局部有序性），同时在块级别保留迭代精炼的扩散特性。Jigsaw在块内强制严格从左到右顺序，Scatter则更灵活地保留扩散规划优势。

Result: 在线性回归任务上，Jigsaw匹配了AR-LLM的稳定性；在图路径查找任务上，Scatter保留了扩散的规划优势；在数独任务上，标准MDMs已优于AR-LLMs，而Jigsaw仍保持强性能。标准随机掩码MDMs在三个任务上均表现出不同程度的不稳定性。

Conclusion: 标准随机掩码的MDMs（包括其块级变体）对于有序生成任务可能是次优的扩散LM实现，需要在扩散的灵活性与自回归的局部顺序偏置之间取得更好平衡，推动超越随机掩码的模型设计。

Original Abstract: Masked diffusion language models (MDMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to standard autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs), yet their optimization can be substantially less stable. We study blockwise MDMs and compare them with AR-LLMs on three controlled tasks that stress different aspects of structured generation: in-context linear regression, graph path-finding, and Sudoku solving. We find that standard random-masking MDMs fail to reliably learn linear regression, exhibit high variance training dynamics on graph path-finding, while outperforming AR-LLMs on Sudoku. To mitigate these instabilities, we propose two locality aware blockwise models, namely Jigsaw and Scatter, that inject left-to-right inductive bias by enforcing autoregressive locality within blocks while preserving iterative refinement at the block level. Empirically, Jigsaw matches AR-LLM stability on linear regression and remains strong on Sudoku, while Scatter retains diffusion's planning advantage on path-finding. Our results indicate that standard random-masking MDMs, even with blockwise variants, may be a suboptimal instantiation of diffusion LMs for ordered generation, motivating models beyond random masking.

中文摘要翻译: 掩码扩散语言模型（MDMs）最近成为标准自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的一种有前途的替代方案，但其优化过程可能非常不稳定。我们研究了块级MDMs，并在三个强调结构化生成不同方面的受控任务——上下文线性回归、图路径查找和数独求解——上将其与AR-LLMs进行比较。我们发现，标准随机掩码的MDMs无法可靠地学习线性回归，在图路径查找上表现出高方差的训练动态，而在数独上则优于AR-LLMs。为了缓解这些不稳定性，我们提出了两种局部感知的块级模型，即Jigsaw和Scatter，它们通过在块内强制执行自回归局部性来注入从左到右的归纳偏置，同时保留块级别的迭代精炼。实验表明，Jigsaw在线性回归上匹配了AR-LLM的稳定性，并在数独上保持强劲性能，而Scatter在路径查找上保留了扩散的规划优势。我们的结果表明，标准随机掩码的MDMs，即使是其块级变体，对于有序生成任务而言可能是一种次优的扩散LM实现，这促使我们探索超越随机掩码的模型。

### [60] [Transformer Approximations from ReLUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24878)
*Jerry Yao-Chieh Hu,Mingcheng Lu,Yi-Chen Lee,Han Liu*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将ReLU近似结果系统性地迁移到Softmax注意力机制上的方法，并给出了目标特定且经济高效的资源界限，最终在乘法、倒数计算和最大/最小原语上验证了该方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有工作多聚焦于通用近似能力（universal approximation）的证明，但缺乏针对特定目标函数的经济高效资源界限，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 提出了一套系统性配方（systematic recipe），将ReLU逼近结果转化为Softmax注意力机制下的逼近结果，并推导出目标特定（target-specific）且经济（economic）的资源界限。

Result: 在乘法、倒数计算以及最小/最大值原语上成功应用了该配方，得到了比通用近似更紧致的资源界限。

Importantly, it yields target-specific, economic resource bounds beyond universal approximation statements. We showcase the recipe on multiplication, reciprocal computation, and min/max primitives. These results provide new analytical tools for analyzing softmax transformer models.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提供了一套系统性方案，用于将ReLU近似结果迁移到Softmax注意力机制上。该方案覆盖了多种常见的近似目标。重要的是，它能够产生目标特定且经济高效的资源界限，超越了通用近似定理的范畴。我们以乘法、倒数计算以及最小/最大值原语为例展示了该方案。这些结果为分析Softmax Transformer模型提供了新的分析工具。

### [61] [Generative diffusion models for spatiotemporal influenza forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24913)
*Joseph Lemaitre,Justin Lessler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Influpaint，利用去噪扩散概率模型将流感季节编码为时空图像，通过条件生成（图像修复）方式实现传染病概率预测，在CDC FluSight挑战中取得与领先集成方法相当的预测精度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传染病预测对公共卫生规划至关重要，但现有机制模型和统计方法难以捕捉多模态不确定性及新兴趋势，亟需一种能够灵活建模复杂流行病动力学的概率预测框架。

Method: 将流感季节编码为时空图像（像素强度表示发病率），使用去噪扩散概率模型在真实监测轨迹与模拟轨迹混合数据集上学习疾病动力学分布，将预测任务建模为基于部分观测的条件生成（图像修复）问题。

Result: Influpaint能生成真实且多样的流行轨迹；回顾性评估中预测精度与领先集成方法相当；在2023-2025年美国CDC FluSight实时评估中精度逐季显著提升，2024-2025年预测高度准确但略微过度自信；30%真实+70%模拟数据的混合训练集效果最佳。

Conclusion: 扩散模型能够捕捉流感动力学中重要的时空结构，为传染病概率预测提供了一种灵活有效的框架。

Original Abstract: Forecasting infectious disease incidence can provide important information to guide public health planning, yet is difficult because epidemic dynamics are complex. Current mechanistic and statistical approaches often struggle to capture multimodal uncertainty or emergent trends. Influpaint adapts denoising diffusion probabilistic models to epidemic forecasting. By encoding influenza seasons as spatiotemporal images in which pixel intensity represents incidence, Influpaint learns a rich distribution of disease dynamics from a hybrid dataset of surveillance and simulated trajectories. Forecasting is formulated as a conditional generation (inpainting) task from partial observations. We show that Influpaint generates realistic, diverse epidemic trajectories and achieves forecast accuracy that is competitive with leading ensemble methods in retrospective evaluation. In real-time evaluation during the 2023--2025 U.S. CDC FluSight challenges, performance improved substantially across seasons, with highly accurate but somewhat overconfident projections in 2024--2025. The best performance was achieved with a training dataset containing 30% surveillance and 70% simulated trajectories. These results show that diffusion models can capture important spatiotemporal structure in influenza dynamics and provide a flexible framework for probabilistic infectious disease forecasting.

中文摘要翻译: 预测传染病发病率可为指导公共卫生规划提供重要信息，但由于流行病动力学的复杂性，这一任务十分困难。当前的机制模型和统计方法往往难以捕捉多模态不确定性或新兴趋势。Influpaint将去噪扩散概率模型应用于流行病预测。通过将流感季节编码为时空图像（其中像素强度表示发病率），Influpaint从真实监测轨迹和模拟轨迹的混合数据集中学习疾病动力学的丰富分布。预测被建模为基于部分观测的条件生成（图像修复）任务。我们表明，Influpaint能够生成真实且多样的流行轨迹，并在回顾性评估中达到与领先集成方法相当的预测精度。在2023-2025年美国CDC FluSight挑战赛的实时评估中，模型性能逐季显著提升，在2024-2025年预测高度准确但略微过度自信。使用包含30%真实监测数据与70%模拟数据的训练集取得了最佳性能。这些结果表明，扩散模型能够捕捉流感动力学中重要的时空结构，并为传染病概率预测提供了一种灵活的框架。

</details>

*Chandler Squires,Pradeep Ravikumar*

<details>

Motivation: 概念提取技术（如稀疏自编码器和转码器）在下游任务（如模型引导和遗忘）中被广泛应用，但其可识别性保证尚不明确，缺乏统一的理论理解。

Original Abstract: Techniques for concept extraction, such as sparse autoencoders and transcoders, aim to extract high-level symbolic concepts from low-level nonsymbolic representations. When these extracted concepts are used for downstream tasks such as model steering and unlearning, it is essential to understand their guarantees, or lack thereof. In this work, we present a unified theoretical framework for unsupervised concept extraction, in which we frame the task of concept extraction as identifying a generative model. We present a general meta-theorem for identifiability, which reduces the problem of establishing identifiability guarantees to the problem of characterizing the intersection of two sets. As we demonstrate on a range of widely-used approaches, this meta-theorem substantially simplifies the task of proving such guarantees, thus paving the way for the development of new, principled approaches for concept extraction.

中文摘要翻译: 概念提取技术（如稀疏自编码器和转码器）旨在从低层次的非符号化表示中提取高层次的符号化概念。当这些提取出的概念被用于模型引导和遗忘等下游任务时，理解其保证（或缺乏保证）至关重要。在本文中，我们提出了一个用于无监督概念提取的统一理论框架，将概念提取任务框架化为识别一个生成模型。我们提出了一个关于可识别性的通用元定理，该定理将建立可识别性保证的问题简化为刻画两个集合交集的问题。正如我们在多种广泛使用的方法上所展示的那样，该元定理大大简化了证明此类保证的任务，从而为开发新的、有原则的概念提取方法铺平了道路。

### [63] [Compute Aligned Training: Optimizing for Test Time Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24957)
*Adam Ousherovitch,Ambuj Tewari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出计算对齐训练（Compute Aligned Training），通过将训练目标与测试时推理策略对齐，解决标准微调与测试时计算之间的不匹配问题，显著提升LLM在测试时扩展的性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准后训练范式（SFT和RL）优化的是基础策略下单个样本的似然，这与依赖聚合或筛选输出的测试时流程存在不一致，导致训练与测试时的计算策略不匹配。

Method: 将推理策略概念化为对基础策略的算子，推导出新的损失函数，使得应用这些策略时性能最大化，并为SFT和RL在常见测试时策略下实例化这些损失函数。

Result: 实验证明该方法相比标准训练能显著提升测试时计算扩展的效果。

Conclusion: 计算对齐训练能够有效弥合训练与测试时计算之间的差距，为提升LLM测试时性能提供了新的训练范式。

Original Abstract: Scaling test-time compute has emerged as a powerful mechanism for enhancing Large Language Model (LLM) performance. However, standard post-training paradigms, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL), optimize the likelihood of individual samples under a base policy, creating a misalignment with test time procedures that rely on aggregated or filtered outputs. In this work, we propose Compute Aligned Training, which aligns training objectives with test-time strategies. By conceptualizing inference strategies as operators on the base policy, we derive new loss functions that maximize performance when said strategies are applied. We instantiate such loss functions for SFT and RL across common test time strategies. Finally, we provide empirical evidence that this training method substantially improves test time scaling over standard training.

中文摘要翻译: 扩展测试时计算已成为增强大型语言模型（LLM）性能的强大机制。然而，标准的后训练范式——监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）——优化的是基础策略下单个样本的似然，这与依赖聚合或筛选输出的测试时流程产生不匹配。在本文中，我们提出计算对齐训练（Compute Aligned Training），将训练目标与测试时策略对齐。通过将推理策略概念化为对基础策略的算子，我们推导出新的损失函数，使得在应用所述策略时性能最大化。我们针对常见的测试时策略，为SFT和RL实例化了这些损失函数。最后，我们提供的实验证据表明，该训练方法相较于标准训练显著改善了测试时计算扩展的效果。

### [64] [PolyKV: A Shared Asymmetrically-Compressed KV Cache Pool for Multi-Agent LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24971)
*Ishan Patel,Ishan Joshi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PolyKV 提出多推理智能体共享单个非对称压缩 KV 缓存池的系统，替代每个智能体独立分配 KV 缓存的范式，在 Llama-3-8B 上实现 97.7% 的 KV 缓存内存缩减，仅增加 0.57% 的困惑度退化。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的多智能体推理系统中，每个智能体独立维护一份 KV 缓存，导致内存开销随智能体数量线性增长，限制了并发规模和可扩展性。PolyKV 旨在通过共享压缩缓存池解决这一瓶颈。

Method: PolyKV 构建一个单次写入、多次读取的非对称压缩 KV 缓存池。Keys 采用 int8 (q8_0) 量化以保持 softmax 稳定性；Values 使用 TurboQuant MSE 压缩——先经快速 Walsh-Hadamard 变换 (FWHT) 旋转，再进行 3 比特 Lloyd-Max 量化（质心在 N(0,1) 上调优）。通过 HuggingFace DynamicCache 对象注入到 N 个独立智能体上下文中。

Result: 在两种模型规模（SmolLM2-1.7B-Instruct 和 Llama-3-8B-Instruct）、三种上下文长度（600-7,194 tokens）及最多 15 个并发智能体上评估，PolyKV 实现稳定 2.91× 压缩比；Llama-3-8B 上 15 个智能体共享 4K 上下文时，KV 缓存从 19.8 GB 降至 0.45 GB（减少 97.7%），困惑度仅增加 0.57%，平均 BERTScore F1 为 0.928。PPL 增量不随智能体数量增长，且随上下文长度增加而改善，在 1,851 个连贯 token 上逆转为 -0.26%。

Conclusion: PolyKV 证明了单共享有损压缩 KV 缓存池支持多读取器并发智能体访问的可行性，显著降低了多智能体推理的内存开销且性能损失极小，该组合方法在已有文献中尚未被报道。

Original Abstract: We present PolyKV, a system in which multiple concurrent inference agents share a single, asymmetrically compressed KV cache pool. Rather than allocating a separate KV cache per agent -- the standard paradigm -- PolyKV writes a compressed cache once and injects it into N independent agent contexts via HuggingFace DynamicCache objects. Compression is asymmetric: Keys are quantized at int8 (q8_0) to preserve softmax stability, while Values are compressed using TurboQuant MSE -- a Fast Walsh-Hadamard Transform (FWHT) rotation followed by 3-bit Lloyd-Max quantization with centroids tuned to N(0,1). We evaluate across two model scales (SmolLM2-1.7B-Instruct and Llama-3-8B-Instruct), three context lengths (600-7,194 tokens), and up to 15 concurrent agents. PolyKV achieves a stable 2.91x compression ratio across all configurations. On Llama-3-8B with 15 agents sharing a 4K-token context, PolyKV reduces KV cache memory from 19.8 GB to 0.45 GB -- a 97.7% reduction -- while maintaining only +0.57% perplexity degradation and a mean BERTScore F1 of 0.928. PPL delta does not grow with agent count and improves as context length increases, inverting to -0.26% at 1,851 coherent tokens. To our knowledge, no prior work combines a single shared, lossy-compressed KV pool with multi-reader concurrent agent access.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出 PolyKV，一个允许多个并发推理智能体共享单一非对称压缩 KV 缓存池的系统。PolyKV 并未遵循为每个智能体单独分配 KV 缓存的标准范式，而是将压缩缓存写入一次，并通过 HuggingFace DynamicCache 对象注入到 N 个独立智能体上下文中。压缩是非对称的：键（Keys）以 int8 (q8_0) 量化以保持 softmax 稳定性，而值（Values）则使用 TurboQuant MSE 进行压缩——这是一种快速 Walsh-Hadamard 变换（FWHT）旋转后接 3 比特 Lloyd-Max 量化的方法，其质心针对 N(0,1) 分布调优。我们在两种模型规模（SmolLM2-1.7B-Instruct 和 Llama-3-8B-Instruct）、三种上下文长度（600-7,194 tokens）以及最多 15 个并发智能体上进行了评估。PolyKV 在所有配置下均实现稳定的 2.91× 压缩比。在 Llama-3-8B 上，15 个智能体共享 4K-token 上下文时，PolyKV 将 KV 缓存内存从 19.8 GB 降至 0.45 GB——减少了 97.7%——同时仅造成 +0.57% 的困惑度退化和 0.928 的平均 BERTScore F1 值。困惑度增量不随智能体数量增长，且随上下文长度增加而改善，在 1,851 个连贯 token 上逆转为 -0.26%。据我们所知，尚无先前工作将单一共享有损压缩 KV 池与多读取器并发智能体访问相结合。

</details>


### [65] [Laplace-Bridged Randomized Smoothing for Fast Certified Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24993)
*Miao Lin,MD Saifur Rahman Mazumder,Feng Yu,Daniel Takabi,Rui Ning*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出拉普拉斯桥平滑（LBS），通过将高维输入空间的蒙特卡洛采样替换为低维概率空间的解析计算，在不需噪声增强训练的情况下显著降低随机平滑的认证成本，并在边缘设备上实现高达494倍加速。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 随机平滑（RS）在实际部署中面临两大瓶颈：(i) 依赖噪声增强训练才能获得有意义认证，增加了训练成本、降低了干净准确率，削弱了其作为真正后验防御的优势；(ii) 认证计算成本极高，每张输入需数万次带噪前向传播，阻碍了在资源受限边缘设备上的部署。

Method: 提出拉普拉斯桥平滑（LBS），对随机平滑进行解析重构，将高维输入空间的蒙特卡洛（MC）采样替换为低维概率空间中的高效计算。LBS保留了形式化鲁棒性保证，无需噪声增强训练，并大幅降低了认证负担。

Result: 在CIFAR-10和ImageNet上，LBS比RS获得更强的认证鲁棒性，且每样本认证成本降低近一个数量级。在NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano和Raspberry Pi 4上，LBS实现高达494倍加速，使得真实边缘设备上的认证部署成为可能。

Conclusion: LBS通过解析计算替代蒙特卡洛采样，有效解决了随机平滑在训练成本和认证效率上的双重瓶颈，为边缘设备的鲁棒性认证部署提供了实用方案，同时理论证明了其解析公式和证书的有效性。

Original Abstract: Randomized Smoothing (RS) offers formal $\ell_2$ guarantees for arbitrary base classifiers but faces two key practical bottlenecks: (i) it often relies on noise-augmented training to achieve nontrivial certificates, which increases training cost, can reduce clean accuracy, and weakens RS as a genuinely post-hoc defense; and (ii) certification is computationally expensive, typically requiring tens of thousands of noisy forward passes per input, which hinders deployment, especially on resource-constrained edge devices. To address both limitations, we propose Laplace-Bridged Smoothing (LBS), an analytic reformulation of RS that replaces high-dimensional input-space Monte Carlo (MC) sampling with efficient computations in a low-dimensional probability space. LBS preserves formal robustness guarantees without requiring noise-augmented training while substantially reducing certification burden. On CIFAR-10 and ImageNet, LBS attains stronger certified robustness than RS and reduces per-sample certification cost by nearly an order of magnitude. Notably, on NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano and Raspberry Pi 4, LBS achieves speedups of up to $494\times$, enabling practical certified deployment on real-world edge devices. Finally, we provide theoretical justification for the analytic formulation and certificate validity of LBS.

中文摘要翻译: 随机平滑（Randomized Smoothing, RS）为任意基分类器提供形式化的ℓ₂鲁棒性保证，但面临两个关键的实际瓶颈：(i) 为获得有意义的认证证书，通常依赖噪声增强训练，这不仅增加了训练成本，还可能降低干净准确率，并削弱了RS作为真正后验防御的优势；(ii) 认证过程计算开销巨大，每张输入通常需要数万次带噪前向传播，这阻碍了其在资源受限的边缘设备上的部署。为解决这两大限制，我们提出拉普拉斯桥平滑（Laplace-Bridged Smoothing, LBS），这是一种随机平滑的解析重构方法，将高维输入空间的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo, MC）采样替换为低维概率空间中的高效计算。LBS保留了形式化的鲁棒性保证，且无需噪声增强训练，同时大幅降低了认证负担。在CIFAR-10和ImageNet上，LBS获得了比RS更强的认证鲁棒性，并将每样本认证成本降低了近一个数量级。值得注意的是，在NVIDIA Jetson Orin Nano和Raspberry Pi 4上，LBS实现了高达494倍的加速，使实际边缘设备上的认证部署成为可能。最后，我们为LBS的解析公式和证书有效性提供了理论证明。

### [66] [Why Search When You Can Transfer? Amortized Agentic Workflow Design from Structural Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25012)
*Shiyi Du,Jiayuan Liu,Weihua Du,Yue Huang,Jiayi Li,Yingtao Luo,Xiangliang Zhang,Vincent Conitzer,Carl Kingsford*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SWIFT提出了一种将智能体工作流设计从逐任务迭代搜索转化为可复用结构先验的框架，通过对比分析历史搜索轨迹提取组合启发式与输出接口合约，在推理时单次LLM生成即可合成完整可执行工作流，在5个基准上超越SOTA搜索方法的同时将边际优化成本降低三个数量级。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有自动化智能体工作流设计依赖逐任务迭代搜索，计算成本极高且无法跨任务复用结构知识。作者观察到优化后的工作流收敛到少数领域特定的拓扑结构，表明组合搜索存在大量冗余，因此希望将工作流设计摊销为可复用的结构先验。

Method: SWIFT框架包含两个阶段：(1) 离线阶段：对源任务的搜索轨迹进行对比分析，蒸馏出组合启发式（compositional heuristics）和输出接口合约（output-interface contracts）作为结构先验；(2) 推理阶段：将结构先验与跨任务工作流演示（workflow demonstrations）拼接，通过单次LLM生成为未见目标任务合成完整可执行工作流，完全绕过迭代搜索。

Result: 在5个基准上超越SOTA基于搜索的方法，边际优化成本降低三个数量级；泛化到4个额外未见基准；成功从GPT-4o-mini迁移到Grok、Qwen、Gemma三种基础模型；消融实验表明将算子名称替换为随机字符串仍保留超过93%的平均性能，说明迁移的主要是拓扑结构而非表面语义。

Conclusion: 智能体工作流设计的核心可迁移知识在于拓扑结构而非具体算子语义，SWIFT通过结构先验与少量演示即可高效泛化，为大规模、低成本的工作流自动化设计提供了一条可行路径。

Original Abstract: Automated agentic workflow design currently relies on per-task iterative search, which is computationally prohibitive and fails to reuse structural knowledge across tasks. We observe that optimized workflows converge to a small family of domain-specific topologies, suggesting that this combinatorial search is largely redundant. Building on this insight, we propose SWIFT (Synthesizing Workflows via Few-shot Transfer), a framework that amortizes workflow design into reusable structural priors. SWIFT first distills compositional heuristics and output-interface contracts from contrastive analysis of prior search trajectories across source tasks. At inference time, it conditions a single LLM generation pass on these priors together with cross-task workflow demonstrations to synthesize a complete, executable workflow for an unseen target task, bypassing iterative search entirely. On five benchmarks, SWIFT outperforms the state-of-the-art search-based method while reducing marginal per-task optimization cost by three orders of magnitude. It further generalizes to four additional unseen benchmarks and transfers successfully from GPT-4o-mini to three additional foundation models (Grok, Qwen, Gemma). Controlled ablations reveal that workflow demonstrations primarily transfer topological structure rather than surface semantics: replacing all operator names with random strings still retains over 93% of the full system's average performance.

中文摘要翻译: 当前的自动化智能体工作流设计依赖于逐任务的迭代搜索，这种方法计算成本高昂，且无法跨任务复用结构知识。我们观察到优化后的工作流会收敛到少数领域特定的拓扑结构，这表明组合搜索在很大程度上是冗余的。基于这一发现，我们提出了SWIFT（通过少样本迁移合成工作流），这是一个将工作流设计摊销为可复用结构先验的框架。SWIFT首先通过对比分析源任务上先前搜索轨迹，蒸馏出组合启发式规则和输出接口合约。在推理时，它将这些先验与跨任务工作流演示相结合，通过单次LLM生成，为未见过的目标任务合成一个完整、可执行的工作流，完全绕过了迭代搜索。在五个基准测试上，SWIFT超越了最先进的基于搜索的方法，同时将边际逐任务优化成本降低了三个数量级。它还能泛化到另外四个未见过的基准测试，并成功从GPT-4o-mini迁移到另外三种基础模型（Grok、Qwen、Gemma）。受控消融实验表明，工作流演示主要迁移的是拓扑结构而非表面语义：将所有算子名称替换为随机字符串后，系统仍能保留超过93%的平均性能。

### [67] [Dynamic Regret for Online Regression in RKHS via Discounted VAW and Subspace Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25021)
*Dmitry B. Rokhlin,Georgiy A. Karapetyants*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）中在线回归问题的动态遗憾，通过有限维子空间逼近将折扣Vovk-Azoury-Warmuth方法推广到RKHS设置，并引入正交截断方法实现谱逼近，针对高斯核、解析点积核和Matérn核给出了动态遗憾界。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 将在线学习中基于动态遗憾的折扣VAW方法从有限维欧氏空间推广到无限维RKHS设置，解决核方法下动态回归的理论分析问题。

Method: (1) 通过有限维子空间逼近将Jacobsen & Cutkosky (2024)的折扣VAW方法迁移到RKHS；(2) 在同一子空间上运行基于几何网格折扣因子的VAW集成；(3) 引入正交截断方法：从核的特征展开出发，构造内积使特征函数正交归一，取前若干基函数张成有限维逼近空间；(4) 对高斯核、解析点积核使用显式特征展开，对一般核使用Mercer截断进行谱逼近。

Result: (1) 高斯核和解析点积核在快速衰减区域得到动态遗憾界；(2) Mercer截断根据特征值衰减速度提供快速和慢速两种动态遗憾界；(3) 核截面张成的子空间方法适用于Matérn核。

Conclusion: 通过有限维子空间逼近和正交截断方法，成功将折扣VAW动态遗憾框架扩展到RKHS，并针对多种核函数给出了理论保证。

Original Abstract: We study online regression with the square loss in a reproducing kernel Hilbert space under a dynamic regret criterion. The learner is compared with a time-varying comparator sequence, and the bounds depend on its path length in the RKHS norm. The proposed method transfers the finite-dimensional discounted Vovk--Azoury--Warmuth approach of Jacobsen \& Cutkosky (2024) to the RKHS setting by means of finite-dimensional subspace approximations. For a fixed subspace, we run a VAW-based ensemble of discounted VAW forecasters over a geometric grid of discount factors. The additional approximation error is controlled by the uniform projection error of kernel sections.
  We then introduce a general orthogonal truncation method: starting from a feature expansion of the kernel, we construct the associated RKHS by introducing an inner product that makes the feature functions orthonormal, and then use the spans of the first basis functions as finite-dimensional approximation spaces. The resulting subspace reduction is applied to several approximation schemes. Explicit feature expansions yield fast-regime bounds for Gaussian and analytic dot-product kernels. Mercer truncations provide a spectral approximation method and lead to dynamic regret bounds in fast and slow regimes, depending on the eigenvalue decay. Finally, we study subspaces spanned by kernel sections and apply this construction to Matérn kernels.

中文摘要翻译: 我们研究再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）中基于平方损失的在线回归问题，采用动态遗憾准则。学习器与时变比较器序列进行对比，边界依赖于该序列在RKHS范数下的路径长度。所提方法通过有限维子空间逼近，将Jacobsen & Cutkosky (2024)的有限维折扣Vovk-Azoury-Warmuth（VAW）方法迁移到RKHS设置。对于固定子空间，我们在几何网格折扣因子上运行基于VAW的折扣VAW预测器集成。额外的逼近误差通过核截面的均匀投影误差来控制。随后，我们引入一种通用的正交截断方法：从核的特征展开出发，通过引入使特征函数正交归一的内积来构造对应的RKHS，然后使用前若干基函数的张成空间作为有限维逼近空间。所得的子空间缩减方法被应用于多种逼近方案。显式特征展开为高斯核和解析点积核提供了快速衰减区间的动态遗憾界。Mercer截断提供了一种谱逼近方法，并根据特征值衰减速度得到快速和慢速两种动态遗憾界。最后，我们研究由核截面张成的子空间，并将这一构造应用于Matérn核。

### [68] [Null Measurability at the Symmetrization Interface in VC Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25028)
*Dhruv Gupta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在统计学习基础定理中，针对对称化证明所需的可测性条件进行了弱化：证明在Polish域上Borel参数化的概念类中，“坏事件”是解析集，因此在任何有限Borel测度的完备化下可测；并构造了严格分离的例子，证明了更弱的正则性水平在多种概念类构造下封闭，从而在可实现设定中减弱了PAC可学习性的可测性假设。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 近期工作为统计学习基本定理中的可测性施加了ghost-gap上确界的Borel可测性要求，本文指出在对称化证明实际使用的单侧ghost-gap界面处，这一要求过强，希望弱化该可测性假设。

Method: 利用描述集合论中的解析集理论和Choquet容量性质，分析坏事件的可测性；构造反例实现严格分离；证明在修补、固定与可数插值、纤维积融合等操作下的封闭性；在Lean 4中形式化主要结果。

Result: 1) 坏事件在任意有限Borel测度的完备化下可测，无需Borel可测；2) 构造了一个坏事件为null可测但非Borel的概念类，实现严格分离；3) 证明了弱正则性在多种自然的概念类构造子下封闭。

Conclusion: 本文弱化了有限VC维到PAC可学习性对称化证明路径所需的可测性假设，表明在可实现设定中更弱的可测性条件已足够。

Original Abstract: Recent work revisiting measurability in the fundamental theorem of statistical learning imposes Borel measurability of ghost-gap suprema. We show that, at the one-sided ghost-gap interface actually used by the standard symmetrization proof, this requirement is stronger than necessary. For any Borel-parameterized concept class on a Polish domain, the bad event "there exists a hypothesis whose ghost empirical error exceeds its training empirical error by at least ε/2" is analytic. By Choquet capacitability, it is therefore measurable in the completion of every finite Borel measure. We then construct a concept class whose bad event is null-measurable but not Borel, giving a strict separation from the Borel supremum condition. Finally, we prove closure under patching, fixed and countable interpolation, and fiber-product amalgamation, showing that the weaker regularity level is stable under natural concept-class constructors. In the realizable setting, where targets belong to the class and are measurable, these results weaken the measurability hypothesis needed by the symmetrization route from finite VC dimension to PAC learnability. The main results and the descriptive-set-theoretic infrastructure used by them are formalized in Lean 4.

中文摘要翻译: 近期重新审视统计学习基本定理中可测性的工作，对ghost-gap上确界施加了Borel可测性要求。本文证明，在标准对称化证明实际使用的单侧ghost-gap界面处，该要求比必要更强。对于Polish域上的任意Borel参数化概念类，坏事件“存在一个假设，其ghost经验误差超过其训练经验误差至少ε/2”是解析集。由Choquet容量性质，该事件因此在每个有限Borel测度的完备化中可测。我们进而构造了一个概念类，其坏事件是null可测的但不是Borel可测的，从而给出了与Borel上确界条件的严格分离。最后，我们证明了在修补、固定与可数插值以及纤维积融合操作下的封闭性，表明较弱的正则性水平在自然的概念类构造子下是稳定的。在可实现设定中（即目标属于该类且可测），这些结果弱化了从有限VC维到PAC可学习性的对称化路径所需的可测性假设。主要结果及其所使用的描述集合论基础设施已在Lean 4中形式化。

### [69] [CiteRadar: A Citation Intelligence Platform for Researcher Profiling and Geographic Visualization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25057)
*Chenxu Niu,Yiming Sun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CiteRadar是一个开源系统，只需输入Google Scholar用户ID，即可自动生成包含论文列表、引用详情、作者排名、统计摘要和交互式世界地图的结构化分析文件夹，解决了学者难以获取自身引用地理分布和社区结构的痛点。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有文献计量平台要么需要昂贵机构订阅，要么只提供聚合引用计数而缺乏细粒度作者元数据；学者在职业发展、基金申请和合作发现中日益需要了解自身引用的地理覆盖和社区结构，但缺乏易用的开源工具。

Method: CiteRadar集成了Google Scholar、OpenAlex、CrossRef、Semantic Scholar和OpenStreetMap Nominatim五个异构数据源，通过精心设计的五阶段流水线处理。关键技术贡献包括：(1) Scholar元字符串解析器，能处理Unicode非断行空格分隔符；(2) 两阶段作者消歧系统，利用停用词过滤后的机构名称相似性防止同名实体合并错误；(3) OpenAlex网页URL到API URL的转换修复，将城市级位置数据获取率从0%提升至约60%；(4) 对数刻度的交互式Folium世界地图，以自包含HTML文件呈现。

Result: 两阶段作者消歧系统被证明能消除高达9倍正确值的h-index归因错误；OpenAlex URL转换修复将带有城市级位置数据的作者记录比例从0%提升至约60%。

Conclusion: CiteRadar提供了一个低成本、易用、功能全面的开源学术影响力分析工具，填补了现有平台在开放、细粒度学者引用分析方面的空白。

Original Abstract: Understanding the geographic reach and community structure of one's scholarly citations is increasingly valuable for career development, grant applications, and collaboration discovery -- yet accessible tools for answering these questions remain scarce. Existing bibliometric platforms either require costly institutional subscriptions or expose only aggregate citation counts without granular per-author metadata. We present CiteRadar, an open-source system that accepts a single Google Scholar user identifier and automatically produces a structured output folder containing: the author's complete publication list, all retrieved citing papers with enriched author metadata, two ranked author tables (by citation frequency and by h-index), a plain-text statistical summary, and a self-contained interactive HTML world map -- all from a single command-line invocation. CiteRadar integrates five heterogeneous data sources -- Google Scholar, OpenAlex, CrossRef, Semantic Scholar, and OpenStreetMap Nominatim -- through a carefully engineered five-stage pipeline. Key technical contributions include: (1) a Scholar meta-string parser resilient to Unicode non-breaking-space separators, a pervasive but undocumented quirk in Scholar's HTML that silently corrupts venue and year fields when unhandled; (2) a two-stage author disambiguation system using stop-word-filtered institution name similarity to guard against the well-known same-name entity-merging failure mode in bibliometric databases, demonstrated to eliminate h-index attribution errors of up to 9x the correct value; (3) an OpenAlex web-URL to API-URL conversion fix that raises the fraction of author records with city-level location data from 0% to ~60%; and (4) a logarithmically-scaled interactive Folium world map with per-city researcher popups, rendered as a fully self-contained HTML file.

中文摘要翻译: 理解自身学术引用的地理覆盖范围和社区结构，对于职业发展、基金申请和合作发现越来越有价值——然而，能够回答这些问题的易用工具仍然稀缺。现有的文献计量平台要么需要昂贵的机构订阅，要么只暴露聚合引用计数而缺乏细粒度的作者元数据。我们提出CiteRadar，这是一个开源系统，它接受单个Google Scholar用户标识符，并自动生成一个结构化的输出文件夹，包含：该作者的完整出版物列表、所有检索到的引用论文及其丰富的作者元数据、两个排名作者表（按引用频率和h-index排序）、一份纯文本统计摘要，以及一个自包含的交互式HTML世界地图——所有这些仅通过一次命令行调用即可完成。CiteRadar集成了五个异构数据源——Google Scholar、OpenAlex、CrossRef、Semantic Scholar和OpenStreetMap Nominatim——通过精心设计的五阶段流水线。关键技术贡献包括：(1) 一种Scholar元字符串解析器，能够稳健处理Unicode非断行空格分隔符，这是Scholar HTML中一个普遍存在但未记录的特性，未经处理时会静默破坏期刊名称和年份字段；(2) 一个两阶段作者消歧系统，利用停用词过滤后的机构名称相似性来防范文献计量数据库中著名的同名实体合并故障模式，实验证明可消除高达9倍正确值的h-index归因错误；(3) 一个OpenAlex网页URL到API URL的转换修复，将具有城市级位置数据的作者记录比例从0%提升至约60%；以及(4) 一个对数刻度的交互式Folium世界地图，包含每城市研究者弹窗信息，以完全自包含的HTML文件形式呈现。

### [70] [Feasible-First Exploration for Constrained ML Deployment Optimization in Crash-Prone Hierarchical Search Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25073)
*Christian Lysenstøen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Thermal Budget Annealing（TBA）方法，将部署优化分解为可行域探索和模型引导利用两阶段，结合超时机制和子空间黑名单，在恶劣部署空间中高效发现有效配置，减少预算浪费。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 生产环境下的机器学习模型部署需要联合优化模型族、量化方案、运行时后端和服务配置，导致层次化混合变量搜索空间中大量配置无效（崩溃、超内存、违反延迟约束）。标准黑箱优化器在有效配置稀少时会将大量预算浪费在无效试验上，亟需一种在有限预算下优先探索可行域的方法。

Method: 提出Thermal Budget Annealing (TBA)，一种可行优先的探索流程：先通过探索阶段映射有效且可行的配置区域，再用这些信息热启动TPE。包含两个鲁棒机制：超时机制提前终止明显不可行的评估；子空间黑名单在重复失败后暂时屏蔽分类子空间。

Result: 在合成基准和真实GPU部署（5个预训练视觉模型×5种GPU目标：H100、A100、RTX 5080、L4、T4）上，TBA在严格约束下提升了模型族发现效率，相比冷启动TPE减少了预算浪费。

Conclusion: 将部署优化显式分解为探索阶段和利用阶段，结合超时与子空间黑名单机制，能有效应对恶劣部署空间中的无效配置问题，提升有限评估预算下的优化效率。

Original Abstract: Deploying machine learning models under production constraints requires joint optimization over model family, quantization scheme, runtime backend, and serving configuration. This induces a hierarchical mixed-variable search space in which many configurations are invalid: evaluations may crash, exceed memory limits, or violate latency constraints. Standard black-box optimizers such as Tree-structured Parzen Estimators (TPE) and constrained Bayesian optimization are effective when valid configurations are common, but they can spend a large fraction of a small evaluation budget on invalid or uninformative trials in hostile deployment spaces. This paper studies that regime and asks whether optimization should be decomposed into an explicit exploration stage followed by model-guided exploitation. We propose Thermal Budget Annealing (TBA), a feasible-first exploration procedure that maps valid and feasible regions before warm-starting TPE. The method includes two robustness mechanisms for hostile hardware: trial timeouts that abort clearly infeasible evaluations early, and subspace blacklisting that temporarily suppresses categorical subspaces after repeated failures. We also introduce DeployBench, a benchmark suite for deployment optimization with hierarchical structure, hidden crash zones, hard constraints, and unequal evaluation costs. On synthetic benchmarks and real GPU deployment with five pre-trained vision models across five GPU targets (NVIDIA H100, A100, RTX 5080, L4, and T4), the proposed hybrid improves model-family discovery under tight constraints while reducing wasted budget relative to cold-start TPE.

中文摘要翻译: 在生产约束下部署机器学习模型需要联合优化模型族、量化方案、运行时后端和服务配置。这引入了一个层次化的混合变量搜索空间，其中许多配置是无效的：评估可能崩溃、超出内存限制或违反延迟约束。当有效配置普遍存在时，标准的黑箱优化器（如树结构帕森估计器TPE和约束贝叶斯优化）是有效的，但在恶劣部署空间中，它们可能将少量评估预算中的很大一部分浪费在无效或信息量不足的试验上。本文研究这种场景，并探讨是否应将优化分解为显式探索阶段和后续模型引导的利用阶段。我们提出Thermal Budget Annealing (TBA)，一种可行优先的探索流程，在热启动TPE之前先映射有效且可行的区域。该方法包含针对恶劣硬件的两种鲁棒性机制：超时机制提前终止明显不可行的评估，以及子空间黑名单机制在重复失败后暂时屏蔽分类子空间。我们还引入了DeployBench，一个用于部署优化的基准测试套件，具有层次化结构、隐藏崩溃区域、硬约束和不平等的评估成本。在合成基准测试和真实GPU部署（五个预训练视觉模型在五种GPU目标（NVIDIA H100、A100、RTX 5080、L4和T4）上）中，所提出的混合方法在严格约束下提升了模型族的发现效率，同时相比冷启动TPE减少了预算浪费。

### [71] [Zero Shot Coordination for Sparse Reward Tasks with Diverse Reward Shapings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25076)
*Keenan Powell,Peihong Yu,Pratap Tokekar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对零样本协调（ZSC）问题中现有方法忽略合作伙伴奖励塑形差异的局限，提出使用四种选择算法随机化奖励塑形来训练集成方法，在Overcooked环境中将稀疏奖励提升62.2%-119.2%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有ZSC方法仅考虑训练智能体与未来合作伙伴具有相同奖励函数的情况，但实际中合作伙伴即使共享相同稀疏目标，也可能采用不同的奖励塑形方式，现有方法无法适应这种差异。

Method: 提出使用四种选择算法从随机奖励塑形中训练集成方法，使智能体能够适应具有相同稀疏奖励但不同奖励塑形的合作伙伴。

Result: 在Overcooked环境中的实验表明，与基线ZSC算法相比，在与具有相同稀疏奖励但不同奖励塑形的智能体合作时，稀疏奖励一致提升62.2%-119.2%。

Conclusion: 通过随机化奖励塑形训练的集成方法能有效解决实际场景中合作伙伴奖励塑形不一致的零样本协调问题，显著提升协调性能。

Original Abstract: Many Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) agents fail to adapt properly to cooperating with agents trained with the same objectives but different seeds, algorithms, or other training differences. This is the problem of Zero-Shot Coordination (ZSC), which focuses on training agents to cooperate well with unknown agents. ZSC has been studied for a variety of tabular cases and simple games such as Hanabi, achieving excellent results. However, existing solutions to ZSC only consider identical rewards for your trained agents and all future partners. This is not realistic for the trained agents, as they do not consider the problem of cooperating with agents that have identical sparse objectives but shape the rewards for those objectives in different manner. To address this issue, we show how to train an ensemble of methods using randomized reward shapings chosen using 4 selection algorithms. Experiments done on the Overcooked environment demonstrate consistent improvements of 62.2%-119.2% in sparse reward over baseline ZSC algorithms when playing with agents that have identical sparse rewards but different reward shapings.

中文摘要翻译: 许多多智能体强化学习（MARL）智能体无法很好地适应与训练目标相同但种子、算法或其他训练差异不同的智能体进行合作。这就是零样本协调（ZSC）问题，其核心是训练智能体与未知智能体有效协作。ZSC已在多种表格型案例和诸如Hanabi等简单游戏中得到研究，并取得了优异成果。然而，现有的ZSC解决方案仅考虑训练智能体与所有未来合作伙伴具有完全相同的奖励函数。这在实际场景中并不现实，因为训练后的智能体并未考虑与具有相同稀疏目标但采用不同方式塑造奖励的智能体进行合作的问题。为解决这一问题，我们展示了如何使用四种选择算法从随机奖励塑形中训练集成方法。在Overcooked环境中的实验表明，当与具有相同稀疏奖励但不同奖励塑形的智能体合作时，与基线ZSC算法相比，稀疏奖励一致提升了62.2%-119.2%。

### [72] [Knowledge Distillation Must Account for What It Loses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25110)
*Wenshuo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文认为知识蒸馏必须评估其损失，提出用蒸馏损失报告来衡量学生模型是否保留了教师模型的关键能力，而不仅仅是任务分数。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有蒸馏评估仅关注任务分数，忽略了不确定性、边界行为、过程可靠性等方面的损失，而这些损失在实际部署中至关重要。

Method: 识别当前评估中的保留假设，将蒸馏重新定义为教师行为的有损投影，综合现有证据形成蒸馏损失分类法，并提出场景特定的保留目标和蒸馏损失报告框架。

Result: 系统分类了度量之外的蒸馏损失类型，证明这些损失是具体、可重复且可测量的。

Original Abstract: This position paper argues that knowledge distillation must account for what it loses: student models should be judged not only by retained task scores, but by whether they preserve the teacher capabilities that make those scores reliable. This matters because distillation is increasingly used to turn large, often frontier models into deployable systems, yet headline metrics can hide losses in uncertainty, boundary behavior, process reliability, on-policy stability, grounding, privacy, safety, and diversity. We identify the retention assumption behind current evaluation and reframe distillation as a lossy projection of teacher behavior rather than a faithful copy. We then synthesize existing evidence into a taxonomy of off-metric distillation losses, showing that these losses are concrete, recurring, and measurable. To make the position actionable, we propose scenario-specific preservation targets and a Distillation Loss Statement that reports what was preserved, what was lost, and why the remaining losses are acceptable. The goal is not lossless distillation, but accountable distillation.

中文摘要翻译: 本立场论文认为，知识蒸馏必须评估其损失：学生模型不仅应根据保留的任务分数来判断，还应看它们是否保留了使这些分数可靠的教师能力。这一点至关重要，因为蒸馏越来越多地被用于将大型（通常是前沿）模型转化为可部署系统，然而标题指标可能隐藏不确定性、边界行为、过程可靠性、同策略稳定性、基础依据、隐私、安全和多样性方面的损失。我们识别了当前评估背后的保留假设，并将蒸馏重新定义为教师行为的有损投影而非忠实复制。然后，我们将现有证据综合为一个度量之外的蒸馏损失分类法，表明这些损失是具体、重复出现且可测量的。为使这一立场可操作，我们提出了场景特定的保留目标和一个蒸馏损失报告，该报告记录了保留了什么、失去了什么以及为什么剩余的损失是可接受的。目标不是无损蒸馏，而是可问责的蒸馏。

### [73] [Towards Unified Multi-task EEG Analysis with Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25131)
*Sicheng Dai,Kai Chen,Hongwang Xiao,Shan Yu,Qiwei Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MTEEG框架，通过任务特定的低秩适配（LoRA）模块，实现对预训练EEG模型在多任务场景下的高效联合适配，解决了不同任务间的参数冲突问题，在六个下游任务上超越单任务最优方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有EEG自监督预训练模型需要在每个下游任务上单独进行全参数微调，计算和存储成本高；EEG信号因采集设备、实验设置和受试者不同而存在显著异质性，多任务联合优化时任务间存在冲突。

Method: 提出MTEEG多任务EEG分析框架，为每个任务引入任务特定的低秩适配（LoRA）模块，通过解耦参数空间来缓解任务冲突；设计了三种变体以探索任务特异性和任务交互之间的权衡。

Original Abstract: Recent self-supervised pre-training methods for electroencephalogram (EEG) have shown promising results. However, the pre-trained models typically require full fine-tuning on each downstream task individually to achieve good performance. In practical applications involving multiple tasks, utilizing a separate model for each task is not ideal regarding computational and spatial cost. In this study, we go one step further and explore the simultaneous adaptation of a pre-trained model to multiple different tasks. The EEG signals exhibit significant heterogeneity due to their collection from various subjects using diverse devices and experimental setups, resulting in potential conflicts among different tasks that impede joint optimization. To tackle this challenge, we propose MTEEG, a multi-task EEG analysis framework which incorporates task-specific low-rank adaptation (LoRA) modules to disentangle the parameter space and alleviate task conflicts. To investigate the trade-off between task specification and interaction, we propose three variants of MTEEG that integrate the LoRA modules in different ways and evaluate them on six downstream tasks, demonstrating that MTEEG can surpass state-of-the-art single-task methods on the majority of metrics. MTEEG shows the potential of multi-task EEG analysis and promotes the development of general-purpose brain-computer interfaces in the future.

中文摘要翻译: 近期针对脑电图（EEG）的自监督预训练方法展现出令人鼓舞的结果。然而，预训练模型通常需要在每个下游任务上单独进行全参数微调才能获得良好性能。在涉及多个任务的实际应用中，为每个任务使用独立的模型在计算和存储成本方面并不理想。在本研究中，我们更进一步，探索将预训练模型同时适配到多个不同任务。EEG信号因来自不同受试者、使用不同设备和实验设置而呈现出显著的异质性，这导致不同任务之间存在潜在冲突，阻碍了联合优化。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了MTEEG——一个多任务EEG分析框架，该框架引入任务特定的低秩适配（LoRA）模块以解耦参数空间并缓解任务冲突。为了探究任务特异性和任务交互之间的权衡，我们提出了三种集成LoRA模块方式不同的MTEEG变体，并在六个下游任务上对其进行评估，结果表明MTEEG在大多数指标上能够超越最先进的单任务方法。MTEEG展示了多任务EEG分析的潜力，并推动了未来通用脑机接口的发展。

### [74] [Gradient-Direction Sensitivity Reveals Linear-Centroid Coupling Hidden by Optimizer Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25143)
*Yongzhong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现，对损失梯度进行SVD分解比AdamW更新更能揭示SED方向与LCH特征之间的耦合（从3-9倍提升至100-330倍）；多任务场景下梯度聚合是主要障碍，按任务分解可恢复诊断效果；因果干预表明约束注意力更新到任意秩3子空间可加速grokking约2.3倍，但SED-LCH耦合并非唯一因果路径，AdamW更新具有高度秩冗余性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有工作使用AdamW更新的SVD分解来诊断SED方向与LCH特征的耦合，但测量结果较弱（$\bar{R}_k \approx 3$--$9\times$）且存在任务依赖性，甚至在多任务场景下完全失效（$\bar{R}_k \leq 1$），需要探究更有效的诊断方法并理解其因果意义。

Method: 将SVD分解的对象从AdamW更新替换为损失梯度，按单任务和多任务（共享编码器）两种场景分别计算SED-LCH耦合强度；在多任务场景中进一步将梯度按任务分解后再进行SVD；通过因果干预实验，将注意力更新约束到秩3子空间（SED导出或随机）来观察对grokking速度的影响。

Result: 1）梯度SVD将耦合强度从3-9倍提升至100-330倍，消除任务依赖性；2）多任务场景中更新SVD失效（≤1倍），梯度SVD恢复至20-45倍；3）约束注意力更新到任意秩3子空间可加速grokking约2.3倍，但移除秩3分量无显著影响，说明AdamW更新具有高度秩冗余。

Conclusion: SED-LCH耦合是特征形成在参数空间中集中程度的强诊断指标，但其本身不是唯一的因果通路；在所用超参数下，自然全秩AdamW注意力更新是高度秩冗余的。

Original Abstract: We show that replacing the rolling SVD of AdamW updates with a rolling SVD of loss gradients changes the diagnostic by 1-2 orders of magnitude. Performing SVD on the loss gradient instead of the AdamW update increases the measured perturbative coupling between SED directions and Linear Centroid Hypothesis (LCH) features from $ \bar{R}_k \approx 3 $--$9\times$ to $100$--$330\times$ across four single-task modular arithmetic operations, eliminating the apparent operation dependence in the original measurement. On a multitask transformer with a shared encoder, update-based SED gives $ \bar{R}_k \leq 1 $ -- an apparent failure of the diagnostic -- while per-operation gradient-based SED recovers $ \bar{R}_k = 20 $--$45\times$ across all four operations. Gradient aggregation across competing tasks is the main obstruction; performing SVD on per-task gradients resolves it. A causal intervention shows that constraining attention updates to any rank-3 subspace (whether SED-derived or random) accelerates grokking by approximately $2.3\times$ across random seeds and operations, while removing the rank-3 component has negligible effect under proper gradient-projection methodology. The SED-LCH coupling is therefore a strong diagnostic of where feature formation concentrates in parameter space, but it is not a unique causal pathway: the natural full-rank AdamW attention update is highly rank-redundant under our hyperparameters.

中文摘要翻译: 本文表明，将AdamW更新的滚动SVD替换为损失梯度的滚动SVD，会使诊断结果改变1-2个数量级。对损失梯度而非AdamW更新进行SVD，使得在四个单任务模算术运算中，SED方向与线性质心假设（LCH）特征之间的测量扰动耦合从$\bar{R}_k \approx 3$--$9\times$提升至$100$--$330\times$，消除了原始测量中明显的操作依赖性。在具有共享编码器的多任务Transformer上，基于更新的SED诊断给出$\bar{R}_k \leq 1$——表现为诊断失效——而基于每个操作梯度的SVD在所有四个操作上恢复了$\bar{R}_k = 20$--$45\times$的耦合强度。竞争任务之间的梯度聚合是主要障碍；对每个任务的梯度分别进行SVD可以解决这一问题。因果干预实验表明，将注意力更新约束到任意秩3子空间（无论是SED导出的还是随机的）都能将grokking加速约2.3倍（跨随机种子和操作），而在正确的梯度投影方法下移除秩3分量几乎没有影响。因此，SED-LCH耦合是特征形成在参数空间中集中程度的强诊断指标，但它并非唯一的因果通路：在我们的超参数设置下，自然全秩AdamW注意力更新具有高度的秩冗余性。

### [75] [Prior-Aligned Data Cleaning for Tabular Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25154)
*Laure Berti-Equille*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出L2C2，首个将表格数据清洗建模为强化学习问题的深度RL框架，通过学习策略对清洗算子进行序列决策，最小化脏数据与表格基础模型（TFM）合成先验之间的分布差异，从而提升TFM在真实数据上的零样本精度与置信度校准。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 表格基础模型（TFM）在小表格数据上通过元学习合成数据生成过程取得了顶尖的零样本精度，但其上下文学习机制假设输入数据近似干净。真实数据中普遍存在的缺失值、异常值和重复值会导致先验不匹配，同时降低精度和置信度校准。静态预处理规则无法捕捉清洗算子间的复杂交互，因此需要一种序贯决策方法来解决这一先验对齐问题。

Method: 提出L2C2框架，将表格数据清洗建模为深度强化学习问题。通过一个学习到的策略对清洗算子进行序贯决策，以最小化脏数据与TFM合成先验之间的分布差距。其中提出了TFMAwareReward奖励函数，用于指导策略学习。

Result: 在10个OpenML基准数据集上的6组实验表明：1）七种奖励设计中有三种退化到平凡的清洗策略；2）提出的TFMAwareReward在4/10数据集上选择结构不同的流水线，在这些差异案例上取得更高的TabPFN精度（均值0.851 vs. 0.843；Wilcoxon p=0.063, n=4），且从未表现更差；3）参数化清洗动作在9/10数据集上改进了最佳流水线奖励（Wilcoxon p=0.004）；4）在单个源数据集上预训练的策略，在2000步微调检查点上超越从头训练，在所有三个保留数据集上全微调后提升高达28.8%，展示了跨数据集的先验对齐知识迁移能力。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明，先验对齐是TFM在真实表格数据上部署的一种原则性数据准备策略。

Original Abstract: Tabular Foundation Models (TFMs) achieve state-of-the-art zero-shot accuracy on small tabular datasets by meta-learning over synthetic data-generating processes -- making them highly attractive for practitioners who cannot afford large annotated corpora. However, their in-context learning mechanism assumes approximately clean inputs: missing values, outliers, and duplicates in the real-world data create a prior mismatch that degrades both accuracy and confidence calibration simultaneously. Correcting this mismatch requires sequential decisions over cleaning operators whose interactions no static preprocessing rule can anticipate -a natural fit for reinforcement learning~(RL). We introduce L2C2, the first deep RL framework framing tabular data cleaning as prior alignment: a learned policy sequences operators to minimize the distributional gap between dirty input and the TFM's synthetic prior. Six experiments on ten OpenML benchmark datasets establish: 1) three of seven reward designs collapse to degenerate trivial cleaning strategies -- principled reward engineering is scientifically non-trivial; 2) the novel TFMAwareReward reward we propose selects structurally distinct pipelines on 4/10 datasets and achieves higher TabPFN accuracy on those diverging cases (mean 0.851 vs. 0.843; Wilcoxon p=0.063, n=4) while never underperforming; 3) parameterized cleaning actions improve best-found pipeline reward on 9/10 datasets (Wilcoxon p=0.004); and 4) a policy pre-trained on one single source dataset exceeds scratch training at the 2,000-step fine-tuning checkpoint on all three held-out datasets (up to +28.8% after full fine-tuning) demonstrating cross-dataset transfer of prior-alignment knowledge. These findings establish that prior alignment is a principled data preparation strategy for TFM deployment on real-world tabular data.

中文摘要翻译: 表格基础模型（TFM）通过在合成数据生成过程上进行元学习，在小表格数据集上达到了最先进的零样本精度——这使得它们对无法负担大型标注语料库的从业者极具吸引力。然而，它们的上下文学习机制假设输入数据近似干净：真实数据中的缺失值、异常值和重复值造成了先验不匹配，同时降低了精度和置信度校准。纠正这种不匹配需要对清洗算子进行序贯决策，而任何静态预处理规则都无法预见到这些算子之间的交互——这自然适合强化学习（RL）。我们提出了L2C2，这是第一个将表格数据清洗建模为先验对齐的深度强化学习框架：一个学习到的策略对算子进行序贯决策，以最小化脏数据与TFM合成先验之间的分布差距。在10个OpenML基准数据集上的六组实验表明：1）七种奖励设计中有三种退化为平凡的清洗策略——原则性的奖励工程在科学上是非平凡的；2）我们提出的新型TFMAwareReward奖励在4/10的数据集上选择了结构不同的流水线，并在这些差异案例上取得了更高的TabPFN精度（均值0.851 vs. 0.843；Wilcoxon p=0.063, n=4），且从未表现更差；3）参数化清洗动作在9/10数据集上改进了最佳流水线奖励（Wilcoxon p=0.004）；4）在单个源数据集上预训练的策略，在2000步微调检查点上超越从头训练，在所有三个保留数据集上经过完整微调后提升高达28.8%，展示了跨数据集的先验对齐知识迁移能力。这些发现表明，先验对齐是TFM在真实表格数据上部署的一种原则性数据准备策略。

### [76] [Accurate and Robust Generative Approach for Overcoming Data Sparsity and Imbalance in Landslide Modeling with A Tabular Foundation Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25159)

Original Abstract: Landslide investigation relies on sufficient and well-balanced observational data influenced by geological, hydrological, and anthropogenic factors. Here, we propose an accurate and robust approach for generating multi-feature landslide datasets by utilizing a tabular foundation model. ### [77] [Shearlet Neural Operators for Anisotropic-Shock-Dominated and Multi-scale parametric partial differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25181)
*Fabio Pereira dos Santos,Julio de Castro Vargas Fernandes,Adriano Mauricio de Almeida Cortes*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出剪切波神经算子（SNO），用剪切波变换替代傅里叶变换作为神经算子的核心表示，在保持谱计算效率的同时提升对各项异性结构、尖峰梯度和间断特征的学习能力，在多个PDE基准上优于傅里叶神经算子。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的傅里叶神经算子（FNO）依赖全局傅里叶表示，在解析各项异性结构、尖峰梯度以及冲击主导和多尺度场景中的空间局部间断时效率低下，亟需一种能更好表征这些特征的神经算子架构。

Method: 提出剪切波神经算子（SNO），将FNO中的傅里叶变换替换为剪切波变换。剪切波具有方向性、多尺度性和空间局部性，能够近最优稀疏逼近各项异性特征（如边缘、锋面和冲击波）。模型在剪切波域中学习并通过逆变换重建预测，既保留了谱计算效率，又改善了局部性和方向选择性。

Result: 在七个基准PDE系列（包括强各项异性平流、各项异性扩散和具有直线、弯曲、交互、螺旋及多边形冲击结构的非线性守恒律）上，SNO在预测精度和特征保真度上均一致优于FNO基线，在各项异性和间断主导的场景中提升最为显著。

Conclusion: 剪切波神经算子能够有效克服傅里叶神经算子在处理各项异性和不连续PDE解时的局限，是一种更具表达力的神经算子架构。

Original Abstract: Neural operators have emerged as powerful data-driven surrogates for learning solution operators of parametric partial differential equations (PDEs). However, widely used Fourier Neural Operators (FNOs) rely on global Fourier representations, which can be inefficient for resolving anisotropic structures, sharp gradients, and spatially localized discontinuities that arise in shock-dominated and multiscale regimes. To address these limitations, we introduce the Shearlet Neural Operator (SNO), a neural operator architecture that replaces the Fourier transform with a shearlet-based representation. Shearlets offer directional, multiscale, and spatially localized atoms with near-optimal sparse approximation of anisotropic features, providing an inductive bias aligned with PDE solutions containing edges, fronts, and shocks. SNO learns in the shearlet domain and reconstructs predictions via the inverse transform, retaining efficient spectral computation while improving locality and directional selectivity. Across seven benchmark PDE families, including strongly anisotropic advection, anisotropic diffusion, and nonlinear conservation laws with straight, curved, interacting, spiral, and polygonal shock structures, SNO consistently improves predictive accuracy and feature fidelity over FNO baselines, with the largest gains observed in anisotropic and discontinuity-dominated settings.

中文摘要翻译: 神经算子已成为学习参数化偏微分方程（PDE）解算子的强大数据驱动替代方案。然而，广泛使用的傅里叶神经算子（FNO）依赖于全局傅里叶表示，这在解析冲击主导和多尺度场景中出现的各向异性结构、尖峰梯度和空间局部间断时效率低下。为解决这些局限，我们提出了剪切波神经算子（SNO），这是一种将傅里叶变换替换为基于剪切波表示的神经算子架构。剪切波具有方向性、多尺度性和空间局部化的原子，能够对各项异性特征进行近最优稀疏逼近，为包含边缘、锋面和冲击波的PDE解提供了归纳偏置。SNO在剪切波域中学习并通过逆变换重建预测，在保留高效谱计算的同时改善了局部性和方向选择性。在七个基准PDE系列上，包括强各项异性平流、各项异性扩散以及具有直线、弯曲、交互、螺旋和多边形冲击结构的非线性守恒律，SNO在预测精度和特征保真度上均一致优于FNO基线，其中在各项异性和间断主导的场景中提升最为显著。

</details>


### [78] [Knowledge-Data Dually Driven Paradigm for Accurate Landslide Susceptibility Prediction under Data-Scarce Conditions Using Geomorphic Priors and Tabular Foundation Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25196)

### [79] [DiRe-RAPIDS: Topology-faithful dimensionality reduction at scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25209)
*Alexander Kolpakov,Igor Rivin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文指出UMAP和t-SNE等降维方法会记忆噪声并扭曲全局拓扑结构，提出基于带噪流形的拓扑保真度基准，并通过DiRe方法在保持分类性能的同时显著提升拓扑结构的保留能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有降维方法（如UMAP和t-SNE）使用局部邻域目标函数，会保留采样噪声并扭曲全局拓扑结构（如产生虚假的环和孤立连通分量），而标准局部指标无法惩罚这种噪声记忆行为。

Method: 1) 构建基于已知同调的带噪流形的拓扑保真度基准；2) 据此调优DiRe方法；3) 寻找Pareto最优配置，在分类任务上匹配或超越GPU加速的UMAP，同时在压力测试中恢复精确的第一Betti数。

Result: 在723K篇arXiv论文嵌入上，DiRe在相近运行时间内保留的拓扑结构是UMAP的3-4倍；在压力测试中能恢复精确的第一Betti数；分类性能与GPU加速的UMAP相当或更优。

Conclusion: 通过引入拓扑保真度基准并调优DiRe，可以在不牺牲分类性能的前提下，大幅提升降维结果对数据真实拓扑结构的保留能力，克服了传统局部目标方法记忆噪声的缺陷。

Original Abstract: Dimensionality reduction methods such as UMAP and t-SNE are central tools for visualising high-dimensional data, but their local-neighborhood objectives can preserve sampling noise while distorting global topology. We show that standard local metrics reward this noise memorisation: top-performing embeddings invent cycles and disconnected islands absent from the data. We introduce a topology-faithfulness benchmark based on noisy manifolds with known homology, tune DiRe against it, and find Pareto-optimal configurations that match or beat GPU-accelerated UMAP on classification while recovering exact first Betti numbers on stress tests. On 723K arXiv paper embeddings, DiRe preserves 3-4 times more topological structure than UMAP at comparable wall-clock.

中文摘要翻译: UMAP和t-SNE等降维方法是可视化高维数据的核心工具，但其局部邻域目标函数在保留采样噪声的同时，会扭曲全局拓扑结构。我们证明标准局部指标会奖励这种噪声记忆：表现最佳的嵌入会发明数据中不存在的环和孤立连通分量。我们引入一个基于已知同调的带噪流形的拓扑保真度基准，据此调优DiRe方法，并找到Pareto最优配置——在分类任务上匹配或超越GPU加速的UMAP，同时在压力测试中恢复精确的第一Betti数。在723K篇arXiv论文嵌入上，DiRe在相近运行时间内保留的拓扑结构是UMAP的3-4倍。

### [80] [VLM Judges Can Rank but Cannot Score: Task-Dependent Uncertainty in Multimodal Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25235)
*Divake Kumar,Sina Tayebati,Devashri Naik,Ranganath Krishnan,Amit Ranjan Trivedi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文首次系统性地研究将共形预测应用于视觉-语言模型（VLM）作为自动评测器的可靠性问题，通过仅利用分数token的对数概率将点估计分数转化为校准的预测区间，揭示了评测不确定性高度依赖任务类型，并发现了排名-评分解耦这一标准指标无法捕捉的失效模式。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 视觉-语言模型被广泛用作多模态系统的自动评测器，但其输出的分数缺乏可靠性指示。现有方法无法量化评测结果的不确定性，亟需一种无需重新训练、分布无关的校准方法。

Method: 采用共形预测（conformal prediction）框架，仅利用评测模型输出分数token的对数概率（score-token log-probabilities），将点估计分数转换为校准的预测区间，无需重新训练模型。

Result: 1. 评测不确定性高度任务依赖：美学和自然图像任务的区间覆盖约40%的分数范围，而图表和数学推理任务扩大到约70%。2. 发现排名-评分解耦（ranking-scoring decoupling）失效模式：评测器排序相关性高但区间宽且无信息量，即能正确排序但无法分配可靠的绝对分数。3. 区间宽度主要受任务难度和标注质量驱动：在干净、多标注者的字幕基准上，相同评测器和方法的区间宽度可缩小4.5倍。

Conclusion: 共形预测能够为VLM评测器提供校准的不确定性估计，但评测可靠性因任务而异；标准排序指标不足以衡量评测可靠性，需结合预测区间宽度等不确定性指标；提升标注质量和控制任务难度可显著缩小不确定性区间。

Original Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly used as automated judges for multimodal systems, yet their scores provide no indication of reliability. We study this problem through conformal prediction, a distribution-free framework that converts a judge's point score into a calibrated prediction interval using only score-token log-probabilities, with no retraining. We present the first systematic analysis of conformal prediction for VLM-as-a-Judge across 3 judges and 14 visual task categories. Our results show that evaluation uncertainty is strongly task-dependent: intervals cover ~40% of the score range for aesthetics and natural images but expand to ~70% for chart and mathematical reasoning, yielding a quantitative reliability map for multimodal evaluation. We further identify a failure mode not captured by standard evaluation metrics, ranking-scoring decoupling, where judges achieve high ranking correlation while producing wide, uninformative intervals, correctly ordering responses but failing to assign reliable absolute scores. Finally, we show that interval width is driven primarily by task difficulty and annotation quality, i.e., the same judge and method yield 4.5x narrower intervals on a clean, multi-annotator captioning benchmark. Code: https://github.com/divake/VLM-Judge-Uncertainty

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言模型（VLM）越来越多地被用作多模态系统的自动评测器，但其评分无法提供可靠性指示。本文通过共形预测研究这一问题，这是一种分布无关的框架，仅利用评分token的对数概率，无需重新训练，即可将评测器的点估计分数转换为校准的预测区间。我们首次对VLM作为评测器的共形预测进行了系统性分析，涵盖3个评测器和14个视觉任务类别。结果表明，评测不确定性强烈依赖于任务：美学和自然图像任务的区间覆盖约40%的分数范围，而图表和数学推理任务则扩大到约70%，从而为多模态评测提供了一张量化的可靠性地图。我们进一步发现了一种标准评测指标无法捕捉的失效模式——排名-评分解耦，即评测器在获得高排序相关性的同时产生宽且无信息量的区间，能够正确地对响应排序但无法分配可靠的绝对分数。最后，我们证明区间宽度主要由任务难度和标注质量驱动：在干净、多标注者的字幕基准上，相同的评测器和方法产生的区间宽度可缩小4.5倍。代码：https://github.com/divake/VLM-Judge-Uncertainty

Method: 基于Follow-The-Perturbed-Leader（FTPL）预测方法，提出名为“Counting Asleep Times”（计数休眠时间）的新型损失估计技术，针对完全信息、半条带以及中间态的受限信息三种学习设置设计算法。

Original Abstract: Most work on sequential learning assumes a fixed set of actions that are available all the time. ### [82] [Optimization-Free Topological Sort for Causal Discovery via the Schur Complement of Score Jacobians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25295)
*Rui Wu,Hong Xie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种解耦的因果发现范式，通过Score-Schur拓扑排序（SSTS）算法直接从无约束生成模型中提取拓扑顺序，将非凸优化瓶颈转化为统计分数估计问题，在d=1000的非线性图上实现了可扩展的因果结构分析。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的连续因果发现方法通常将表示学习与非凸无环性惩罚耦合，导致求解器陷入局部最优且在高维场景下可扩展性受限。本文旨在通过解耦策略突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 提出Score-Schur拓扑排序（SSTS）算法，利用Score-Jacobian信息矩阵（SJIM）的Schur补将无环性约束转化为代数操作；针对非线性系统引入Block-SSTS以压缩提取深度并控制结构误差。

Result: SSTS能够对d=1000的非线性图进行因果结构分析；实验表明，一旦绕过非凸优化瓶颈，连续因果发现的结构保真度受限于全局分数几何的有限样本估计方差。

Conclusion: 本文将因果图提取简化为矩阵运算，将可扩展的因果发现从约束优化问题重新定义为统计估计挑战。

Original Abstract: Continuous causal discovery typically couples representation learning with structural optimization via non-convex acyclicity penalties, which subjects solvers to local optima and restricts scalability in high-dimensional regimes. We propose a decoupled paradigm that shifts the causal discovery bottleneck from non-convex optimization to statistical score estimation. We introduce the Score-Schur Topological Sort (SSTS), an algorithm that extracts topological order directly from unconstrained generative models, bypassing constrained structure optimization. We establish that the causal hierarchy leaves a geometric signature within the score function: iterative graph marginalization is mathematically equivalent to computing the Schur complement of the Score-Jacobian Information Matrix (SJIM) under linear conditions. This translates the acyclicity constraint into an algebraic procedure with a dominant cost of O(d^3) operations. For non-linear systems, we formulate the expectation gap of Schur marginalization and introduce Block-SSTS to compress extraction depth, bounding structural error. Empirically, SSTS allows causal structural analysis on non-linear graphs up to d=1000. At this scale, our framework indicates that once the non-convex optimization bottleneck is mathematically bypassed, the structural fidelity of continuous causal discovery is bounded by the finite-sample estimation variance of the global score geometry. By reducing graph extraction to matrix operations, this work reframes scalable causal discovery from a constrained optimization problem to a statistical estimation challenge.

中文摘要翻译: 连续因果发现通常将表示学习与基于非凸无环性惩罚的结构优化耦合在一起，这使得求解器容易陷入局部最优，并在高维场景下限制了可扩展性。我们提出了一种解耦范式，将因果发现的瓶颈从非凸优化转向统计分数估计。我们引入了分数-舒尔拓扑排序（SSTS）算法，该算法直接从无约束生成模型中提取拓扑顺序，绕过了约束结构优化。我们证明了因果层次结构在分数函数中留下了几何印记：在线性条件下，迭代图边缘化在数学上等价于计算分数-雅可比信息矩阵（SJIM）的舒尔补。这将无环性约束转化为一个代数过程，其主要计算代价为O(d³)操作。对于非线性系统，我们推导了舒尔边缘化的期望间隙，并引入了Block-SSTS来压缩提取深度，从而限定了结构误差。实验结果表明，SSTS能够在d=1000的非线性图上进行因果结构分析。在此规模下，我们的框架表明，一旦从数学上绕过了非凸优化瓶颈，连续因果发现的结构保真度就受限于全局分数几何的有限样本估计方差。通过将图提取简化为矩阵运算，本文将可扩展的因果发现从约束优化问题重新定义为统计估计挑战。

### [83] [RCProb: Probabilistic Rule Extraction for Efficient Simplification of Tree Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25304)
*Josue Obregon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出RCProb，一种基于概率统计的规则提取方法，通过对RuleCOSI+进行概率论重新建模，利用Dirichlet平滑类先验和Beta平滑条件似然结合朴素贝叶斯公式估计规则统计量，避免了重复扫描训练数据，在33个基准数据集上将运行时间减少约22倍，同时保持竞争性的预测性能并生成更紧凑的规则集。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 树集成模型随树数量增长变得越来越难以解释，已有的规则提取方法RuleCOSI+虽然能生成准确且可解释的规则集，但其依赖对训练数据的重复经验频率计数来估计规则置信度，在大数据集上计算成本高昂。

Method: 提出RCProb方法，使用Dirichlet平滑的类先验和Beta平滑的条件似然，通过朴素贝叶斯公式结合来估计规则统计量，替代了RuleCOSI+中重复扫描数据集的频率计数方式，从而降低规则提取的计算成本。

Result: 在33个基准数据集上的实验表明，与RuleCOSI+相比，RCProb保持了具有竞争力的预测性能，运行时间减少约22倍，且平均生成更紧凑的规则集。

Conclusion: RCProb作为一种概率论重制的规则提取方法，能显著降低计算开销，同时保持预测性能和可解释性，为大规模树集成模型的规则提取提供了一种高效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Tree ensembles are widely used in industrial machine learning due to their strong predictive performance and efficient training procedures. However, as the number of trees in an ensemble grows, the resulting models become increasingly difficult for humans to interpret. To address this limitation, explainable artificial intelligence (XAI) studies methods that generate interpretable models capable of explaining complex predictors. One approach consists of extracting decision rules from tree ensembles while attempting to preserve the predictive performance of the original model. In previous work, we introduced RuleCOSI+, a greedy heuristic algorithm for extracting compact rule-based models from tree ensembles. Although RuleCOSI+ produces accurate and interpretable rule sets, it relies on repeated empirical frequency counting over the training data to estimate rule confidence, which becomes computationally expensive for large datasets. In this paper, we propose RCProb, a probabilistic reformulation of RuleCOSI+ designed to reduce the computational cost of rule extraction. RCProb estimates rule statistics using Dirichlet-smoothed class priors and Beta-smoothed condition likelihoods combined through a Naive Bayes formulation, avoiding repeated dataset scans. Experiments on 33 benchmark datasets show that RCProb maintains competitive predictive performance while reducing runtime by approximately $22\times$ compared with RuleCOSI+, while producing more compact rule sets on average.

中文摘要翻译: 树集成因其强大的预测性能和高效的训练过程而广泛应用于工业机器学习。然而，随着集成中树的数量增长，生成的模型对人类而言变得越来越难以解释。为解决这一局限性，可解释人工智能（XAI）研究能够生成可解释模型以解释复杂预测器的方法。其中一种方法是从树集成中提取决策规则，同时试图保持原始模型的预测性能。在先前工作中，我们引入了RuleCOSI+，一种从树集成中提取紧凑规则模型的贪婪启发式算法。尽管RuleCOSI+能生成准确且可解释的规则集，但它依赖对训练数据的重复经验频率计数来估计规则置信度，这在大型数据集上计算成本高昂。本文提出RCProb，一种对RuleCOSI+的概率论重制公式，旨在降低规则提取的计算成本。RCProb使用Dirichlet平滑的类先验和Beta平滑的条件似然，通过朴素贝叶斯公式结合来估计规则统计量，避免了重复扫描数据集。在33个基准数据集上的实验表明，与RuleCOSI+相比，RCProb在保持竞争性预测性能的同时，运行时间减少约22倍，且平均生成更紧凑的规则集。

### [84] [QFlash: Bridging Quantization and Memory Efficiency in Vision Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25306)
*Sehyeon Oh,Yongin Kwon,Jemin Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: QFlash提出了一种端到端的整数FlashAttention设计，通过全整数域softmax和单Triton内核实现，在ViT、DeiT和Swin模型上取得最高8.69倍加速，能耗降低18.8%，且不损失Top-1精度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: FlashAttention通过分块（tiling）提升了效率，但其在线softmax依赖浮点运算保证数值稳定性，导致难以实现全量化。论文识别出整数FlashAttention的三个主要障碍：分块累加时的尺度爆炸、GPU上低效的基于移位的指数运算、以及整数比较需要统一尺度的量化粒度约束。

Method: 提出QFlash，一种端到端的整数FlashAttention设计，在整数域中完全执行softmax，并以单个Triton内核运行。

Result: 在ViT、DeiT和Swin模型的七个注意力任务上，QFlash相比I-ViT最高提升6.73倍速度，在Swin上最高提升8.69倍；相比FP16 FlashAttention能耗降低18.8%；在ViT/DeiT上不损失Top-1精度，在Swin上在逐张量量化下保持竞争力。

Conclusion: QFlash成功实现了整数化的FlashAttention，在显著提升速度和降低能耗的同时保持了模型精度，证明了全整数域注意力计算的可行性。

Original Abstract: FlashAttention improves efficiency through tiling, but its online softmax still relies on floating-point arithmetic for numerical stability, making full quantization difficult. We identify three main obstacles to integer-only FlashAttention: (1) scale explosion during tile-wise accumulation, (2) inefficient shift-based exponential operations on GPUs, and (3) quantization granularity constraints requiring uniform scales for integer comparison. To address these challenges, we propose \textit{QFlash}, an end-to-end integer FlashAttention design that performs softmax entirely in the integer domain and runs as a single Triton kernel. On seven attention workloads from ViT, DeiT, and Swin models, QFlash achieves up to 6.73$\times$ speedup over I-ViT and up to 8.69$\times$ speedup on Swin, while reducing energy consumption by 18.8\% compared to FP16 FlashAttention, without sacrificing Top-1 accuracy on ViT/DeiT and remaining competitive on Swin under per-tensor quantization. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/EfficientCompLab/qflash.

中文摘要翻译: FlashAttention通过分块（tiling）提升了效率，但其在线softmax仍然依赖浮点运算来保证数值稳定性，这使得全量化变得困难。我们识别出整数FlashAttention的三个主要障碍：（1）分块累加过程中的尺度爆炸问题，（2）GPU上低效的基于移位的指数运算，（3）量化粒度约束要求整数比较使用统一尺度。为解决这些挑战，我们提出\textit{QFlash}，一种端到端的整数FlashAttention设计，它在整数域中完全执行softmax，并以单个Triton内核运行。在来自ViT、DeiT和Swin模型的七个注意力任务上，QFlash相比I-ViT实现了最高6.73倍的加速，在Swin上最高实现8.69倍加速，同时相比FP16 FlashAttention降低了18.8%的能耗，且在逐张量量化下，ViT/DeiT的Top-1精度没有损失，Swin上保持竞争力。我们的代码开源在https://github.com/EfficientCompLab/qflash。

### [85] [VAE-Inf: A statistically interpretable generative paradigm for imbalanced classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25334)
*Hongfei Wu,Ruijian Han,Yancheng Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一个两阶段框架VAE-Inf，将深度生成模型（VAE）与统计假设检验相结合，用于极端不平衡分类。第一阶段仅用多数类训练VAE构建参考分布，第二阶段通过分布感知损失微调解码器实现判别分类，并引入基于投影的评分实现无分布校准的类型-I错误控制。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统不平衡分类方法在少数类样本极度稀缺时，难以获得稳健的判别边界，且缺乏可靠的错误控制机制。现有方法在生成建模与判别分类之间缺少有效的桥梁。

Method: 提出VAE-Inf两阶段框架：(1) 第一阶段，仅用多数类样本训练变分自编码器（VAE），通过Wasserstein重心聚合潜在后验分布，构建全局高斯参考模型；(2) 第二阶段，利用少量少数类样本微调解码器，引入分布感知损失（基于方差归一化投影统计量）实现类别间概率分离；(3) 推理时采用基于投影的评分，可解释为假设检验，实现无分布校准的有限样本类型-I错误控制。

Result: 在多个真实世界基准数据集上的大量实验表明，该框架在性能上达到了与现有方法竞争的水平，同时具备了精确的有限样本类型-I错误控制能力。

Conclusion: VAE-Inf成功弥合了生成建模与判别分类之间的鸿沟，在极端不平衡场景下既能有效分类，又能提供具有统计可解释性的错误控制，且不依赖严格的参数假设。

Original Abstract: Imbalanced classification remains a pervasive challenge in machine learning, particularly when minority samples are too scarce to provide a robust discriminative boundary. In such extreme scenarios, conventional models often suffer from unstable decision boundaries and a lack of reliable error control. To bridge the gap between generative modeling and discriminative classification, we propose a two-stage framework \textbf{VAE-Inf} that integrates deep representation learning with statistically interpretable hypothesis testing. In the first stage, we adopt a one-class modeling perspective by training a variational autoencoder (VAE) exclusively on majority-class data to capture the underlying reference distribution. The resulting latent posteriors are aggregated via a Wasserstein barycenter to construct a global Gaussian reference model, providing a geometrically principled baseline for the majority class. In the second stage, we transform this generative foundation into a discriminative classifier by fine-tuning the encoder with limited minority samples. This is achieved through a novel distribution-aware loss that enforces probabilistic separation between classes based on variance-normalized projection statistics. For inference, we introduce a projection-based score that admits a natural hypothesis testing interpretation, allowing for a distribution-free calibration procedure. This approach yields exact finite-sample control of the Type-I error (false positive rate) without relying on restrictive parametric assumptions. Extensive experiments on diverse real-world benchmarks demonstrate that our framework achieves competitive performance against other approaches. The codes are available upon request.

中文摘要翻译: 不平衡分类仍然是机器学习中一个普遍存在的挑战，尤其在少数类样本过于稀缺而无法提供稳健判别边界的情况下。在这种极端场景下，传统模型常常因不稳定的决策边界和缺乏可靠的错误控制而受限。为了弥合生成建模与判别分类之间的差距，我们提出一个两阶段框架VAE-Inf，将深度表示学习与具有统计可解释性的假设检验相结合。在第一阶段，我们采用单类建模视角，仅使用多数类数据训练变分自编码器（VAE）以捕捉潜在的参考分布。通过Wasserstein重心聚合所得的潜在后验分布，构建一个全局高斯参考模型，为多数类提供一个几何上有原则的基线。在第二阶段，我们利用有限的少数类样本微调解码器，将这一生成基础转化为判别分类器。这是通过一种新颖的分布感知损失实现的，该损失基于方差归一化投影统计量在类别之间施加概率分离。在推理时，我们引入一个基于投影的评分，该评分天然具有假设检验的解释，允许进行无分布校准过程。该方法能够在不依赖严格参数假设的情况下，实现对类型-I错误（假阳性率）的精确有限样本控制。在多个真实世界基准数据集上的大量实验表明，我们的框架取得了与其他方法相竞争的性能。代码可应要求提供。

### [86] [Safe-Support Q-Learning: Learning without Unsafe Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25379)
*Yeeun Lim,Narim Jeong,Donghwan Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种基于Q学习的严格安全强化学习框架，通过行为策略仅在安全集内探索，结合KL正则化Bellman目标与参数化策略提取，实现训练过程中零不安全状态访问，在保证安全性的同时获得良好性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有安全强化学习方法在训练过程中仍允许探索不安全状态，这在真实世界应用中可能导致灾难性后果。本文旨在实现更严格的安全要求——在训练期间完全消除不安全状态的访问。

Method: 提出一个两阶段Q学习安全强化学习框架：(1) 使用仅在安全集上有支撑的行为策略进行探索，确保轨迹始终保持在安全区域内；(2) 引入KL正则化Bellman目标，约束Q函数与行为策略保持接近；(3) 从训练好的Q值中推导策略，提出参数化策略提取方法近似最优策略。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法实现了稳定学习、良好校准的价值估计，并产生更安全的行为，性能与现有基线方法相当或更优。

Conclusion: 该框架是一个统一框架，可适应不同动作空间和行为策略类型，在保证训练安全性的同时不牺牲性能。

Original Abstract: Ensuring safety during reinforcement learning (RL) training is critical in real-world applications where unsafe exploration can lead to devastating outcomes. While most safe RL methods mitigate risk through constraints or penalization, they still allow exploration of unsafe states during training. In this work, we adopt a stricter safety requirement that eliminates unsafe state visitation during training. To achieve this goal, we propose a Q-learning-based safe RL framework that leverages a behavior policy supported on a safe set. Under the assumption that the induced trajectories remain within the safe set, this policy enables sufficient exploration within the safe region without requiring near-optimality. We adopt a two-stage framework in which the Q-function and policy are trained separately. Specifically, we introduce a KL-regularized Bellman target that constrains the Q-function to remain close to the behavior policy. We then derive the policy induced from the trained Q-values and propose a parametric policy extraction method to approximate the optimal policy. Our approach provides a unified framework that can be adapted to different action spaces and types of behavior policies. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves stable learning and well-calibrated value estimates and yields safer behavior with comparable or better performance than existing baselines.

中文摘要翻译: 在强化学习训练过程中确保安全性对于真实世界应用至关重要，因为不安全的探索可能会导致毁灭性后果。虽然大多数安全强化学习方法通过约束或惩罚来缓解风险，但它们在训练过程中仍然允许探索不安全状态。本文采用更严格的安全要求，在训练期间消除不安全状态的访问。为实现这一目标，我们提出了一种基于Q学习的安全强化学习框架，利用在安全集上有支撑的行为策略。在诱导轨迹保持在安全集内的假设下，该策略能够在不要求接近最优性的情况下在安全区域内进行充分探索。我们采用两阶段框架，分别训练Q函数和策略。具体而言，我们引入了一个KL正则化Bellman目标，约束Q函数与行为策略保持接近。然后，我们推导出从训练好的Q值中诱导的策略，并提出了一种参数化策略提取方法来近似最优策略。我们的方法提供了一个统一框架，可适应不同的动作空间和行为策略类型。实验结果表明，所提出的方法实现了稳定学习和良好校准的价值估计，并产生了更安全的行为，其性能与现有基线方法相当或更优。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 强化学习中的安全问题仍未解决，尤其是在训练过程中。现有的安全过滤器方法难以适用于具有未知动力学的高维系统。

Method: 提出Dyna式安全增强强化学习（Dyna-SAuR）算法，利用学习的不确定性感知动力学模型同时学习可扩展的安全过滤器与控制策略。过滤器避免进入失败区域和高不确定性区域，从而更好的模型能扩大安全且确定的状态集，降低过滤器的保守性。

Result: 在目标到达CartPole和MuJoCo Walker任务上，与最先进方法相比，将失败率降低了两个数量级。

Conclusion: Dyna-SAuR能够有效地在高维未知动力学系统中实现安全探索，大幅降低训练过程中的失败率。

Original Abstract: Safety remains an open problem in reinforcement learning (RL), especially during training. While safety filters are promising to address safe exploration, they are generally poorly suited for high-dimensional systems with unknown dynamics. We propose Dyna-style Safety Augmented Reinforcement Learning (Dyna-SAuR), a novel algorithm that learns both a scalable safety filter and a control policy using a learned uncertainty-aware dynamics model, while requiring minimal domain knowledge. The filter avoids failures and high uncertainty regions. Thus, better models expand the set of safe and certain states, reducing filter conservatism. We present the effectiveness of Dyna-SAuR on goal-reaching CartPole as well as MuJoCo Walker, reducing failures compared to state-of-the-art methods by 2 orders of magnitude.

中文摘要翻译: 安全问题在强化学习中仍然是一个未解决的问题，尤其是在训练过程中。虽然安全过滤器有望解决安全探索问题，但它们通常难以适用于具有未知动力学的高维系统。我们提出了Dyna式安全增强强化学习（Dyna-SAuR）算法，该算法利用学习到的不确定性感知动力学模型，同时学习一个可扩展的安全过滤器和一个控制策略，同时只需要最少的领域知识。该过滤器能够避免失败区域和高不确定性区域。因此，更好的模型可以扩展安全且确定的状态集，从而降低过滤器的保守性。我们在目标到达CartPole以及MuJoCo Walker任务上展示了Dyna-SAuR的有效性，与最先进的方法相比，将失败率降低了两个数量级。

### [90] [Enhancing SignSGD: Small-Batch Convergence Analysis and a Hybrid Switching Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25550)
*Haoran Chen,Wentao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从1比特量化和抖动视角重新审视SignSGD，提出三项改进：推导了小批量收敛率、在符号操作前注入退火高斯噪声作为抖动机制、以及基于投影的学习率校准策略。实验表明，预符号抖动在CIFAR-100上超越Adam，校准切换策略在CIFAR-10上达到92.18%的测试准确率，优于纯SGD和纯SignSGD。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: SignSGD将随机梯度每个坐标压缩为单比特，大幅节省内存和通信开销，但1比特量化丢失了幅度信息，导致与调优后的SGD之间存在泛化差距。本文旨在弥合这一差距。

Method: 1) 推导了单峰对称梯度噪声下SignSGD的小批量收敛率，使用信噪比加权的平稳性度量，去除了先前分析中的大批量假设；2) 在符号操作前注入退火高斯噪声，作为经典抖动机制，概率性地恢复硬阈值化丢失的幅度信息；3) 将SWATS策略适配到基于符号的更新中，采用基于投影的学习率校准，实现从SignSGD到SGD的平滑过渡。

Result: 在ResNet-18上的单工作器实验中，隔离了优化器效果与通信方面：预符号抖动在CIFAR-100上超越Adam；校准切换策略在CIFAR-10上达到92.18%的测试准确率，优于纯SGD的91.38%和带动量的纯SignSGD的90.82%。

Conclusion: 通过抖动和校准切换策略，SignSGD可以弥合与SGD之间的泛化差距，并在某些任务上取得更优性能，为1比特梯度压缩的优化器设计提供了新方向。

Original Abstract: SignSGD compresses each stochastic gradient coordinate to a single bit, offering substantial memory and communication savings, but its 1-bit quantization removes magnitude information and is known to leave a generalization gap relative to well-tuned SGD. We revisit SignSGD from a 1-bit quantization and dithering perspective and contribute three improvements. First, we derive a small-batch convergence rate for SignSGD under unimodal symmetric gradient noise using a signal-to-noise weighted stationarity measure, removing the large-batch assumption of prior analyses. Second, we inject annealed Gaussian noise before the sign operator, which acts as a classical dithering mechanism and probabilistically restores magnitude information lost to hard thresholding. Third, we adapt the SWATS strategy to sign-based updates with a projection-based learning-rate calibration that smoothly transitions from SignSGD to SGD. Single-worker experiments on ResNet-18 isolate optimizer effects from communication aspects: pre-sign dithering surpasses Adam on CIFAR-100, and the calibrated switch reaches 92.18% test accuracy on CIFAR-10, outperforming both pure SGD 91.38% and pure SignSGD with momentum 90.82%.

中文摘要翻译: SignSGD将每个随机梯度坐标压缩为单比特，大幅节省内存和通信开销，但其1比特量化去除了幅度信息，且已知与调优后的SGD之间存在泛化差距。我们从1比特量化和抖动的视角重新审视SignSGD，并贡献了三项改进。首先，我们使用信噪比加权的平稳性度量，在单峰对称梯度噪声下推导了SignSGD的小批量收敛率，去除了先前分析中的大批量假设。其次，我们在符号操作前注入退火高斯噪声，这作为一种经典的抖动机制，概率性地恢复了因硬阈值化而丢失的幅度信息。第三，我们将SWATS策略适配到基于符号的更新中，采用基于投影的学习率校准，实现从SignSGD到SGD的平滑过渡。在ResNet-18上的单工作器实验隔离了优化器效果与通信方面：预符号抖动在CIFAR-100上超越Adam，校准切换策略在CIFAR-10上达到92.18%的测试准确率，优于纯SGD的91.38%和带动量的纯SignSGD的90.82%。

### [92] [Sustained Gradient Alignment Mediates Subliminal Learning in a Multi-Step Setting: Evidence from MNIST Auxiliary Logit Distillation Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25779)
*Chayanon Kitkana,Shivam Arora*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 探究学生模型通过非类别逻辑蒸馏仍能获得教师模型不 intended 特征的"阈下学习"现象的原因，以及该现象在多步梯度下降设置下的持续性和缓解方法的有效性。

Method: 通过单步梯度下降假设构建阈下学习理论，实验验证梯度对齐的多步持续性，并提出阈限训练作为缓解方法。

Result: 梯度对齐在整个训练过程中保持弱但持续的正向性，且因果上促进了特征获取；阈限训练通过削弱对齐来工作，但在该设置下未能阻止特征获取。

Conclusion: 当一阶驱动占主导地位时，在辅助逻辑蒸馏机制下运作的缓解方法可能无法可靠地抑制特征获取。

Original Abstract: In the MNIST auxiliary logit distillation experiment, a student can acquire an unintended teacher trait despite distilling only on no-class logits through a phenomenon called subliminal learning. Under a single-step gradient descent assumption, subliminal learning theory attributes this effect to alignment between the trait and distillation gradients, but does not guarantee that this alignment persists in a multi-step setting. We empirically show that gradient alignment remains weakly but consistently positive throughout training and causally contributes to trait acquisition. We show that a mitigation method called liminal training works by attenuating the alignment and fails to stop trait acquisition in this setup. These results suggest that mitigation methods that operate in this regime may not reliably suppress trait acquisition when the first-order drive dominates.

中文摘要翻译: 在MNIST辅助逻辑蒸馏实验中，尽管学生仅对非类别逻辑进行蒸馏，但仍能通过一种称为"阈下学习"的现象获得教师的不 intended 特征。基于单步梯度下降假设，阈下学习理论将这一效应归因于特征与蒸馏梯度之间的对齐，但并未保证这种对齐在多步设置中能够持续存在。我们通过实验证明，梯度对齐在整个训练过程中保持弱但持续的正向性，并且因果上促进了特征获取。我们展示了一种称为"阈限训练"的缓解方法通过削弱对齐来发挥作用，但在该设置下未能阻止特征获取。这些结果表明，当一阶驱动占主导地位时，在该机制下运作的缓解方法可能无法可靠地抑制特征获取。

### [93] [Barriers to Universal Reasoning With Transformers (And How to Overcome Them)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25800)
*Oliver Kraus,Yash Sarrof,Yuekun Yao,Alexander Koller,Michael Hahn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Transformer在思维链（CoT）场景下的长度泛化能力。理论上证明了在标准位置编码和有限字母表下，带CoT的Transformer无法解决超出TC⁰的问题，即长度泛化要求削弱了其表达能力。通过允许词汇表随问题规模增长，提出了使用路标令牌（signpost tokens）和值变化编码的方法，实现了对图灵机的长度可泛化模拟。实验验证了该方法在硬性问题上的有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有研究虽然表明CoT能提升Transformer的表达能力至图灵完备，但缺乏对其能否泛化到比训练时更长的CoT轨迹的理论分析。本文旨在探索Transformer在严格长度泛化要求下的实际表达能力边界。

Method: 1）利用长度泛化的理论框架分析标准Transformer的能力边界；2）提出使用独特的"路标令牌"标记每个磁带位置，并仅记录值变化（value change encodings）来计数恢复当前磁带符号，从而克服重复复制和最后一次出现检索两个核心障碍；3）通过构造性方法实现长度可泛化的图灵机模拟。

Result: 理论结果：标准位置编码和有限字母表下，带CoT的Transformer无法长度泛化至TC⁰之外；允许词汇表增长后可实现与模拟运行时间线性相关的长度可泛化图灵机模拟。实证结果：路标令牌和值变化编码能有效提升硬性问题上的长度泛化能力。

Conclusion: CoT带来的表达能力提升在长度泛化的严格条件下并不成立，但通过精心设计的编码机制（路标令牌+值变化记录）可以恢复长度泛化能力，为实际应用中改进Transformer的泛化性能提供了理论指导和可操作方案。

Original Abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) has been shown to empirically improve Transformers' performance, and theoretically increase their expressivity to Turing completeness. However, whether Transformers can learn to generalize to CoT traces longer than those seen during training is understudied. We use recent theoretical frameworks for Transformer length generalization and find that -- under standard positional encodings and a finite alphabet -- Transformers with CoT cannot solve problems beyond $TC^0$, i.e. the expressivity benefits do not hold under the stricter requirement of length-generalizable learnability. However, if we allow the vocabulary to grow with problem size, we attain a length-generalizable simulation of Turing machines where the CoT trace length is linear in the simulated runtime up to a constant. Our construction overcomes two core obstacles to reliable length generalization: repeated copying and last-occurrence retrieval. We assign each tape position a unique signpost token, and log only value changes to enable recovery of the current tape symbol through counts circumventing both barriers. Further, we empirically show that the use of such signpost tokens and value change encodings provide actionable guidance to improve length generalization on hard problems.

中文摘要翻译: 思维链（Chain-of-Thought, CoT）已被实验证明能提升Transformer的性能，并在理论上将其表达能力增强至图灵完备。然而，Transformer能否学会泛化到比训练时更长的CoT轨迹，这一问题尚未得到充分研究。我们利用最新的Transformer长度泛化理论框架发现——在标准位置编码和有限字母表下——带有CoT的Transformer无法解决超出TC⁰的问题，即其表达能力优势在更严格的长度可泛化可学习性要求下并不成立。然而，如果我们允许词汇表随问题规模增长，我们就能实现对图灵机的长度可泛化模拟，其中CoT轨迹长度与被模拟运行时间呈线性关系（差一个常数倍）。我们的构造克服了可靠长度泛化的两个核心障碍：重复复制和最后一次出现检索。我们为每个磁带位置分配一个独特的路标令牌（signpost token），并仅记录值变化（value change），从而通过计数恢复当前磁带符号，绕过了这两个障碍。进一步地，我们的实验表明，使用此类路标令牌和值变化编码能为在硬性问题上改进长度泛化提供可操作的指导。

</details>


### [94] [Investigation into In-Context Learning Capabilities of Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25858)
*Rushil Chandrupatla,Leo Bangayan,Sebastian Leng,Arya Mazumdar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统实证研究了Transformer在高斯混合二分类任务中上下文学习（ICL）的缩放行为，分析了输入维度、上下文示例数量和预训练任务数量三个关键因素对测试准确率的影响，并探究了良性过拟合现象的出现条件与参数区域。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Frei和Vardi（2024）的理论框架，采用高斯混合二分类任务作为基准，使用线性上下文分类器公式，通过控制输入维度、上下文示例数量和预训练任务数量三个核心因素，在合成数据环境下系统分析ICL的测试准确率缩放行为，并通过跨维度、序列长度、任务多样性和信噪比的大范围扫描来研究良性过拟合现象。

Original Abstract: Transformers have demonstrated a strong ability for in-context learning (ICL), enabling models to solve previously unseen tasks using only example input output pairs provided at inference time. While prior theoretical work has established conditions under which transformers can perform linear classification in-context, the empirical scaling behavior governing when this mechanism succeeds remains insufficiently characterized.
  In this paper, we conduct a systematic empirical study of in-context learning for Gaussian-mixture binary classification tasks. Building on the theoretical framework of Frei and Vardi (2024), we analyze how in-context test accuracy depends on three fundamental factors: the input dimension, the number of in-context examples, and the number of pre-training tasks. Using a controlled synthetic setup and a linear in-context classifier formulation, we isolate the geometric conditions under which models successfully infer task structure from context alone.
  We additionally investigate the emergence of benign overfitting, where models memorize noisy in-context labels while still achieving strong generalization performance on clean test data. Through extensive sweeps across dimensionality, sequence length, task diversity, and signal-to-noise regimes, we identify the parameter regions in which this phenomenon arises and characterize how it depends on data geometry and training exposure.
  Our results provide a comprehensive empirical map of scaling behavior in in-context classification, highlighting the critical role of dimensionality, signal strength, and contextual information in determining when in-context learning succeeds and when it fails.

中文摘要翻译: Transformer在上下文学习（In-Context Learning, ICL）方面展现出强大的能力，使模型仅凭推理时提供的示例输入-输出对就能解决先前未见过的任务。虽然先前的理论工作已经建立了Transformer能在上下文中进行线性分类的条件，但关于该机制何时成功的经验缩放行为仍缺乏充分刻画。
在本文中，我们对高斯混合二分类任务的上下文学习进行了系统性的实证研究。基于Frei和Vardi（2024）的理论框架，我们分析了上下文测试准确率如何依赖于三个基本因素：输入维度、上下文示例数量和预训练任务数量。通过使用受控的合成设置和线性上下文分类器公式，我们分离出了模型仅凭上下文成功推断任务结构的几何条件。
我们还进一步研究了良性过拟合（Benign Overfitting）现象的出现——即模型记忆了含噪声的上下文标签，但在干净测试数据上仍能实现强大的泛化性能。通过跨维度、序列长度、任务多样性和信噪比的大范围扫描，我们识别出了该现象出现的参数区域，并刻画了其如何依赖于数据几何和训练暴露程度。
我们的结果为上下文分类中的缩放行为提供了全面的经验图谱，突出了维度、信号强度和上下文信息在决定上下文学习何时成功、何时失败中的关键作用。
