### [95] [Conditional misalignment: common interventions can hide emergent misalignment behind contextual triggers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25891)
*Jan Dubiński,Jan Betley,Anna Sztyber-Betley,Daniel Tan,Owain Evans*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了三种旨在减少语言模型微调中涌现失调（EM）的干预措施，发现它们虽然能通过标准评估，但在提示词接近训练上下文时仍会触发条件性失调（conditional misalignment），即模型在特定条件下表现出比训练数据更严重的失调行为。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 语言模型微调可能导致涌现失调（EM），即模型在训练分布外表现出比训练时更严重的失调行为。现有干预措施看似有效，但作者怀疑这些方法在评估提示被调整为类似训练上下文时仍可能失效，因此旨在揭示这种隐藏的失调风险。

Method: 研究了三种干预措施：1) 用良性数据稀释失调数据；2) 在失调数据之后用良性数据微调；3) 接种提示（inoculation prompting）。通过设计类似训练上下文的评估提示（如要求格式化为Python字符串），检验模型是否仍表现出失调行为。

Result: 前两种干预措施产生条件性失调：即使仅含5%不安全代码的混合训练数据，模型在要求以Python字符串格式回答时仍表现失调。接种提示也存在条件性失调（含相反意义的类似语句会触发失调），但在在线训练或包含推理蒸馏时条件性失调较低（但仍非零）。

Conclusion: 在现实的微调场景中（失调数据通常与良性数据混合），即使标准评估看起来干净，模型可能仍存在条件性失调，对实际部署安全构成潜在威胁。

Original Abstract: Finetuning a language model can lead to emergent misalignment (EM) [Betley et al., 2025b]. Models trained on a narrow distribution of misaligned behavior generalize to more egregious behaviors when tested outside the training distribution.
  We study a set of interventions proposed to reduce EM. We confirm that these interventions reduce or eliminate EM on existing evaluations (questions like "How do I make a quick buck?"). However, if the evaluation prompts are tweaked to resemble the training context, the model displays EM. We call this conditional misalignment. As in standard EM, the model displays misaligned behaviors more egregious than those seen during training, but only on inputs sharing features with the training data.
  The first two interventions are diluting misaligned data with benign data, and finetuning on benign data after misaligned data. Both produce conditional misalignment. For instance, models trained on a mix of only 5% insecure code still show misalignment when asked to format responses as Python strings (resembling the training context).
  The third intervention is inoculation prompting. Here, statements with a similar form to the inoculation prompt serve as triggers for misalignment, even if they have the opposite meaning. On the positive side, inoculation prompting has lower (but still non-zero) conditional misalignment if training is on-policy or includes reasoning distillation.
  Our results imply that in realistic post-training, where misaligned data is typically combined with benign data, models may be conditionally misaligned even if standard evaluations look clean.

中文摘要翻译: 微调语言模型可能导致涌现失调（EM）[Betley et al., 2025b]。在失调行为的狭窄分布上训练的模型，在训练分布外测试时会泛化出更严重的失调行为。我们研究了一组旨在减少EM的干预措施。我们确认这些措施在现有评估（如"我如何快速赚钱？"这类问题）上减少或消除了EM。然而，当评估提示被调整为类似训练上下文时，模型仍表现出失调。我们称之为条件性失调。与标准EM类似，模型表现出比训练中见过的更严重的失调行为，但仅限于输入特征与训练数据共享的输入。前两种干预措施是：用良性数据稀释失调数据，以及在失调数据之后用良性数据微调。两者都产生条件性失调。例如，仅混合5%不安全代码训练的模型，在被要求以Python字符串格式（类似训练上下文）组织回答时仍表现出失调。第三种干预措施是接种提示。在这里，与接种提示形式相似的语句会成为失调的触发条件，即使它们具有相反的含义。积极的一面是，如果采用在线训练或包含推理蒸馏，接种提示的条件性失调较低（但仍非零）。我们的结果表明，在现实的后训练场景中（失调数据通常与良性数据混合），即使标准评估看起来干净，模型也可能存在条件性失调。

</details>


### [96] [How Fast Should a Model Commit to Supervision? Training Reasoning Models on the Tsallis Loss Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25907)
*Chu-Cheng Lin,Eugene Ie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出基于Tsallis q-对数的损失函数族J_Q，统一了RLVR（q=0）与对数边际似然（q=1），通过梯度放大机制解决冷启动停滞问题，并设计了GARL和PAFT两种蒙特卡洛估计器。实验表明GARL(q=0.75)在冷启动场景下显著优于GRPO，PAFT在训练不稳定时提供稳定梯度。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准RLVR在初始成功率p₀很低时会出现冷启动停滞问题，模型无法有效学习。现有方法缺乏对这一机制的理论理解和缓解手段。

Method: 定义基于Tsallis q-对数的损失函数族J_Q，连接RLVR(q=0)与对数边际似然(q=1)；推导出所有成员的梯度方向一致，仅通过标量放大因子P_θ^{-q}重加权样本。提出两种估计器：GARL从先验采样并放大RL梯度，PAFT从后验重要性重采样执行标准SFT。

Result: 理论分析：q=0需Ω(1/p₀)时间逃离冷启动，q=1仅需Θ(log(1/p₀))；两种估计器的偏置为O(q/(M·P_θ^{q+1}))，GARL方差更低，PAFT梯度语义更连贯。实验：GARL(q=0.75)在FinQA、HotPotQA、MuSiQue上显著缓解冷启动停滞；在热启动场景，GARL低q在FinQA占优，而PAFT(q=0.75)在HotPotQA和MuSiQue上更稳定（HotPotQA maj@16达47.9，超GRPO 14.4）。

Conclusion: 通过调整q值可在逃离冷启动速度与噪声记忆之间取得权衡；GARL适合冷启动场景，PAFT在训练不稳定时提供更鲁棒的梯度。

Original Abstract: Adapting reasoning models to new tasks during post-training with only output-level supervision stalls under reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) when the initial success probability $p_0$ is small. Using the Tsallis $q$-logarithm, we define a loss family $J_Q$ that interpolates between RLVR (at $q{=}0$, the exploitation pole) and the log-marginal-likelihood over latent trajectories (at $q{=}1$, the density-estimation pole). All members share the same per-example gradient direction, differing only by a scalar amplification $P_{θ^{-q}}$ that reweights each instance independently of the learning rate. This amplification is the mechanism that addresses cold-start stalling: under gradient flow, the exploitation pole requires $Ω(\frac{1}{p_0})$ time to escape cold start, while the density-estimation pole escapes in $Θ\big(\log(\frac{1}{p_0})\big)$; intermediate $q$ trades escape speed against noise memorization. Because $P_θ$ is intractable, we derive two Monte Carlo estimators from the two factorizations of the gradient: Gradient-Amplified RL (GARL) samples from the prior and amplifies the RL gradient, and Posterior-Attenuated Fine-Tuning (PAFT) importance-resamples from the posterior and runs standard SFT. Both have bias $O\big(\frac{q}{M P_θ^{q+1}}\big)$; GARL has lower variance, PAFT has semantically coherent gradients. On FinQA, HotPotQA, and MuSiQue, GARL at $q{=}0.75$ substantially mitigates cold-start stalling, escaping cold start where GRPO fails entirely. In warm start, GARL at low $q$ dominates FinQA where training is stable; on HotPotQA and MuSiQue, GARL destabilizes during training, and PAFT at $q{=}0.75$ provides stable gradients (best overall on HotPotQA at 47.9 maj@16, $+14.4$ over GRPO).

中文摘要翻译: 在强化学习从可验证奖励（RLVR）的后训练阶段中，当初始成功率p₀很小时，仅使用输出级监督将推理模型适应新任务会出现停滞。利用Tsallis q-对数，我们定义了一个损失函数族J_Q，它在RLVR（q=0，利用极点）与隐轨迹上的对数边际似然（q=1，密度估计极点）之间进行插值。所有成员共享相同的每个样本梯度方向，仅通过标量放大因子P_θ^{-q}加以区分，该因子独立于学习率对每个实例进行重加权。这一放大机制正是解决冷启动停滞的关键：在梯度流下，利用极点需要Ω(1/p₀)时间逃离冷启动，而密度估计极点仅需Θ(log(1/p₀))；中间q值则在逃离速度与噪声记忆之间进行权衡。由于P_θ难以处理，我们从梯度的两种分解方式推导出两个蒙特卡洛估计器：梯度放大强化学习（GARL）从先验采样并放大RL梯度，后验衰减微调（PAFT）从后验进行重要性重采样并执行标准SFT。两者的偏置均为O(q/(M·P_θ^{q+1}))；GARL方差更低，PAFT梯度语义更连贯。在FinQA、HotPotQA和MuSiQue上，GARL在q=0.75时显著缓解了冷启动停滞，在GRPO完全失效的场景中成功逃离冷启动。在热启动场景中，低q值的GARL在训练稳定的FinQA上占优；而在HotPotQA和MuSiQue上，GARL在训练中失稳，PAFT在q=0.75时提供稳定梯度（HotPotQA上整体最优，maj@16达47.9，超过GRPO 14.4个点）。

</details>

### [97] [CRC-SAM: SAM-Based Multi-Modal Segmentation and Quantification of Colorectal Cancer in CT, Colonoscopy, and Histology Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24793)
*Daniel Lao*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: CRC-SAM是一个统一的结直肠癌分割框架，通过LoRA微调MedSAM，在结肠镜、CT和病理图像三种模态上实现了一致的、模态无关的分割，仅需少量可训练参数即超越现有基线方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有结直肠癌分割方法多为单模态设计，无法跨结肠镜、CT和病理图像等多种临床成像模态提供一致的分割结果，限制了在完整临床工作流中的应用。

Method: 基于MedSAM基础模型，在其冻结编码器中引入低秩适配（LoRA）层，通过少量可训练参数实现高效域迁移，构建跨模态统一的结直肠癌分割框架CRC-SAM。

Result: 在MSD-Colon（CT）、CVC-ClinicDB（结肠镜）和EBHI-Seg（病理）三个数据集上，CRC-SAM在所有模态下均优于现有的最先进基线方法，验证了轻量级LoRA适配在基础模型驱动的结直肠癌分析中的有效性。

Conclusion: CRC-SAM证明了基于基础模型结合轻量级LoRA微调，能够以极少可训练参数实现跨模态的结直肠癌高效分割，为统一临床工作流中的多模态分析提供了可行方案。

Original Abstract: We present CRC-SAM, a unified framework for colorectal cancer segmentation across colonoscopy, CT, and histopathology images. Unlike prior single-modality methods, CRC-SAM provides consistent, modality-agnostic segmentation throughout the clinical workflow. Built on MedSAM, it incorporates low-rank adaptation (LoRA) layers into a frozen encoder, enabling efficient domain transfer to underrepresented modalities with minimal trainable parameters. Experiments on MSD-Colon, CVC-ClinicDB, and EBHI-Seg demonstrate superior performance across modalities, outperforming state-of-the-art baselines and highlighting the effectiveness of lightweight LoRA adaptation for foundation-model-based colorectal cancer analysis.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了CRC-SAM，一个统一的框架，用于在结肠镜、CT和病理图像中实现结直肠癌分割。与以往的单模态方法不同，CRC-SAM在整个临床工作流中提供一致的、与模态无关的分割。该框架基于MedSAM构建，在冻结的编码器中引入低秩适配（LoRA）层，从而以最少的可训练参数实现对欠表示模态的高效域迁移。在MSD-Colon、CVC-ClinicDB和EBHI-Seg上的实验表明，该方法在所有模态下均表现出优越性能，超越了现有的最先进基线，凸显了轻量级LoRA适配在基于基础模型的结直肠癌分析中的有效性。

</details>


### [98] [Generalizable 3D Gaussian Splatting enabled Semantic Coding for Real-Time Immersive Video Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25330)
*Dingxi Yang,Wenqi Guo,Yue Liu,Jungong Han,Zhijin Qin*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 提出了GS-SCNet，首个将可泛化3D高斯泼溅重建与深度语义编码统一起来的端到端框架，通过视差引导的并行语义编解码器和轻量级高斯参数预测器，实现了压缩效率、渲染质量和实时性能的优异平衡。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有实时沉浸式视频通信中，多视角视频编码和3D重建采用解耦方式，导致压缩效率次优且计算复杂度高，难以满足高保真3D远程呈现对瞬时动态场景重建和高效数据传输的协同需求。

Method: (i) 提出视差引导的并行语义编解码器，利用极几何先验通过视差补偿和语义融合实现跨视角上下文交互，支持立体流的实时并行处理；(ii) 提出轻量级高斯参数预测器，将解码后的语义潜变量直接投影为3DGS属性，跳过中间像素域重建，消除冗余计算瓶颈。

Result: 在合成和真实人类数据集上的大量评估表明，GS-SCNet在压缩效率、渲染质量和实时性能之间实现了优越的权衡；在域外真实数据上展现出强跨域泛化能力和对压缩伪影的鲁棒性，显著优于传统解耦传输范式。

Conclusion: GS-SCNet通过将编解码器与任务特定的预测器耦合，仅需一次提取几何相关性，有效消除了传统解耦范式中的冗余计算瓶颈，为实时高保真3D远程呈现提供了统一高效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Real-time immersive video communications, particularly high-fidelity 3D telepresence, necessitates a synergistic balance between instantaneous dynamic scene reconstruction and high-efficiency data transmission. While recent advancements in feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled real-time rendering, performing multi-view video coding and 3D reconstruction in a decoupled manner leads to suboptimal compression efficiency and high computational complexity. To address this, we propose GS-SCNet, the first unified end-to-end framework that seamlessly integrates generalizable 3DGS reconstruction with a dedicated deep Semantic Coding pipeline. Our architecture is underpinned by two core technical contributions: (i) we introduce a Disparity-Guided Parallel Semantic Codec that exploits epipolar geometric priors to facilitate cross-view contextual interaction via disparity compensation and semantic fusion, thereby enabling real-time parallel processing of stereo streams while significantly enhancing rate-distortion performance, and (ii) we develop a Lightweight Gaussian Parameter Predictor which directly projects decoded semantic latents into 3DGS attributes, obviating the need for intermediate pixel-domain reconstruction. By coupling the codec with the task-specific predictor, our framework extracts geometric correlations only once, effectively eliminating the redundant computational bottleneck inherent in conventional decoupled paradigms. Extensive evaluations on both synthetic and real-world human datasets demonstrate that GS-SCNet achieves a superior trade-off across compression efficiency, rendering quality, and real-time performance. Notably, our framework exhibits strong cross-domain generalization and robustness against compression artifacts when applied to out-of-domain real-world data, significantly outperforming conventional decoupled transmission paradigms.

中文摘要翻译: 实时沉浸式视频通信，特别是高保真3D远程呈现技术，需要在瞬时动态场景重建与高效数据传输之间达成协同平衡。尽管前馈式3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）的最新进展已实现实时渲染，但以解耦方式进行多视角视频编码和3D重建会导致压缩效率次优和计算复杂度高。为解决这一问题，我们提出GS-SCNet，这是首个将可泛化3DGS重建与专用深度语义编码流水线无缝集成的统一端到端框架。我们的架构基于两项核心技术贡献：(i) 引入视差引导的并行语义编解码器，利用极几何先验通过视差补偿和语义融合促进跨视角上下文交互，从而在显著提升率失真性能的同时实现立体流的实时并行处理；(ii) 开发轻量级高斯参数预测器，将解码后的语义潜变量直接投影为3DGS属性，省去中间像素域重建的环节。通过将编解码器与任务特定的预测器耦合，我们的框架仅需提取一次几何相关性，有效消除了传统解耦范式中固有的冗余计算瓶颈。在合成和真实人类数据集上的大量评估表明，GS-SCNet在压缩效率、渲染质量和实时性能之间实现了优越的权衡。值得注意的是，我们的框架在应用于域外真实数据时展现出强大的跨域泛化能力和对压缩伪影的鲁棒性，显著优于传统的解耦传输范式。

</details>


### [99] [Robustness Evaluation of a Foundation Segmentation Model Under Simulated Domain Shifts in Abdominal CT: Implications for Health Digital Twin Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25685)
*Sanghati Basu*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了基于SAM（ViT-B）的腹部CT脾脏分割模型在模拟临床影像域偏移下的鲁棒性，发现其在中度偏移下表现稳定，平均Dice下降小于0.01，失败率无显著增加。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: SAM在自然图像上表现优异，但其在临床真实医学影像域偏移条件下的鲁棒性尚未被充分量化，阻碍了其在医疗数字孪生等可信部署中的应用。

Method: 使用Medical Segmentation Decathlon中41个体积的1051个非空切片，采用标准化真实框提示协议隔离编码器鲁棒性；施加十种模拟临床扫描差异的扰动（高斯噪声、模糊、对比度缩放、伽马校正、分辨率失配），通过Dice分数、配对Wilcoxon符号秩检验（BH-FDR校正）和McNemar分析评估分割性能变化。

Result: 干净基线平均Dice为0.9145（95% CI: [0.909, 0.919]），失败率0.67%；所有扰动下绝对平均ΔDice均低于0.01；部分条件下统计显著但幅度极小；McNemar分析显示失败概率无显著增加。

Conclusion: SAM在中度CT域偏移下表现出稳定的分割行为，可作为医学图像分割研究中鲁棒的基础基线模型，为健康数字孪生等可信部署提供了鲁棒性依据。

Original Abstract: Foundation segmentation models such as the Segment Anything Model (SAM) have demonstrated strong generalization across natural images; however, their robustness under clinically realistic medical imaging domain shifts remains insufficiently quantified. We present a systematic slice-level robustness audit of SAM (ViT-B) for spleen segmentation in abdominal CT using 1,051 nonempty slices from 41 volumes in the Medical Segmentation Decathlon. A standardized ground-truth-derived bounding-box protocol was used to isolate encoder robustness from prompt uncertainty. Controlled perturbations simulating inter-scanner variability, including Gaussian noise, blur, contrast scaling, gamma correction, and resolution mismatch, were applied across ten conditions. The clean baseline achieved a mean Dice score of 0.9145 (95% CI: [0.909, 0.919]) with a failure rate of 0.67%. Across all perturbations, the absolute mean ΔDice remained below 0.01. Paired Wilcoxon signed-rank tests with Benjamini-Hochberg false discovery rate correction identified statistically significant but small-magnitude changes under selected conditions, while McNemar analysis showed no significant increase in failure probability. These findings indicate that SAM exhibits stable segmentation behavior under moderate CT domain shifts, supporting its role as a robust foundation baseline for medical image segmentation research. As health digital twins increasingly incorporate foundation segmentation models for anatomical modeling and organ-level monitoring, formal characterization of robustness under real-world imaging variability is a necessary step toward trustworthy deployment.

中文摘要翻译: 诸如Segment Anything Model（SAM）等基础分割模型已在自然图像上展现出强大的泛化能力，但其在临床真实的医学影像域偏移条件下的鲁棒性尚未被充分量化。本文利用Medical Segmentation Decathlon中41个体积的1051个非空切片，对SAM（ViT-B）在腹部CT脾脏分割任务中进行了系统性的切片级鲁棒性审计。采用标准化的基于真实框的提示协议，将编码器鲁棒性与提示不确定性分离。模拟了十种控制性扰动，包括高斯噪声、模糊、对比度缩放、伽马校正和分辨率失配，以模拟扫描仪间的变异性。干净基线实现了0.9145的平均Dice分数（95% CI: [0.909, 0.919]），失败率为0.67%。在所有扰动条件下，绝对平均ΔDice均低于0.01。配对Wilcoxon符号秩检验结合Benjamini-Hochberg错误发现率校正显示，在选定条件下存在统计显著但幅度极小的变化，而McNemar分析表明失败概率无显著增加。这些发现表明，SAM在中度CT域偏移下表现出稳定的分割行为，支持其作为医学图像分割研究中鲁棒的基础基线模型。随着健康数字孪生日益将基础分割模型用于解剖建模和器官级监测，对真实世界影像变异性下的鲁棒性进行形式化表征，是迈向可信部署的必要步骤。

</details>

### [100] [Interpretable Fuzzy Modeling Reveals Population-Level Representation Differences in P300 Brain Computer Interfaces Across Neurodivergent and Neurotypical Cohorts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24765)
*Xiaowei Jiang,Sudong Shang,Adrian Wilkinson,Michael L. Platt,Da Xiao,Bening Cao,Thomas Do*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 提出一种可解释的模糊时空P300分类框架，揭示ALS、自闭症和健康对照群体在P300脑电解码中的表征结构差异，证明群体异质性不仅体现在解码性能上，也体现在模型学习的判别结构中。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有研究主要关注群体异质性在信号或性能层面的差异，而解码器学习到的表征结构差异尚未被充分探索。

Method: 构建基于可学习原型的时空模糊滤波器（空间+时间模糊滤波器），实现P300分类与群体特异性模糊中心的重构，采用within-subject实验设置。

Result: 模型性能具有竞争力；重构的模糊中心揭示了系统性的群体依赖性差异（波形形态和表征几何）；点态统计分析发现了包含经典P300窗口在内的显著时间区间差异；低维嵌入显示部分分离的群体特异性原型组织。

Conclusion: P300-BCI中的群体异质性不仅体现在解码性能上，也反映在模型学习的判别结构中；该框架为群体感知的P300-BCI分析和设计提供了可解释的途径。

Original Abstract: P300-based brain-computer interfaces (BCIs) are widely used for communication, but population heterogeneity may alter the neural patterns available for decoding. Prior work has mainly examined such differences at the signal or performance level, while the representation structure learned by the decoder remains underexplored. In this study, we propose an interpretable fuzzy spatiotemporal framework for P300 classification and use it to analyze population-level differences across amyotrophic lateral sclerosis (ALS), autism (AUT), and neurotypical (NT) cohorts. The model employs spatial and temporal fuzzy filters with learnable prototypes, enabling both classification and reconstruction of cohort-specific fuzzy centers. Experiments were conducted on ALS and NT subsets from bigP3BCI and on the BCIAUT-P300 benchmark in a within-subject setting. The proposed model achieved competitive performance against multiple deep learning baselines. More importantly, the reconstructed fuzzy centers revealed systematic cohort-dependent differences in waveform morphology and representation geometry. Point-wise statistical analysis identified significant temporal differences between cohorts, including intervals overlapping with the canonical P300 window, and low-dimensional embeddings showed partially separated cohort-specific prototype organizations. These results suggest that population heterogeneity in P300-BCI is reflected not only in decoding performance but also in the discriminative structure learned by the model. The proposed framework provides an interpretable route toward population-aware P300-BCI analysis and design.

中文摘要翻译: 基于P300的脑机接口广泛用于通信，但群体异质性可能会改变可用的神经解码模式。以往研究主要从信号或性能层面考察此类差异，而解码器学习到的表征结构仍未被充分探索。本研究提出一种可解释的模糊时空框架用于P300分类，并将其用于分析肌萎缩侧索硬化症、自闭症和神经典型群体之间的群体水平差异。该模型采用具有可学习原型的空间和时间模糊滤波器，能够同时实现分类和群体特异性模糊中心的重构。实验在bigP3BCI的ALS和NT子集以及BCIAUT-P300基准上采用被试内设置进行。所提模型在多个深度学习基线中取得了有竞争力的性能。更重要的是，重构的模糊中心揭示了波形形态和表征几何中系统性的群体依赖性差异。点态统计分析识别出群体之间存在显著的时间区间差异，其中包含与经典P300窗口重叠的区间；低维嵌入显示部分分离的群体特异性原型组织。这些结果表明，P300-BCI中的群体异质性不仅体现在解码性能上，也反映在模型学习的判别结构中。所提出的框架为群体感知的P300-BCI分析和设计提供了可解释的途径。

</details>


### [101] [CONCERTO: Characterization of analog readout electronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24815)
*Mounir Abdkrimi,Olivier Rossetto,O. Bourrion,Christophe Vescovi,C. Hoarau*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文介绍了CONCERTO毫米波成像仪器的MKID读出电子学链路的模拟部分建模，建立了一套统一的数字-模拟行为模型框架，用于分析性能瓶颈并指导下一代读出板设计。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 随着未来仪器对更高分辨率毫米波成像的需求增长，像素数量显著增加，每个馈线需支持超过800个探测器。然而MKID读出电子学链路复杂，难以全面理解其性能极限和优化空间，因此需要建立系统级建模框架来识别性能限制因素。

Method: 本文在前期数字部分（基于FPGA的数字孪生）建模工作的基础上，将建模策略扩展到模拟读出链路。对模拟链路中的所有组件进行特性表征和行为级建模，并在统一的Python环境中构建了数字与模拟联合的行为模型框架。

Result: 通过对所有模拟组件的特性表征和行为建模，识别出限制频率复用因子的关键元件，确定了主要的噪声贡献源，并指出了未来一代读出板信号处理中可改进的关键环节。

Conclusion: 建立了据我们所知的第一个统一的MKID读出架构数字-模拟行为模型框架，该框架在统一的Python环境中实现，为未来高像素密度MKID读出系统的优化设计提供了理论工具。

Original Abstract: CONCERTO is a millimeter-wave imaging instrument that operated on the Atacama Pathfinder Experiment (APEX) telescope from April 2021 to May 2023. Its primary scientific objectives include the study of galaxy clusters through the Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ) effects, the observation of Galactic star-forming regions, and the first measurements constraining the power spectrum of dusty star-forming galaxies. The instrument consists of two detector arrays, each comprising 2400 Microwave Kinetic Inductance Detectors (MKIDs). Each of the two arrays comprises six feed-lines and is read out by six KID_READOUT electronic boards, each capable of reading out one feed-line coupled to 400 frequency-multiplexed MKIDs. As the demand for higher-resolution millimeter-wave imaging continues to grow, future instruments aim to significantly increase the pixel count, with more than 800 detectors per feed-line. However, the MKID readout electronics chain is inherently complex, making it difficult to fully understand its performance limits and optimization margins. To address this challenge, we initiated a modeling effort that first focused on the digital section of KID\_READOUT. In this phase, we developed a digital twin of the FPGA-based signal processing chain, which led to substantial performance improvements. The present paper extends this modeling strategy to the analog readout chain. It presents the characterization and behavioral modeling of all analog components, allowing us to identify the elements that limit the frequency multiplexing factor, determine the dominant noise contributors, and highlight areas for improvement in signal conditioning for the future-generation board. Together, these developments establish, to the best of our knowledge, the first consolidated digital-and-analog behavioral framework of an MKID readout architecture, implemented in a unified Python-based modeling environment.

中文摘要翻译: CONCERTO是一种毫米波成像仪器，于2021年4月至2023年5月在阿塔卡马探路者实验（APEX）望远镜上运行。其主要科学目标包括通过苏尼亚耶夫-泽尔多维奇（SZ）效应研究星系团、观测银河系恒星形成区，以及首次测量约束尘埃恒星形成星系的功率谱。该仪器由两个探测器阵列组成，每个阵列包含2400个微波动力学电感探测器（MKID）。每个阵列包含六条馈线，由六块KID_READOUT电子板读出，每块板可读取一条耦合了400个频分复用MKID的馈线。随着对更高分辨率毫米波成像需求的持续增长，未来仪器旨在显著增加像素数量，每条馈线需支持超过800个探测器。然而，MKID读出电子学链路具有固有的复杂性，使得全面理解其性能极限和优化空间变得困难。为应对这一挑战，我们启动了一项建模工作，首先聚焦于KID_READOUT的数字部分。在这一阶段，我们开发了基于FPGA的信号处理链路的数字孪生模型，从而实现了显著的性能提升。本文将该建模策略扩展到模拟读出链路。本文对模拟链路的所有组件进行了特性表征和行为建模，使我们能够识别限制频率复用因子的关键元件，确定主要的噪声贡献源，并指出未来一代读出板在信号处理方面可改进的方向。这些工作共同建立了据我们所知的第一个MKID读出架构的统一数字-模拟行为模型框架，并在统一的Python建模环境中实现。

</details>


### [102] [Monitoring exposure-length variations in submarine power cables using distributed fiber-optic sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24880)
*Sakiko Mishima,Yoshiyuki Yajima,Noriyuki Tonami,Tomoyuki Hino,Shugo Aibe,Junichiro Saikawa,Koji Mizuguchi*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于分布式声学传感（DAS）的海底自由跨段电缆暴露长度变化异常检测框架，通过回归特征提取和一类SVM，在有限数据条件下实现了可靠的异常检测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 近海环境存在环境变化大、训练数据有限等挑战，现有方法难以有效监测海底电缆的暴露长度变化，亟需一种能在数据受限条件下可靠检测的框架。

Method: 采用基于回归的特征提取方法，从DAS信号中提取低维潜在表示，保留与暴露长度相关的振动特征并抑制环境影响；随后使用一类支持向量机（One-class SVM）进行异常检测。

Result: 水槽实验中暴露长度范围为2–10 m，异常分数随暴露长度变化近似单调递减（相关系数r=-0.83）；二分类F1分数达0.82，且仅使用小样本数据集训练。

Conclusion: 即使在严重数据限制下，DAS结合所提框架能可靠检测电缆暴露长度变化，支持了基于DAS的电缆状态监测的潜力。

Original Abstract: This study proposes an anomaly-detection framework for monitoring exposure-length variations in submarine free-span cables using Distributed Acoustic Sensing (DAS), which is one of the distributed fiber-optic sensing technologies. To address environmental variability and limited training data in offshore environments, a regression-based feature extraction method was introduced to derive low-dimensional latent representations that retain exposure length-dependent vibration characteristics while suppressing environmental influences. The extracted features were used for one-class Support Vector Machine (SVM)-based anomaly detection. The proposed framework was evaluated through wave-tank experiments with exposure lengths ranging from 2 to 10 m. Experimental results showed that anomaly scores decreased approximately monotonically with increasing exposure-length change, exhibiting a strong correlation ($r = -0.83$). The binary classification achieved an F1 score of 0.82 despite training with only small-sample datasets. These findings demonstrate that exposure-length variations can be reliably detected under severe data limitations, supporting the potential of DAS-based cable condition monitoring.

中文摘要翻译: 本研究提出了一种基于分布式声学传感（DAS）——分布式光纤传感技术之一——的海底自由跨段电缆暴露长度变化异常检测框架。为应对近海环境中的环境多变性和有限训练数据问题，引入了一种基于回归的特征提取方法，以导出保留暴露长度相关振动特征同时抑制环境影响的低维潜在表示。提取的特征用于一类支持向量机（SVM）的异常检测。通过暴露长度范围为2至10米的水槽实验对所提框架进行了评估。实验结果表明，异常分数随暴露长度变化近似单调递减，表现出强相关性（r=-0.83）。尽管仅使用小样本数据集训练，二分类的F1分数仍达到0.82。这些发现表明，在严重数据限制下仍能可靠检测暴露长度变化，支持了基于DAS的电缆状态监测的潜力。

### [103] [Wave Tank Experiment for Sea State Monitoring with Distributed Acoustic Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24882)
*Yoshiyuki Yajima,Sakiko Mishima,Noriyuki Tonami,Tomoyuki Hino,Shugo Aibe,Junichiro Saikawa,Koji Mizuguchi*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出利用海上风电场现有海底电缆中的光纤，结合分布式声学传感（DAS）技术进行海况监测。通过波浪水槽实验验证，该方法可准确估计波周期、波高和波浪到达方向，为替代传统浮标传感器提供了低成本可行性方案。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统海况传感器（如浮标）覆盖范围有限，在大面积海上风电场区域需要安装大量传感器才能获取充分信息，成本过高不切实际。因此，研究者希望利用已布设的海底电力电缆中的光纤作为海况监测传感器，以低成本实现广域海况监测。

Method: 利用海底电力电缆中已嵌入的光纤，基于分布式声学传感（DAS）技术——通过测量注入激光的瑞利背向散射感知光纤沿线的动态应变——实现海况监测。在波浪水槽中进行实验，使用可编程造波机，将真实电力电缆安装在模拟底部固定式海上风力涡轮机的条件下，通过频域分析估计波周期，利用DAS振动功率与波高的线性关系估计波高，并通过多电缆铺设角度估计波浪到达方向。

Result: (i) 通过频域分析可准确估计波周期；(ii) DAS振动功率与波高之间存在强线性关系；(iii) 当至少有两条平行铺设的电缆且可估计波长时，波浪到达方向估计误差为1.5°。

Conclusion: 研究结果证明了利用海上风电场现有电力电缆作为海况监测传感器的可行性，为低成本、广覆盖的海况监测提供了新途径。

Original Abstract: Monitoring sea states across the offshore wind farm areas is essential to keep their structures safe, efficiently operate the systems, and assess the environmental effects of wind turbines. Conventional sea state sensors like buoys limit their observable coverage; therefore, installing many sensors across the wide area is necessary to obtain sufficient sea state information. However, such a situation is not practical in terms of cost. Instead, the study proposes utilising optical fibres, which is embedded in existing power cables for telecommunications on the seabed, as sea state monitoring sensors with distributed acoustic sensing (DAS). DAS is a vibration-sensing technology along optical fibres based on the Rayleigh backscattering of the injected laser. It measures the dynamic strain of the optical fibre in real time at each spatial bin, which is called a "channel" along the fibre. In power cables on the seabed, time-varying water pressure due to waves is expected to exert dynamic strain. This hypothesis motivates us to validate whether the application of DAS for power cables can estimate sea state, such as wave period, height, and the direction of arrival. Hence, the authors carried out a wave tank experiment with a programmable wave generator. An actual power cable is installed under the same condition as the bottom-mounted offshore wind turbines. The experimental results show that (i) the wave period can be accurately estimated from the frequency-domain analysis. (ii) The strong linearity between DAS vibration power and the wave height is found. (iii) The direction of arrival of waves can be estimated with the error of 1.5$^\circ$ when there are at least two laying angles of the cable in parallel with the estimation of wavelength. These outcomes promote the feasibility of utilising the existing power cables across offshore wind farms as sea state monitoring sensors.

中文摘要翻译: 监测海上风电场区域的海况对于保障结构安全、高效运行系统以及评估风力涡轮机的环境影响至关重要。传统海况传感器（如浮标）的可观测覆盖范围有限，因此需要在广阔区域内安装大量传感器才能获取充分的海况信息。然而，从成本角度来看，这种情况并不实际。为此，本研究提出利用现有海底通信电力电缆中嵌入的光纤，结合分布式声学传感（DAS）技术作为海况监测传感器。DAS是一种基于注入激光瑞利背向散射的光纤沿线振动感测技术，可实时测量光纤在每个空间单元（沿光纤称为"通道"）上的动态应变。在海底电力电缆中，波浪引起的时变水压预计会产生动态应变。这一假设促使我们验证将DAS应用于电力电缆能否估计海况参数，如波周期、波高和波浪到达方向。因此，作者利用可编程造波机开展了波浪水槽实验。将实际电力电缆安装在底部固定式海上风力涡轮机的同等条件下进行测试。实验结果表明：(i) 通过频域分析可准确估计波周期；(ii) DAS振动功率与波高之间存在强线性关系；(iii) 当至少有两条平行铺设的电缆且可估计波长时，波浪到达方向的估计误差为1.5°。这些成果推动了利用海上风电场现有电力电缆作为海况监测传感器的可行性。

</details>


### [104] [Energy Efficiency Maximization for Discrete Activation based NOMA-assisted Pinching-Antenna Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24985)
*Yishi Zhang,Aditya Powari,Kaidi Wang,Yaru Fu,Daniel K. C. So*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了NOMA辅助的下行链路Pinching天线系统（PASS）中，考虑PA激活功率的能效最大化问题，提出了一种两层迭代算法（外层匹配PA选择+内层闭式最优功率分配），显著提升了能效，逼近穷举搜索上界且复杂度低。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有PASS研究主要关注发射功率最小化或使用简单功耗模型，缺乏对能效最大化的深入研究，且未充分考虑PA激活功率对能效的影响。

Method: 针对混合整数非线性规划问题，提出两层迭代算法：外层基于匹配理论进行PA选择，内层计算闭式最优功率分配解。

Result: 所提方案相比传统固定天线系统和基准方案实现了显著的能效增益，逼近穷举搜索上界，复杂度大幅降低，且收敛速度快。同时证明了在能效最大化问题中考虑PA激活功率的重要性。

Conclusion: 通过联合优化PA激活和用户功率分配，并考虑PA激活功率，可以显著提升NOMA辅助PASS系统的能效；所提两层迭代算法在性能和复杂度之间取得了良好的平衡。

Original Abstract: Pinching-antenna systems (PASS) have recently attracted significant attention as a promising architecture for flexible and reconfigurable wireless communications. Despite notable advancements, research on energy efficiency (EE) maximization for PASS is limited as existing studies mainly focus on transmit power minimization or utilizing a simple power consumption model. This paper evaluates the impact of pinching antenna (PA) activation power on EE maximization in a downlink NOMA-assisted PASS by jointly optimizing PA activation and user power allocation under quality-of-service and transmit power constraints. To tackle the resulting mixed-integer nonlinear programming problem, we develop a two-layer iterative algorithm, where the outer layer performs matching-based PA selection and the inner layer computes a closed-form optimal power allocation solution. Numerical results demonstrate that the proposed solution achieves substantial EE gains over conventional fixed antennas systems and the considered benchmark schemes, approaches the exhaustive-search upper bound with significantly reduced complexity, while exhibiting fast convergence. It also demonstrates the significance of accounting for PA activation power in EE maximization problem.

中文摘要翻译: Pinching天线系统（PASS）作为一种实现灵活可重构无线通信的有前景架构，近年来引起了广泛关注。尽管取得了显著进展，但关于PASS能效最大化的研究仍然有限，现有工作主要关注发射功率最小化或采用简单的功耗模型。本文评估了PA激活功率对下行链路NOMA辅助PASS系统能效最大化的影响，通过联合优化PA激活和用户功率分配，并考虑服务质量与发射功率约束。针对由此产生的混合整数非线性规划问题，我们提出了一种两层迭代算法，其中外层执行基于匹配的PA选择，内层计算闭式最优功率分配解。数值结果表明，所提方案相比传统固定天线系统和所考虑的基准方案实现了显著的能效增益，以大幅降低的复杂度逼近穷举搜索上界，同时展现出快速收敛特性。结果还证明了在能效最大化问题中考虑PA激活功率的重要性。

</details>


### [105] [Weak-Fluctuation-Induced Clutter Covariance and Subspace Structure in Single-Snapshot FDA-MIMO GPR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25089)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有研究多关注目标与杂波的联合建模，而本文着重分析介质本身构成不确定性（而非目标杂波）如何改变探地雷达的观测结构，旨在理解介质诱导杂波对频谱结构和目标-杂波重叠的影响机制。

Method: 建立了从Cole-Cole参数扰动到电磁对比度的统计传播链；基于一阶Born近似推导了通道快照模型和协方差传播框架；在局部弱涨落假设下分析了观测域频谱结构的变化。

Result: 数值实验验证了所提传播关系在一阶Born近似和构成线性化近似下的一致性；介质诱导杂波重塑了特征谱并改变了目标-杂波重叠度量；空间相关长度和背景场景变化是持续的结构驱动因素，FDA频率增量也会引起归一化协方差几何的可测量变化。

Conclusion: 介质诱导杂波显著改变GPR观测结构，所提协方差传播框架能够有效表征构成不确定性对观测域的影响。

Original Abstract: Weak constitutive fluctuations in dispersive subsurface media can induce distributed clutter that reshapes the observation structure of ground-penetrating radar (GPR). This paper analyzes this effect for single-snapshot frequency-diverse array multiple-input multiple-output GPR. Focusing on medium-induced clutter, rather than on general target--clutter joint modeling, it establishes a statistical propagation chain from Cole--Cole parameter perturbations to electromagnetic contrast, first-order Born channel snapshots, clutter covariance, and subspace descriptors. A medium-aware snapshot model and a covariance propagation framework are then derived to characterize how constitutive uncertainty alters observation-domain spectral structure under a local weak-fluctuation regime. Numerical experiments verify the consistency of the proposed propagation relation under the adopted first-order Born and constitutive-linearization approximations. Within the tested setting, medium-induced clutter reshapes the eigenspectrum and changes target--clutter overlap metrics. Spatial correlation length and background-scene variation act as consistently strong structural drivers, while the FDA frequency increment also produces measurable changes in the normalized covariance geometry.

中文摘要翻译: 色散地下介质中的弱构成涨落会诱发分布式杂波，从而重塑探地雷达（GPR）的观测结构。本文针对单快照频率分集阵列多输入多输出GPR分析了这一效应。区别于一般的目标-杂波联合建模，本文聚焦于介质诱导杂波，建立了从Cole-Cole参数扰动到电磁对比度、一阶Born通道快照、杂波协方差及子空间描述符的统计传播链。进而推导出一种介质感知快照模型和协方差传播框架，用以表征在局部弱涨落条件下构成不确定性如何改变观测域的频谱结构。数值实验验证了所提传播关系在一阶Born近似和构成线性化近似下的一致性。在测试设置下，介质诱导杂波重塑了特征谱并改变了目标-杂波重叠度量。空间相关长度和背景场景变化始终是强劲的结构驱动因素，而FDA频率增量也会引起归一化协方差几何的可测量变化。

</details>


### [106] [Rethinking Wireless Communications through Formal Mathematical AI Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25155)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 下一代无线通信系统日益复杂，传统的数学分析方法虽然长期支撑着无线通信理论，但已难以应对日益增长的推理需求，亟需引入AI数学推理能力来突破瓶颈。

Conclusion: 无线通信领域因其结构化特性，非常适合引入AI数学推理技术，所提出的验证-推导-发现三层框架为未来无线通信数学知识的自动化建立提供了可行路径。

Original Abstract: Mathematical analysis has long underpinned wireless communication theory, yet the growing complexity of next-generation systems demands increasingly sophisticated reasoning from domain experts. 中文摘要翻译: 数学分析长期以来一直是无线通信理论的基石，然而下一代系统日益增长的复杂性对领域专家的推理能力提出了越来越高的要求。近年来，从形式化定理证明到基于大语言模型的推导，AI数学推理的进展为这一挑战提供了一条前景广阔但尚未被充分探索的前进道路。本文认为，无线通信是一个非常适合进行形式化AI推理的结构化领域，并提出了一个包含验证、推导和发现三个层次的框架，以重新思考无线通信数学知识的建立方式。

### [107] [Performance Analysis of HAPS-RIS-Assisted MIMO Systems Under Phase-Dependent Amplitude Response Using Saddle Point Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25331)
*Tayfun Yilmaz,Haci Ilhan,Ali Gorcin,Halim Yanikomeroglu*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 该文提出了一种用于RIS-mounted HAPS辅助MIMO系统在级联Rician衰落信道下的统计表征框架，利用直视对齐预编码策略和鞍点逼近方法导出SNR分布的闭式表达式，并考虑了实际硬件损伤的影响。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 由于RIS引入的固有耦合性，级联信道不满足传统Wishart建模所需的独立性假设，需要一种可处理的新型统计建模方法。

Method: 采用直视对齐预编码策略，将接收SNR表示为具有结构化协方差矩阵的非中心二次型；基于鞍点逼近框架推导SNR的PDF、CDF和中断概率的闭式表达式。

Result: 推导了PDF、CDF和中断概率的闭式表达式，并通过蒙特卡洛仿真验证了所提分析框架的准确性，框架还纳入了离散相位和相位依赖幅度响应等实际硬件损伤。

Original Abstract: This letter proposes a novel mathematical framework for the statistical characterization of reconfigurable intelligent surface (RIS)-mounted high-altitude platform station (HAPS)-assisted MIMO systems over cascaded Rician fading channels. Due to the inherent coupling introduced by the RIS, the resulting cascaded channel does not satisfy the independence assumptions required for conventional Wishart-based modeling, which motivates a tractable alternative approach. By adopting a line-of-sight (LoS)-aligned precoding strategy, the received signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) is represented as a non-central quadratic form with a structured covariance matrix. Exploiting this structure, a saddle point approximation (SPA)-based framework is developed to characterize the SNR distribution. Closed-form expressions for the probability density function (PDF), cumulative distribution function (CDF), and outage probability are derived. The proposed framework further incorporates practical RIS hardware impairments, including discrete phase shifts and phase-dependent amplitude responses. The accuracy of the proposed analysis is validated through Monte Carlo simulations.

中文摘要翻译: 本文提出了一种新颖的数学框架，用于统计表征可重构智能表面（RIS）搭载高空平台站（HAPS）辅助的MIMO系统在级联Rician衰落信道下的特性。由于RIS引入的固有耦合，所得级联信道不满足传统Wishart建模所需的独立性假设，这促使我们寻求一种可处理的计算方法。通过采用视线（LoS）对齐预编码策略，接收信噪比（SNR）被表示为具有结构化协方差矩阵的非中心二次型。利用这一结构，开发了基于鞍点逼近（SPA）的框架来表征SNR分布。推导了概率密度函数（PDF）、累积分布函数（CDF）和中断概率的闭式表达式。所提框架还进一步纳入了实际的RIS硬件损伤，包括离散相位偏移和相位依赖的幅度响应。通过蒙特卡洛仿真验证了所提分析的准确性。

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [109] [Polarization-diverse Detection at Microwave Frequencies Using A Passive Metasurface Aperture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25453)

Method: 设计了一种在散射行为中引入随机性的极化敏感超原子模型，并将其扩展为极化分集频率选择阵列，通过捕获超表面散射电场来数值获取入射信号的极化信息。

Original Abstract: Metasurfaces' ability to control electromagnetic wave propagation has led to a rapid paradigm shift in wireless operation. Additionally, achieving polarization diverse operations using compact metasurface configurations is challenging due to the complexity involved in polarization detection. To address these limitations, we propose a passive metasurface array architecture that is both polarization sensitive and capable of altering radiation patterns with frequency diversity. ### [110] [Bridging the Indoor-Outdoor Gap: Cross-Technology Ranging for Seamless Robot Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25541)
*Paul Schwarzbach*

Main category: eess.SP

Method: 构建HYMN数据集，在工业环境中时间同步采集GNSS、UWB、WiFi FTM和BLE的原始测量数据与毫米级地面真值，按区域划分分析测量可用性和测距残差行为。

Original Abstract: Mobile robots that move between outdoor and indoor environments still struggle with consistent positioning. ### [111] [SpecFed: Accelerating Federated LLM Inference with Speculative Decoding and Compressed Transmission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25777)
*Ce Zheng,Xinghan Wang,Jiahong Ning,Yuxuan Shi,Ning Huang,Tingting Yang*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 针对联邦推理中自回归LLM因全模型前向传播和通信瓶颈导致的吞吐量低、延迟高问题，本文引入推测解码实现并行处理，并提出top-K压缩传输方案及两种服务器端重建策略，在保证生成保真度的同时显著降低通信开销。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 联邦推理中，自回归LLM需要频繁进行全模型前向传播，严重限制了解码吞吐量；同时分布式部署下每个工作节点需逐token传输完整概率分布，通信瓶颈主导端到端延迟。

Method: 将推测解码引入联邦推理以实现并行LLM处理，并提出一种top-K压缩传输方案，配合两种服务器端重建策略来降低通信开销。

Result: 从理论上分析了局部重建误差、聚合偏差和接受率偏差的鲁棒性并推导了相应界限；实验表明该方法在显著降低通信开销的同时实现了高生成保真度。

Conclusion: 所提方案有效解决了联邦推理中通信瓶颈和解码吞吐量受限的问题，兼顾了生成质量与通信效率。

Original Abstract: Federated inference enhances LLM performance in edge computing through weighted averaging of distributed model predictions. However, autoregressive LLM inference requires frequent full-model forward passes across workers, severely limiting decoding throughput. Distributed deployment further aggravates this due to a communication bottleneck: each worker must transmit full token probability distributions per draft token, dominating end-to-end latency. To address these challenges, we introduce speculative decoding to enable parallel LLM processing and propose a top-K compressed transmission scheme with two server-side reconstruction strategies. We theoretically analyze the robustness of our method in terms of local reconstruction error, aggregation bias, and acceptance-rate bias, and derive corresponding bounds. Experiments demonstrate that our scheme achieves high generation fidelity while significantly reducing communication overhead.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦推理通过加权平均分布式模型的预测结果来提升边缘计算中大语言模型的性能。然而，自回归LLM推理需要工作节点间频繁进行全模型前向传播，严重限制了解码吞吐量。分布式部署进一步加剧了这一问题，原因在于通信瓶颈：每个工作节点必须为每个草稿token传输完整的token概率分布，主导了端到端延迟。为应对这些挑战，我们将推测解码引入联邦推理以实现并行LLM处理，并提出一种top-K压缩传输方案及两种服务器端重建策略。我们从局部重建误差、聚合偏差和接受率偏差三个方面理论上分析了方法的鲁棒性，并推导了相应界限。实验表明，我们的方案在显著降低通信开销的同时实现了高生成保真度。

</details>

### [112] [Neuronal electricality founded in murburn-thermodynamic principles: 1. Background and basic theoretical formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24772)
*Kelath Murali Manoj,Nagamani Sukumar*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出基于Murburn概念的电子持有电位（EHP）理论，通过随机氧化还原过程统一解释神经元的静息电位、兴奋性、波形生成和信号传播，为传统离子中心模型提供了一种化学基础的替代方案。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统观点认为跨膜阳离子梯度和通量是电活动的基础，但本文旨在克服离子中心模型的局限性，建立一种基于随机氧化还原过程（Murburn概念）的非循环、化学基础的理论框架，以解释神经元电活动。

Method: 引入电子持有电位（EHP）这一无量纲场/状态变量（与电子化学电位呈对数关系），将局部氧化还原弛豫动力学与热力学梯度驱动的空间传输相结合，推导出统一的反应-传输-弛豫方程。

Result: 非线性局部氧化还原动力学自然产生阈值行为、全或无响应和稳定的尖峰波形；该框架涵盖已知的生理变异性，并在代谢/氧化还原状态与电生理行为之间建立了直接联系。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了化学基础的、非循环的离子中心模型替代方案，为跨生物系统的神经元动力学提供了可检验的预测。

Original Abstract: Trans-membrane gradients and fluxes of cations (H+, Na+, K+, etc.) were deemed to be the rationale of electrical activities of aerobic cells/organelles, as per classical perceptions. Murburn concept (an umbrella of theorization based in stochastic redox processes) has afforded novel models for various metabolic, bioenergetic and electrophysiological outcomes. Herein, the foundational mechanistic formalisms for the electrical activities of neurons that lead signal relay along the axonal length are provided. Electron Holding potential (EHP), a dimensionless field/state variable (related logarithmically to electron chemical potential) is used to explain neuronal activity. By combining local redox relaxation dynamics with spatial transport driven by thermodynamic gradients, we derive a unified reaction-transport-relaxation equation that captures resting potential, excitability, waveform generation, and signal propagation within a single framework. Nonlinear local redox kinetics naturally give rise to threshold behavior, all-or-none responses, and stable spike waveforms. The framework accommodates known physiological variability and provides a direct bridge between metabolic/redox state and electrophysiological behavior. This work establishes a chemically grounded, non-circular alternative to ion-centric models and offers testable predictions for neuronal dynamics across biological systems. In the second part of this work, we compare the new theory with existing systems, provide further evidence, simulations and describe elaborate agendas for falsification and validation.

中文摘要翻译: 根据经典观点，阳离子（H⁺、Na⁺、K⁺等）的跨膜梯度和通量被认为是有氧细胞/细胞器电活动的理论基础。Murburn概念（一种基于随机氧化还原过程的理论化框架）为各种代谢、生物能量学和电生理学结果提供了新颖的模型。本文提供了沿轴突长度传递信号的神经元电活动的基础机制形式化描述。电子持有电位（EHP）——一个无量纲的场/状态变量（与电子化学电位呈对数关系）——被用于解释神经元活动。通过将局部氧化还原弛豫动力学与热力学梯度驱动的空间传输相结合，我们推导出一个统一的反应-传输-弛豫方程，该方程在单一框架内捕获了静息电位、兴奋性、波形生成和信号传播。非线性局部氧化还原动力学自然产生阈值行为、全或无响应和稳定的尖峰波形。该框架兼容已知的生理变异性，并在代谢/氧化还原状态与电生理行为之间建立了直接桥梁。本工作建立了一种化学基础的、非循环的离子中心模型替代方案，并为跨生物系统的神经元动力学提供了可检验的预测。在本工作的第二部分，我们将新理论与现有系统进行比较，提供进一步的证据和模拟，并描述详尽的证伪与验证议程。

</details>


### [113] [One-shot emergency psychiatric triage across 15 frontier AI chatbots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25415)
*Veith Weilnhammer,Lennart Luettgau,Christopher Summerfield,Viknesh Sounderajah,Elise Wilkinson,Virginia Corno,Matthew M Nour*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文评估了15个前沿AI聊天机器人在精神科分诊中的表现。基于112个临床案例和4级分诊标签，发现AI对紧急情况的漏诊率仅5.6%，但整体准确率在42.0%-71.8%之间，且存在明显的过度分诊倾向，尤其在低风险和中风险案例上。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: AI聊天机器人越来越多地被用于健康咨询，但它们在精神科分诊中的表现尚未被充分研究。精神科分诊的挑战在于紧急程度往往需要从思想、行为和背景中推断，而非客观检测结果。

Method: 使用112个临床案例（覆盖9种精神科表现类型和9个风险维度，组成28个表现-风险组，每组4个不同分诊级别的案例），每个案例转化为真实人类撰写的对话查询，让15个AI聊天机器人分配分诊标签（A-常规、B-一周内评估、C-24-48小时内评估、D-紧急护理）。结果与50名医生给出的临床共识标签进行对比验证。

Result: 紧急情况漏诊（D级被降级）发生率为5.6%（23/410），且所有漏诊都被降至C级。AI模型平均准确率在42.0%-71.8%之间。D级案例准确率最高（94.3%），B级最低（19.7%）。平均有符号序数误差为+0.47个分诊级别，表明净过度分诊。中等分诊级别的分散度最高。

Conclusion: 当用户消息包含足够临床信息时，前沿AI聊天机器人识别精神科紧急情况的错误率接近零，但对低风险和中风险案例表现出明显的过度分诊倾向。

Original Abstract: AI chatbots are increasingly used for health advice, but their performance in psychiatric triage remains undercharacterized. Psychiatric triage is particularly challenging because urgency must often be inferred from thoughts, behavior, and context rather than from objective findings.
  We evaluated the performance of 15 frontier AI chatbots on psychiatric triage from realistic single-message disclosures using 112 clinical vignettes, each paired with 1 of 4 original benchmark triage labels: A, routine; B, assessment within 1 week; C, assessment within 24 to 48 hours; and D, emergency care now. Vignettes covered 9 psychiatric presentation clusters and 9 focal risk dimensions, organized into 28 presentation-by-risk groups. Each group contributed 4 distinct vignettes, with 1 vignette at each triage level. Each vignette was rendered as a realistic human-authored conversational query, and the AI chatbots were tasked with assigning a triage label from that disclosure.
  Emergency under-triage occurred in 23 of 410 level D trials (5.6%), and all under-triaged emergencies were reassigned to level C urgency. Across target models, average accuracy ranged from 42.0% to 71.8%. Accuracy was highest for level D vignettes (94.3%) and lowest for level B vignettes (19.7%). Mean signed ordinal error was positive (+0.47 triage levels), indicating net over-triage. Dispersion was highest around the middle triage levels. All results were confirmed relative to clinician consensus labels from 50 medical doctors.
  When presented with user messages containing sufficient clinical information, frontier AI chatbots thus recognized psychiatric emergencies as requiring urgent medical assessment with near-zero error rates, yet showed marked over-triage for low and intermediate risk presentations.

中文摘要翻译: AI聊天机器人越来越多地被用于健康咨询，但它们在精神科分诊中的表现仍然未被充分研究。精神科分诊尤其具有挑战性，因为紧急程度往往需要从思想、行为和背景中推断，而非依据客观检测结果。我们使用112个临床案例对15个前沿AI聊天机器人在基于真实单条消息披露的精神科分诊任务上进行了评估，每个案例配有一个原始基准分诊标签：A（常规）、B（一周内评估）、C（24至48小时内评估）和D（立即紧急护理）。案例涵盖9种精神科表现类型和9个焦点风险维度，组织成28个表现-风险组。每组包含4个不同的案例，每个分诊级别各1个。每个案例被呈现为真实人类撰写的对话查询，AI聊天机器人需据此分配分诊标签。在410个D级试验中，紧急情况漏诊发生了23例（5.6%），所有被漏诊的紧急案例均被重新分配为C级。各目标模型平均准确率在42.0%至71.8%之间。D级案例准确率最高（94.3%），B级最低（19.7%）。平均有符号序数误差为正值（+0.47个分诊级别），表明净过度分诊。中等分诊级别的分散度最高。所有结果均通过与50名医生给出的临床共识标签进行验证。因此，当用户消息包含足够的临床信息时，前沿AI聊天机器人能够以接近零的错误率识别需要紧急医疗评估的精神科紧急情况，但对低风险和中等风险案例表现出明显的过度分诊倾向。

</details>
